# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Low-Magnification SEM May Suffice: Interpretable Deep Learning for Multi-Scale Fracture-Cause Classification in Zirconia-Toughened Alumina](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29798)
*Julian Schmid,Pawel Astankow,Tom Vater,Julius Beck,Robert Cichon,Danny Krautz*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可解释的视觉Transformer（ViT）工作流，用于对氧化铝基复合材料（BIOLOX delta）人工关节植入物的断裂原因进行自动分类。基于8,493张SEM图像数据集的五折交叉验证显示，该模型在严重类别不平衡条件下达到0.907的准确率和0.888的宏F1分数；低放大倍率（50x）下的性能与高放大倍率相当，且Grad-CAM归因定位与传统断口学特征一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氧化铝基复合材料髋/膝关节植入物中断裂起源（fracture origin）的可靠识别对质量保证和患者安全至关重要。当前断口学工作流程耗时、部分主观，且依赖高放大倍率扫描电子显微镜（scanning electron microscopy, SEM），亟需一种更高效、客观的自动化分类方法。

Method: 构建了一个包含8,493张50x至10,000x放大倍率SEM图像的数据集，按制造链三个环节划分为生坯缺陷、硬加工缺陷和材料缺陷三类。采用可解释视觉Transformer（vision transformer, ViT）进行微调后分类；通过两阶段感知哈希（perceptual-hash）与结构相似性指数（SSIM）泄漏审计确认样本无重叠；使用Grad-CAM进行归因定位。

Result: 在分层五折交叉验证下，微调ViT达到0.907准确率和0.888宏F1分数。低放大倍率（50x）与高放大倍率（1k-10kx）性能相当；Grad-CAM归因一致地定位在镜面、劈裂线、气孔、加工痕等典型断口学特征上。

Conclusion: 可解释ViT可作为陶瓷植入物质量保证的互补工具，支持低放大倍率预筛，减少对耗时的高放大倍率检查的依赖。

Abstract: Reliable identification of fracture origins in alumina matrix composite hip and knee implants is critical for quality assurance and patient safety, yet current fractographic workflows are time-consuming, partly subjective, and reliant on high-magnification scanning electron microscopy (SEM). We present an interpretable vision-transformer (ViT) workflow for automated classification of fracture causes in an alumina matrix composite (BIOLOX delta, CeramTec GmbH) widely used in total joint replacements. A dataset of 8,493 SEM images (50x-10,000x) was curated from five years of in-production burst and proof tests and annotated into three defect categories defined along the manufacturing chain: green body, hard machining, and material defects. Under severe class imbalance, the fine-tuned ViT reached an accuracy of 0.907 and a macro-F1 of 0.888 in stratified five-fold cross-validation, with a two-stage perceptual-hash/SSIM leakage audit confirming negligible specimen overlap. Notably, performance at low magnification (50x) was comparable to that at high magnification (1k-10kx), indicating that macro-scale features - mirror geometry and hackle line fields - already encode sufficient diagnostic signal. Grad-CAM attributions consistently localised on canonical fractographic cues (mirrors, hackles, pores, machining marks), aligning with established fractographic criteria. Together, these results position interpretable ViTs as a complementary tool for ceramic-implant quality assurance, enabling low-magnification pre-screening and reducing reliance on time-intensive high-magnification inspection.

</details>

# astro-ph.GA [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Equilibrium Core and Vortex Solutions of Bose Einstein Condensate Dark Matter around a Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29069)
*Ivan Alvarez-Rios,Francisco S. Guzman*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过虚时方法构造了黑洞引力源周围玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚暗物质（BECDM）的稳态轴对称解，包括基态核心解和首位非零涡旋解，并分析了自相互作用和黑洞质量对密度分布及稳定性的影响，发现稳定涡旋解在黑洞存在时也可存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究黑洞周围BECDM稳态解的构造及其稳定性，特别是涡旋解是否能在黑洞引力场中稳定存在，以评估这类构型的天体物理相关性。

Method: 针对一般轴对称构型，采用虚时方法（imaginary-time approach）求解稳态方程，构造了基态核心解和首位非零涡数（winding number）的线涡旋（line vortex）解；通过基于焓泛函（enthalpy functional）的转向点判据（turning point criterion）评估解的稳定性。

Result: 自相互作用为负（$g<0$）时，构型存在最大质量，据此可推断该参数范围内解可能出现的区间；验证了在非相互作用情况（$g=0$）下球对称核心解作为坍缩吸引子的性质。稳定涡旋解在黑洞存在时也可形成，其稳定性特征表明这些构型可能与物理相关的形成场景兼容。

Conclusion: 黑洞周围的BECDM不仅存在稳定的基态核心解，还存在稳定的涡旋解，后者在合适的参数范围内具有天体物理形成机制的潜在可行性。

Abstract: We present the construction of stationary solutions of Bose-Einstein condensate dark matter (BECDM) around a point-like gravitational source representing a black hole. The problem is formulated for general axisymmetric configurations, and we focus on two cases: the ground-state core solution and the first nonzero winding number configuration corresponding to a line vortex solution. The stationary equations are solved using an imaginary-time approach, which enables the construction of families of solutions across a wide range of self-interaction and black hole masses. We analyze the impact of these parameters on the density distribution and on the stability properties of the solutions, assessing stability through the turning point criterion based on the enthalpy functional, which allows us to identify stable and unstable branches along each family of solutions. It has been shown in the past that spherical core solutions act as attractors in the collapse of BECDM around black holes in the non-interacting case ($g=0$), supporting their astrophysical relevance. In the present work, the existence of a maximum mass for configurations with attractive self-interaction ($g<0$) allows us to infer the parameter range in which such solutions may also arise in this regime. Building on this picture, we show that stable vortex solutions of BECDM can also exist in the presence of a black hole, whose stability properties suggest that these configurations may likewise be compatible with physically relevant formation scenarios.

</details>

### [3] [Multifractal Complexity of the Chandler Wobble and Its Anomalous Disappearance (2015--2020): A MFDFA Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29056)
*Sebastián Jaroszewicz,Nahuel Mendez,Maria P. Beccar-Varela,Maria Cristina Mariani*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文利用超过60年（1962-2024）的极移数据，通过多重分形去趋势波动分析（MFDFA）首次系统刻画了钱德勒摆动（CW）的多重分形特征，揭示了2015-2020年间CW振幅近乎消失及其后相位反转这一异常的动力学机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钱德勒摆动（Chandler wobble, CW）——地球自转极约433天的自由章动——在2015至2020年间出现了异常的近乎消失，随后伴随约180°相位反转重新激发。这一异常现象的动力学本质尚不清楚，亟需定量刻画与机理分析。

Method: 采用多重分形去趋势波动分析（Multifractal Detrended Fluctuation Analysis, MFDFA），分析了1962至2024年超过六十年逐日的IERS EOP C04极移数据，并结合滑动窗口分析及替代数据检验（shuffled与相位随机化ensemble）以验证多重分形来源。

Result: 全局MFDFA表明残余极移分量和CW振幅是真正的多重分形过程，具有强q依赖的广义赫斯特指数（generalised Hurst exponents）和宽奇异谱。替代数据检验证实，该多重分形性源于长程时间相关性（long-range temporal correlations）与重尾激发统计（heavy-tailed excitation statistics）的联合作用。滑动窗口分析揭示，在2015-2020振幅极小期之前及期间，几何极移信号的长程持久性和多重分形谱宽度发生显著坍缩，表明存在真实的动力学状态转变。相比之下，振幅和相位相关变量在所有时期均保持宽多重分形谱和稳定标度指数，显示出CW几何结构与振幅/相位涨落的多尺度结构之间存在动力学解耦。

Conclusion: CW振幅是地球物理激发（geophysical excitation）的异常敏感的多重分形积分器，多重分形指标可能为地球自转动力学中的重大转变提供早期预警信号。

Abstract: The Chandler wobble (CW) -- the $\sim$433-day free nutation of Earth's rotation pole -- experienced an anomalous near-disappearance between 2015 and 2020, followed by a re-excitation with an approximately $180^{\circ}$ phase reversal. Using Multifractal Detrended Fluctuation Analysis (MFDFA) applied to more than six decades (1962--2024) of daily IERS EOP C04 polar motion data, this study provides the first multifractal characterisation of the CW and its recent anomaly. Global MFDFA shows that the residual polar motion components and the CW amplitude are genuine multifractal processes with strongly $q$-dependent generalised Hurst exponents and broad singularity spectra. Surrogate-data tests with shuffled and phase-randomised ensembles demonstrate that this multifractality originates from the combined action of long-range temporal correlations and heavy-tailed excitation statistics. A sliding-window analysis reveals a pronounced collapse in long-range persistence and multifractal spectral width of the geometric polar motion signal several years before and during the 2015--2020 amplitude minimum, indicating a genuine dynamical regime change rather than a simple suppression of oscillation amplitude. In contrast, the amplitude- and phase-related variables retain broad multifractal spectra and stable scaling exponents across all epochs, revealing a dynamical decoupling between the geometry of the CW and the multiscale structure of its amplitude and phase fluctuations. These findings highlight the CW amplitude as an exceptionally multifractal integrator of geophysical excitation and suggest that multifractal metrics may provide early-warning indicators of major transitions in Earth rotation dynamics.

</details>


### [4] [Partial Entropy production of active particles with hidden states in potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29201)
*Jacob Knight,Gunnar Pruessner*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文扩展了微扰框架（perturbative framework），用于计算一般束缚势（confining potential）中活性粒子（active particle）的局部熵产生（partial entropy production），从而量化带有隐蔽自驱动（hidden self-propulsion）的随机系统的时间反演不对称性（time-reversal asymmetry）。在简谐势（harmonic case）下，该框架成功复现了活性 Ornstein-Uhlenbeck 粒子的局部熵产生率精确解，并推导了游走-翻滚粒子（run-and-tumble particle）的相应结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 部分可观测的随机系统可能表现出（近乎）时间反演对称（time-reversal symmetric）的假象，而实际上系统可能处于远离平衡态（far from equilibrium）的运行状态。因此，需要一种量化方法来揭示此类系统中被隐藏的非平衡特征。

Method: 本文基于文献 [Phys. Rev. Lett. 136, 198302 (2026)] 中提出的微扰框架（perturbative framework）进行扩展，将其应用于一般束缚势（generic confining potential）中的活性粒子系统，计算局部熵产生（partial entropy production）。

Result: 针对简谐势（harmonic case）这一特例，该框架成功复现了活性 Ornstein-Uhlenbeck 粒子（active Ornstein-Uhlenbeck particle）的局部熵产生率（partial entropy production rate）精确解，并进一步推导出游走-翻滚粒子（run-and-tumble particle）的局部熵产生率。

Conclusion: 所扩展的微扰框架能够有效量化一般束缚势中活性粒子的隐蔽非平衡性，为分析更广泛的部分可观测随机系统的时间反演不对称性提供了可行途径。

Abstract: Partially observed stochastic systems can appear (almost) time-reversal symmetric while in fact operating far from equilibrium. The present work extends the perturbative framework introduced in [Phys. Rev. Lett. 136, 198302 (2026)] to calculate in a generic confining potential the partial entropy production, which quantifies the time-reversal asymmetry of a generic active particle with hidden self-propulsion. Focusing on the harmonic case, we apply our framework to reproduce an exact result for the partial entropy production rate of an active Ornstein-Uhlenbeck particle and to derive the partial entropy production rate of a run-and-tumble particle.

</details>


### [5] [Criticality in the disordered $N$-color Ashkin-Teller model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29810)
*Youssef Makoudi,Gesualdo Delfino*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文利用标度不变散射理论（scale invariant scattering theory）求解了二维N色Ashkin-Teller模型在淬火无序（quenched disorder）下的精确重整化群（renormalization group）不动点方程。研究发现，弱无序区域存在一条具有伊辛（Ising）热指数和连续变化磁指数的不动点线；强无序区域则展现出更多的不动点解，并出现不依赖于对称性参数N的超普适性（superuniversality）临界指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在揭示二维N色Ashkin-Teller模型在淬火无序（quenched disorder）影响下的临界行为，特别是通过求解精确重整化群（renormalization group）不动点方程，探索无序系统中可能出现的普适类（universality class）及其对称性特性。

Method: 采用标度不变散射理论（scale invariant scattering theory）作为核心方法，求解二维情形下存在淬火无序（quenched disorder）时Ashkin-Teller模型的精确重整化群（renormalization group）不动点方程。

Result: 弱无序（weak disorder）区域存在一条对于任何N>1均成立的不动点线（line of fixed points），其热指数为伊辛（Ising）型，磁指数（magnetic exponents）则连续变化。强无序（strong disorder）区域允许更多的不动点解，且出现了独立于对称性参数N的临界指数，体现了超普适性（superuniversality）。

Conclusion: 无序的强度显著影响Ashkin-Teller模型的固定点结构，强无序区域的不动点解数量增加反映了随机耦合分布（distributions of the two random couplings）依赖性的增强。超普适性（superuniversality）作为随机临界性（random criticality）的独特特征得到进一步确认。

Abstract: The $N$-color Ashkin-Teller model corresponds to $N$ Ising models coupled by four-spin interactions. We consider the two-dimensional case in presence of quenched disorder and use scale invariant scattering theory to determine all the solutions of the exact renormalization group fixed points equations. The weak disorder sector is characterized by a solution that, for any fixed $N$ larger than 1, is a line of fixed points with Ising thermal exponents and continuously varying magnetic exponents. The number of fixed point solutions allowed by the symmetries of the model increases at strong disorder illustrating the growing dependence on the distributions of the two random couplings. The presence of some critical exponents which do not depend on the symmetry parameter $N$ confirms this type of superuniversality as a peculiar feature of random criticality.

</details>


### [6] [Hidden Ising models from the generalized Yang-Baxter equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30007)
*Akash Sinha,Somnath Maity,Pramod Padmanabhan,Vladimir Korepin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种具有多体相互作用但仍保持局域性的一维自旋1/2哈密顿量模型，其哈密顿量密度的代数结构与横向场伊辛模型类似。通过这一性质，证明了该模型谱为自由费米子型但每个能级具有巨大简并度。简并来源是一组局域守恒量，它们像经典背景场一样作用于量子系统。在能谱无隙点，该系统可通过推广的杨-巴克斯特方程和量子反散射方法导出，其R-矩阵由超特殊2-群的生成元构造，有助于提取所有守恒荷，并建立一种通用机制来生成“伪装的”横向场伊辛模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索具有多体位点相互作用但仍保持局域性的一维自旋系统的可解结构，揭示其与横向场伊辛模型之间的代数联系，并建立生成此类多体相互作用自旋系统的通用机制。

Method: 利用哈密顿量密度与横向场伊辛模型相似的代数性质证明谱的自由费米子性质；在无隙点采用推广的杨-巴克斯特方程（multi-site generalization of the Yang-Baxter equation）和量子反散射方法（quantum inverse scattering method）；R-矩阵由超特殊2-群（extraspecial 2-groups）的生成元构造。

Result: 该模型的能谱为自由费米子型，但每个能级具有巨大简并度；局域守恒量是简并的来源，它们充当量子系统的经典背景场；该模型的热力学与标准伊辛模型形成对比；在无隙点可通过推广的杨-巴克斯特方程和量子反散射方法导出。

Conclusion: 该工作为生成“伪装成横向场伊辛模型”的多体相互作用自旋系统提供了通用框架，并包含了如何在该形式中获取Fendley的伪自由费米子模型（free-fermion in disguise models）的说明。

Abstract: We introduce a one dimensional spin $\frac{1}{2}$ Hamiltonian with multi-site interactions, but still local. The algebra of its Hamiltonian densities resembles that of the transverse field Ising model. Using this fact we show that its spectrum is free-fermionic but with a huge degeneracy for each level. The source of the degeneracy is a set of local conserved quantities that act like a classical background field for the quantum system. The thermodynamics of this system is contrasted with the standard Ising model. At the gapless points in the energy spectrum, we show that this system can be derived from the quantum inverse scattering method adapted to a multi-site generalization of the Yang-Baxter equation as introduced by E. Rowell and Z. Wang. The $R$-matrix is constructed using generators of extraspecial 2-groups. This helps us extract all the conserved charges and lay the framework for a general mechanism to generate such multi-site interaction spin systems that are transverse field Ising models under the hood. A remark on how to obtain P. Fendley's free-fermion in disguise models in this formalism is also included.

</details>


### [7] [Charged Abelian Higgs phase transitions in three-dimensional compact lattice U(1) gauge models with multicharge scalar matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29884)
*Claudio Bonati,Filippo Mariani,Ettore Vicari*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 通过三维双电荷阿贝尔希格斯模型（Abelian Higgs models）的蒙特卡罗模拟与有限尺寸标度分析，估计出该模型从无序-禁闭相到有序-解禁闭相连续相变所需的最小标量分量数为 $N_{\rm cL}=9(1)$，从而逼近三维阿贝尔希格斯场论中稳定带电不动点（charged fixed point, CFP）存在的临界分量数 $N_3^*$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维阿贝尔希格斯场论（scalar electrodynamics）中的稳定带电不动点（CFP）仅当标量场分量数 $N \ge N_d^*$ 时存在。已知四维下 $N_4^*=183$，但三维下的 $N_3^*$ 尚未确定。本文旨在通过格点模型数值模拟来估计这一临界值。

Method: 采用三维双电荷紧致 U(1) 格点阿贝尔希格斯模型（CLAH），对 $N\in[4,10]$ 的分量数进行蒙特卡罗模拟，并对晶格尺寸 $L\approx 100$ 的结果进行有限尺寸标度分析（finite-size scaling analysis），以判断沿无序-禁闭（DC）与有序-解禁闭（OD）相变线的相变连续性。

Result: 模拟结果表明：$N=10$ 时存在连续的 DC-OD 相变；$N\le 7$ 时表现为弱一阶相变；$N=8,\,9$ 的结果不具有决定性。据此估计 $N_{\rm cL}=9(1)$，即连续相变所需的最小分量数约为 9，误差为 1。

Conclusion: 本文通过格点蒙特卡罗模拟将三维双电荷 CLAH 模型连续相变所需的最小标量分量数确定为 $N_{\rm cL}=9(1)$，该数值为三维阿贝尔希格斯场论中 CFP 存在的临界分量数 $N_3^*$ 提供了近似估计。

Abstract: We consider three-dimensional (3D) lattice Abelian Higgs models, with compact U(1) gauge variables coupled to a doubly-charged $N$-component complex scalar field (CLAH). We focus on their phase transitions between the disordered-confined (DC) and ordered-deconfined (OD) phases. When they are continuous they belong to the 3D Abelian Higgs (AH) universality class associated with the stable charged fixed point (CFP) of the renormalization-group flow of the 3D AH field theory, or scalar electrodynamics, describing $N$-component complex scalar fields minimally coupled to a U(1) gauge field. This CFP exists only for a sufficiently large number of components, i.e., $N \ge N_d^*$, where the integer $N_d^*$ depends on the spatial dimension $d$ (for example $N_4^*=183$). To estimate $N_3^*$, we look for the minimum number $N_{\rm cL}$ of scalar components of 3D doubly-charged CLAH models developing continuous transitions along their DC-OD transition line. For this purpose, we present finite-size scaling analyses of Monte Carlo simulations for $N\in[4,10]$, up to lattice sizes $L\approx 100$. The results provide evidence of continuous DC-OD transitions for $N=10$, and weak first-order transitions for $N\le 7$. They are not conclusive for $N=8,\,9$. Therefore, we estimate $N_{\rm cL}=9(1)$.

</details>


### [8] [Universal thermokinetic decomposition of short-time information fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29957)
*Giorgio Nicoletti,Daniel M. Busiello*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对任意朗之万动力学（Langevin dynamics）的随机可预测性（stochastic predictability）建立了一种通用的热力学-动力学分解（thermokinetic decomposition），揭示了在短时间尺度下，信息涨落（information fluctuations）被能量耗散（energy dissipation）抑制，并被动力学活性（dynamical activity）放大；平均可预测性（average predictability）则与热力学和动力学特征无关，表明耗散的作用是降低涨落而非增强信息本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管信息论工具已被广泛用于刻画信息处理能力，但系统沿单个轨迹获取信息的可靠性程度以及哪些方面需要付出热力学代价（thermodynamic cost）仍是未解问题。

Method: 将可预测性定义为当前状态与未来状态之间的点互信息（pointwise mutual information），并基于任意朗之万动力学（Langevin dynamics）在短时间尺度下推导其涨落的通用热力学-动力学分解（thermokinetic decomposition）。

Result: 发现信息涨落被能量耗散抑制、被动力学活性放大；平均可预测性与热力学和动力学特征无关；耗散仅在非线性操作下才有效发挥作用；在随机振荡器（stochastic oscillators）中，能量消耗通过结构上不同且可独立调节的机制控制短时间和长时间精度。

Conclusion: 该分解为理解非平衡系统中信息传输的可靠性、生物系统的精度约束以及能量受限控制策略的设计提供了基础性热力学依据。

Abstract: Biological, artificial, and physical systems dissipate energy to accurately transmit information. While tools of information theory have been used to characterize information-processing capabilities, how reliably this information is acquired along individual trajectories, and which aspects require a thermodynamic cost, is an open question. In this work, we focus on the stochastic predictability of an arbitrary Langevin dynamics, defined as the pointwise mutual information between the current and future states of a system. We show that the fluctuations of predictability obey a universal thermokinetic decomposition at short times, which reveals that information fluctuations are suppressed by energy dissipation and become stronger with increased dynamical activity. Remarkably, we find that the average predictability, i.e., the short-time mutual information, does not carry any dependence on the underlying thermodynamic and kinetic features. Thus, the role of dissipation at short times is not to enhance information, but to reduce its fluctuations. Such dissipative control is effective only when instantiated by nonlinear operations. Moreover, energy consumption governs short- and long-time precision in stochastic oscillators through structurally different mechanisms that can be independently tuned. Our decomposition offers a fundamental thermodynamic basis for understanding the reliability of information transmission in nonequilibrium systems, the constraints on precision in biological systems, and the design of energy-limited control strategies.

</details>


### [9] [Quantum Spin-5/2 Blume-Capel Model in a Random Transverse-Crystalline Field Anisotropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30125)
*Claudio M. Salgado,Karollaine C. Leite,Thiago M. Tunes,Marcelo F. Z. de Arruda,Jorge L. B. de Faria,Alberto S. de Arruda*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文采用平均场方法（mean-field approach）和Bogoliubov不等式，研究了存在横向和随机晶场的自旋 S = 5/2 量子Blume-Capel模型的热力学性质，分析了纵向和横向各向异性对磁有序和相变的影响。结果显示，大多数参数范围内系统呈现标准二级相变（second-order phase transition），但某些正各向异性值下会出现有序相内部的弱一级相变（first-order phase transition）；负横向各向异性（transverse anisotropy）提高临界温度（critical temperature），正横向各向异性则降低临界温度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究横向和随机晶场对高自旋（S=5/2）量子Blume-Capel模型热力学性质的影响，揭示纵向和横向各向异性参数在磁有序（magnetic ordering）和相变行为中的作用机制。

Method: 采用基于Bogoliubov不等式的平均场方法推导吉布斯自由能（Gibbs free energy）的基本热力学势和磁化强度状态方程（equation of state for the magnetization）。

Result: 大多数参数范围内系统呈现标准二级相变，未发现三临界点（tricritical behavior）；特定正各向异性值下出现有序相内部的一级相变，表现为从高自旋有序态跳跃至低自旋有序态。负横向各向异性提高临界温度，正横向各向异性降低临界温度。

Conclusion: 该研究系统给出了S=5/2量子Blume-Capel模型的相图（phase diagram），强调了横向各向异性在调控临界行为中的关键作用，为理解高自旋系统的量子相变提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the thermodynamic properties of the quantum Blume-Capel model with spin \( S = 5/2 \) in the presence of transverse and random crystalline fields. The system is described by a Hamiltonian that includes ferromagnetic exchange interactions between nearest neighbors, a longitudinal single-ion anisotropy, and a transverse single-ion anisotropy. Using a mean-field approach based on Bogoliubov's inequality for the Gibbs free energy, we derive the fundamental thermodynamic potential and the equation of state for the magnetization. The influence of the longitudinal and transverse anisotropy parameters on the magnetic ordering and phase transitions is analyzed in detail. We present magnetization versus temperature diagrams for various combinations of the anisotropies, exploring both positive and negative values. Our results reveal that the system exhibits standard second-order phase transitions for most parameter ranges, with no evidence of tricritical behavior. However, for certain positive values of the anisotropies, the model displays a first-order phase transition within the ordered phase, characterized by a jump from a higher-spin ordered state to a lower-spin ordered state. The critical temperatures are shown to be sensitive to the magnitude and sign of the anisotropy parameters. In particular, negative transverse anisotropies favor magnetic order, raising the critical temperature, while positive anisotropies promote disorder, lowering the critical temperature. This study provides a comprehensive analysis of the phase diagram of the \( S = 5/2 \) quantum Blume-Capel model and highlights the role of transverse fields in modifying the critical behavior.

</details>

### [10] [Higher Mellin Moments of the Unpolarized PDF of the Pion and the Kaon from Lattice QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29998)
*Constantia Alexandrou,Simone Bacchio,Priyajit Jana,Marcus Petschlies,Luis Alberto Rodriguez Chacon,Gregoris Spanoudes,Fernanda Steffens,Carsten Urbach,Urs Wenger*

TL;DR: 本文基于一组 $N_f=2+1+1$ 味扭曲质量费米子（twisted mass fermions）规范系综，计算了未极化部分子分布函数（parton distribution function, PDF）的梅林矩（Mellin moments）最高至四阶，并通过连通贡献（connected contributions）重构了价夸克（valence）π介子和Kaon的PDF，最后将结果与格点QCD及其他唯象学（phenomenological）结果进行了比较。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确描述π介子和Kaon的内部结构是理解强相互作用（strong interaction）的重要环节，而PDF是刻画强子内部部分子动量分布的核心可观测量（observable）。利用格点QCD（lattice QCD）直接计算PDF的梅林矩，可从第一性原理出发为唯象模型提供非微扰（non-perturbative）输入，但现有计算结果仍存在不确定性，需要更精确的格点计算进行检验和补充。

Method: 研究采用一套 $N_f=2+1+1$ 味扭曲质量费米子规范系综，夸克质量调至接近物理值（physical values）。通过计算连通贡献部分得到了三个梅林矩，并在此基础上重构了价夸克的π介子和Kaon PDF。

Result: 获得了π介子和Kaon未极化PDF的前四阶梅林矩，并重构了相应的价夸克PDF。将得到的梅林矩和重构PDF与其他格点QCD及唯象学确定的结果进行了对比。

Conclusion: 本文的计算结果与已有的格点QCD和唯象学结果总体上具有可比性，为π介子和Kaon的PDF提供了来自第一性原理格点QCD的新检验数据。研究同时表明，基于物理点附近质量参数和连通贡献的梅林矩方法可用于有效重构轻介子（light meson）的价夸克PDF。

Abstract: We present results on the Mellin moments of the unpolarized parton distribution function (PDF) of the pion and kaon up to the fourth order. The computation is done using one $N_f=2+1+1$ gauge ensemble of twisted mass fermions with quark masses tuned to approximately their physical values. We reconstruct the valence pion and kaon PDFs using the connected contributions to the three Mellin moments. We compare our results on the Mellin moments and the reconstructed PDFs with other lattice QCD and phenomenological determinations.

### [11] [Mellin Moments of the Unpolarized Gluon PDF in the Proton from Nonlocal Operators in Lattice QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30193)
*Joseph Delmar,Krzysztof Cichy,Martha Constantinou,Yong Zhao*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文利用格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD）计算了质子中非极化胶子部分子分布函数（PDF）的Mellin矩，基于短距离算子乘积展开（OPE）从约化胶子Ioffe时间分布中提取了高阶胶子矩与胶子动量分数的比值，并系统评估了OPE矩阶数截断、Wilson线分离范围、夸克单态混合以及DGLAP标度演化等系统性效应，最终在2 GeV标度下给出了比值⟨x³⟩_g/⟨x⟩_g的测定结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质子内部结构中的胶子部分子分布函数（gluon parton distribution function, gluon PDF）对于理解强相互作用及质子自旋与动量构成至关重要，而胶子矩的高阶矩（Mellin moments）直接关联胶子在质子中的动量分布细节。现有格点QCD计算主要集中于胶子动量分数⟨x⟩_g，对高阶胶子矩的系统性提取尚不充分，且需要处理算子乘积展开截断、夸克-胶子混合等理论不确定性，因此亟需一个更完整的格点计算来提供可靠的高阶矩比值。

Method: 使用N_f=2+1+1最大扭曲质量费米子（maximally twisted mass fermions）配合clover改进以及Iwasaki改进规范作用的格点系综，在π介子质量约260 MeV下计算耦合到动量增强质子态的非定域胶子算符的矩阵元。基于约化胶子Ioffe时间分布（reduced gluon Ioffe-time distribution），利用短距离算子乘积展开（OPE）提取高阶胶子矩⟨x^n⟩（n>1）与胶子动量分数⟨x⟩的比值。系统研究了OPE中矩阶数截断、Wilson线最小/最大分离范围的选择、以及微扰匹配中夸克单态（quark-singlet）混合处理的影响，并通过DGLAP方程进行标度演化，通过改变标度评估微扰截断带来的不确定性。

Result: 在2 GeV标度下给出了比值⟨x³⟩_g/⟨x⟩_g的确定结果，其不确定性同时包含了统计误差和主要的理论系统误差。

Conclusion: 论文表明，结合格点QCD和短距离OPE方法可以系统性地提取胶子高阶矩与动量分数的比值，并通过多种系统性检验（包括OPE截断、Wilson线范围、夸克混合、DGLAP演化与标度变化）确保了结果的稳定性，提供了目前格点计算中较为完整的胶子矩比值测定。

Abstract: We present a lattice QCD determination of the Mellin moments of the unpolarized gluon parton distribution function in the proton. The analysis is based on matrix elements of nonlocal gluon operators coupled to momentum-boosted proton states. The calculation relies on an $N_f=2+1+1$ ensemble of maximally twisted mass fermions with clover improvement and the Iwasaki-improved gauge action, at a pion mass of approximately 260 MeV. Working within the short-distance operator product expansion (OPE) of the reduced gluon Ioffe-time distribution, we extract ratios of higher-order gluon moments, $\langle x^n\rangle$ with $n>1$, to the gluon momentum fraction, $\langle x\rangle$. We investigate systematic effects associated with the truncation of the order of moment in the OPE, the choice of minimum and maximum Wilson-line separations entering the analysis, and the treatment of mixing with the quark-singlet under perturbative matching. The stability of the extracted moments is further studied under scale evolution using DGLAP equations, allowing us to assess uncertainties related to perturbative truncation by varying the scale. Our work provides a determination of the ratio $\langle x^3\rangle_g/\langle x\rangle_g$ at a scale of 2 GeV, with uncertainties that account for both statistical and the dominant theoretical systematic uncertainties.

</details>

### [12] [Impact of the equation of state on core collapse supernovae I: the low-$T/|W|$ instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28944)
*Marco Cusinato,Martin Obergaulinger,Miguel Ángel Aloy*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过三维中微子磁流体动力学模拟，研究快速旋转的大质量前身星（35 M☉）坍缩过程中，五种有限温度核物质状态方程如何影响低T/|W|不稳定性及其多信使信号特征。结果表明该不稳定性在所有模型中均出现，但引力波频率与前身中子星的致密性和刚度相关，可为探测致密物质状态方程提供诊断工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 快速旋转的核坍缩超新星（core-collapse supernovae）是多信使发射（multimessenger emission）的重要来源，但致密物质物理如何影响低T/|W|不稳定性（low-T/|W| instability）及其引力波和中微子信号尚不清楚。

Method: 采用三维中微子磁流体动力学（neutrino-magnetohydrodynamics）数值模拟，对快速旋转的35 M☉前身星坍缩过程进行计算，并引入五种不同的有限温度原子核状态方程（finite-temperature nuclear equations of state）进行对比分析。

Result: 所有状态方程模型均出现了低T/|W|不稳定性，但其起爆时间、主导方位角模结构、寿命和多信使特征频率因模型而异。不稳定性驱动的大尺度螺旋模（spiral modes）产生准周期性引力波发射（quasi-periodic gravitational wave emission），并对中微子光度（neutrino luminosities）产生调制，尤其在赤道面附近方向最为显著。主导引力波频率与前身中子星的有效刚度和致密性（effective stiffness and compactness）正相关。

Conclusion: 在快速旋转核坍缩超新星中，低T/|W|不稳定性驱动的引力波频率可成为致密物质状态方程的诊断手段，与中微子信号提供的信息互补。

Abstract: Rapidly rotating core-collapse supernovae are promising sources of multimessenger emission, as non-axisymmetric dynamics in the newly formed proto-neutron star can leave characteristic imprints on both gravitational waves and neutrinos. We present three-dimensional neutrino-magnetohydrodynamics simulations of the collapse of a rapidly rotating $35\,\mathrm{M}_\odot$ progenitor, performed with five different finite-temperature nuclear equations of state, to investigate how dense-matter physics affects the development of the low-$T/|W|$ instability and its associated multimessenger signatures.
  We find that the low-$T/|W|$ instability develops in all equation of state models considered, indicating that its occurrence is robust for this rapidly rotating progenitor. However, its onset time, dominant azimuthal structure, lifetime, and characteristic multimessenger frequencies vary among models, reflecting differences in the evolving proto-neutron star structure and rotation profile. The instability produces large-scale spiral modes that generate quasi-periodic gravitational wave emission and modulate the neutrino luminosities, especially along directions close to the equatorial plane.
  The dominant gravitational wave frequency associated with the instability correlates with the effective stiffness and compactness of the proto-neutron star: models with more compact/stiffer configurations emit at higher frequencies. This suggests that, in rapidly rotating core-collapse supernovae, the frequency of the low-$T/|W|$ instability-driven gravitational wave signal may provide a diagnostic of the dense-matter equation of state, complementary to the information carried by the neutrino signal.

</details>


### [13] [Assessing the Relative Importance of Neutrino Matter Interaction Channels in Post-Merger Remnant of Binary Neutron Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29187)
*Samantha Rath,Francois Foucart,Lawrence E. Kidder,Harald P. Pfeiffer,Mark A. Scheel*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文利用能量依赖的蒙特卡洛中微子输运模拟，系统评估了双中子星并合后遗体中微子与物质退耦的热力学条件，并比较了平衡假设与非平衡分布下的不透明度，揭示了电子散射对重轻子中微子热化的重要贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双中子星并合（neutron star mergers）是引力波与电磁信号联合探测的重要源，也是r-过程元素生产和超核饱和密度物质状态方程（equation of state）的探针。并合及并合后中微子-物质相互作用强烈影响残余物质的热力学演化、成分、千新星（kilonova）发射和核合成产额，但现有模拟在中微子输运（neutrino transport）和相互作用率的处理上存在显著近似。

Method: 首先在假设中微子与流体处于平衡（equilibria）的条件下，估算并合后残余物中的不透明度（opacities），并与采用灰体两矩格式（gray two-moment scheme）的模拟结果进行对比。随后利用蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟中的实际中微子分布函数重新评估不透明度，重点关注电荷流吸收、核子与核上的准弹性散射、对产生过程以及非弹性中微子-电子散射（inelastic neutrino-electron scattering）对电子中微子、电子反中微子和重轻子中微子的影响。

Result: 平衡假设下的不透明度结果与基于灰体两矩格式的先前研究一致，并明确了核子-核子轫致辐射（nucleon-nucleon Bremmstrahlung）和电子-正电子湮灭（electron-positron annihilation）分别活跃于高密度和低密度区域。利用蒙特卡洛模拟的实际中微子分布函数后，发现冷低密度区域中（尤其对重轻子中微子）的配对湮灭率大幅增加。此外，此前未被纳入并合模拟的非弹性电子散射对重轻子中微子的热化（thermalization）具有重要贡献。

Conclusion: 中微子分布函数的非平衡效应对不透明度和反应率有显著影响，特别是对重轻子中微子；在未来的双中子星并合模拟中需要纳入非弹性电子散射过程，以更准确地描述中微子输运和热化行为。

Abstract: Neutron star mergers are amongst the most promising sources for the joint detection of gravitational waves and electromagnetic signals. They are also potential sites for the production of r-process elements and probes of the equation of state of matter above nuclear saturation density. Neutrino-matter interactions during and after merger strongly influence the thermodynamic evolution and composition of the remnant and its outflows, thereby affecting kilonova emission and nucleosynthesis yields. However, existing merger simulations remain limited by significant approximations in the treatment of neutrino transport and interaction rates. In this work, we assess the thermodynamic conditions under which neutrinos decouple from matter and show the effect of charged-current absorption, quasi-elastic scattering on nucleons and nuclei, pair-production processes, and inelastic neutrino-electron scattering for electron neutrinos, electron antineutrinos, and heavy-lepton neutrinos in the different thermodynamical conditions sampled by a simulation using an energy-dependent Monte Carlo neutrino transport.
  We first estimate opacities in the post-merger remnant assuming neutrinos in equilibria with the fluid, and find results consistent with previous studies performed on simulations using a gray two-moment scheme. We note the very distinct regions in which nucleon-nucleon Bremmstrahlung and electron-positron annihilation are active (high and low density regions, respectively). We then evaluate opacities using the actual distribution function of neutrinos within a Monte Carlo simulation. We show greatly increased pair annihilation rates in cold, low-density regions, especially for heavy-lepton neutrinos. We also show that inelastic scattering on electrons, which has not been included in merger simulations so far, makes important contributions to the thermalization of heavy-lepton neutrinos.

</details>

# math.AP [[Back]](#toc)

### [14] [On the solvability of the discrete nonlinear Schrodinger equation with subcubic potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29145)
*Daniel Maroncelli*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文分析了带离散拉普拉斯算子和非线性项的非线性薛定谔方程（discrete nonlinear Schrödinger equation）的可解性（solvability），其中参数β和ε为正实数，γ为非零实数，势函数g连续。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究离散非线性薛定谔方程的可解性，该方程在非线性光学、凝聚态物理等领域有重要应用，其离散形式对于数值模拟和理论分析均具有关键意义。

Method: 通过引入时间变量t上的标准前向差分算子（forward difference operator）Δ_t和标准后向差分算子（standard backward difference operator）∇_t，以及空间变量k上的离散拉普拉斯算子（discrete Laplacian）Δ_k²，建立了该方程的完整离散化框架，并在参数和势函数满足特定条件下进行分析。

Result: 在参数β>0、ε>0、γ≠0以及势函数g连续的条件下，给出了离散非线性薛定谔方程可解性的分析结论。

Conclusion: 在一定参数约束和势函数连续性假设下，所研究的离散非线性薛定谔方程具备可解性。

Abstract: In this paper, we analyze the solvability of the discrete nonlinear Schrödinger equation \begin{equation*} iβ(Δ_t+\nabla_t)φ(t,k) +γ|φ(t,k)|^2φ(t,k) +\varepsilon Δ_k^2φ(t,k-1) = g(t,φ(t,k)), \end{equation*} where $Δ_t$ and $Δ_k$ denote the standard forward difference operators in the variables $t$ and $k$, respectively, $\nabla_t$ denotes the standard backward difference operator in $t$, and \begin{equation*} Δ_k^2φ(t,k-1) = φ(t,k+1)-2φ(t,k)+φ(t,k-1) \end{equation*} is the discrete Laplacian operator in the spatial variable $k$. Throughout, we will assume the parameters $β$ and $\varepsilon$ are positive real numbers, the parameter $γ$ is a nonzero real number, and the potential function $g:\mathbb{Z}\times\mathbb{C}\to \mathbb{C}$ is continuous.

</details>

### [15] [Testing loop quantum gravity through EHT observations of M87* and Sgr A* using rotating holonomy-corrected black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28871)
*Heena Ali,Sushant G. Ghosh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope, EHT）对M87*和Sgr A*的观测数据，检验了带有完整量子修正的旋转黑洞（rotating holonomy-corrected black holes, RHCBHs）——一种圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity）的预言——是否在强引力区域留下可观测印记。结果表明，量子修正参数b会增大黑洞阴影，且非零的b值与当前EHT数据一致，使RHCBH成为经典克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）在强引力区域的可替代候选天体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EHT提供了检验强场引力（strong-field regime of gravity）的新工具。作者希望利用M87*和Sgr A*的阴影成像（shadow imaging）数据，首次在实际观测中检验圈量子引力是否在时空中留下可观测印记，从而评估量子修正黑洞作为经典克尔几何替代方案的可行性。

Method: 采用Kumar–Ghosh方法，基于阴影观测量（shadow observables）——阴影面积A和扁率D——对自旋参数a和量子修正参数b进行唯一确定。利用EHT对M87*（观测倾角θ_o=17°）和Sgr A*（θ_o=50°）的角直径（angular diameter）边界约束，对RHCBH模型施加参数限制。

Result: 量子修正参数b增大了黑洞阴影尺寸；在RHCBH中，顺行光子轨道（prograde photon orbits）随b增加向外移动，表明中心区域附近有效引力场减弱。与克尔裸奇点（Kerr naked singularities）产生开放式弧状阴影不同，RHCBH即使在没有事件视界的情况下仍能产生闭合阴影环。光子环（photon rings）在参数区间b_E ≤ b ≤ b_p内因存在不稳定圆形光子轨道而持续存在。M87*的角直径限给出：a=0时b ≤ 0.1319M，a=0.784M时b ≤ 0.421M；Sgr A*给出：a=0时b ≤ 0.5764M，a=0.6253M时b ≤ 0.7482M。

Conclusion: 非零的完整修正参数b与当前EHT数据一致，表明RHCBH在强引力区域提供了经典克尔几何的可行替代方案，是强有力的天体物理黑洞候选体。

Abstract: The Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) has provided a new tool for testing the strong-field regime of gravity by imaging the shadows of M87* and Sgr A*. These observations provide the first real opportunity to test whether quantum gravity--specifically loop quantum gravity--leaves observable imprints on spacetime. We use the EHT observations of M87* and Sgr A* to examine the observational signs of rotating holonomy-corrected black holes (RHCBHs). We discover that, in comparison to the typical Kerr black hole, the quantum correction parameter $b$ increases the size of the black hole shadow. As the deviation parameter $b$ increases in RHCBH, the prograde photon orbits shift outward, indicating a weaker effective gravitational field near the central region. Unlike Kerr naked singularities, which produce open arc-like shadows, the RHCBH spacetime can still produce closed shadow rings even in the absence of an event horizon. We find that photon rings continue to exist in the parameter range $b_E \leq b \leq b_p$, due to the presence of unstable circular photon orbits.We apply the Kumar--Ghosh method based on the shadow observables: the shadow area $A$ and the oblateness $D$ that together allow a unique determination of the spin parameter $a$ and the quantum correction parameter $b$. At $θ_o=17$\textdegree~, the angular diameter bound of M87$^{*}$ yields $b \leq 0.1319\,M$ at $a = 0\,$ and $b \leq 0.421\,M$ at $a = 0.784\,M$, while at $θ_o=50$\textdegree~, the angular diameter bound of Sgr A$^{*}$ yields $b \leq 0.5764\,M$ at $a = 0\,$ and $b \leq 0.7482\,M$ at $a = 0.6253\,M$ the Sgr~A$^{*}$. Our results show that nonzero values of the holonomy correction parameter are consistent with current EHT data, indicating that RHCBHs provide viable alternatives to the classical Kerr geometry in the strong-gravity regime and are strong astrophysical black hole candidates.

### [16] [Effective chemical potential and its phenomenological implications for the Hubble parameter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28881)
*L. L. Sales,F. C. Carvalho*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究在Tsallis统计框架内，通过引入非相对论性物质的等效化学势并将其与Unruh温度建立联系，推导出一个包含统计依赖项的哈勃参数表达式。该统计效应对哈勃常数敏感性的提升比先前相对论性构造高出约十个数量级，从而为哈勃张力问题提供了新的统计力学解释路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前宇宙学哈勃参数（Hubble parameter）在不同探针（如造父变星和宇宙微波背景）下的测量值之间存在持续张力，即“哈勃张力”（Hubble tension）。本研究旨在从Tsallis统计力学的非广延框架出发，探索非高斯统计效应对哈勃参数的影响。

Method: 在Tsallis统计框架中，识别了与相对论性和非相对论性区域对应的两种不同逸度（fugacity）定义。针对非相对论性部分，引入一个等效化学势（effective chemical potential），并建立其与吉布斯自由能（Gibbs free energy）的联系；进而探索该等效化学势与膨胀宇宙背景中加速轨迹相关的Unruh温度（Unruh-like temperature）之间的现象学对应关系。

Result: 推导出一个包含统计依赖项的哈勃参数有效表达式，该贡献来源于非相对论性物质部分。当非高斯统计效应被一致纳入非相对论性物质部分时，膨胀率对底层热统计假设（thermostatistical assumptions）的敏感性相比先前基于相对论性构造的现象学方案提高了约十个数量级。

Conclusion: 非高斯统计效应在非相对论性物质部分的一致引入，能够显著增强哈勃参数对热统计假设的敏感性，这一机制为理解哈勃张力的来源提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: In cosmological models, the Hubble parameter is determined by the time evolution of the scale factor, and current observations reveal a persistent tension between its values inferred from different probes, such as Cepheid variable stars and the cosmic microwave background. Within Tsallis' statistical framework, we identify two distinct definitions of fugacity associated with relativistic and non-relativistic regimes. For the non-relativistic sector, we introduce an effective chemical potential and establish its connection with the Gibbs free energy. We then explore a phenomenological correspondence between this effective chemical potential and an Unruh-like temperature associated with accelerated trajectories in an expanding cosmological background. As an application, we derive an effective expression for the Hubble parameter that includes a statistics-dependent contribution arising from the non-relativistic matter sector. This contribution suggests that non-Gaussian statistical effects, when consistently incorporated in the non-relativistic matter sector, can enhance the sensitivity of the expansion rate to underlying thermostatistical assumptions, achieving a substantial increase in sensitivity by approximately ten orders of magnitude when compared with previous relativistic constructions that investigated, at a phenomenological level, the discrepancy observed in current determinations of the Hubble constant.

</details>


### [17] [A Covariant Chiral-Hydrodynamic Formulation of the Dirac Equation in Curved Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28887)
*Jorge Meza-Domínguez,Tonatiuh Matos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文解决了狄拉克方程流体力学表述中长期存在的封闭性问题，通过在弯曲时空中发展协变手征流体力学形式，引入两个独立零矢量解耦左右手征分量，建立了与狄拉克场自由度精确对应的八实方程封闭系统，并应用于施瓦西几何获得精确径向解、准束缚态谱、准正则模频率和灰体因子，同时从手征流守恒导出霍金辐射通量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 狄拉克方程的流体力学表述（hydrodynamic formulation）长期受困于物理变量系统无法封闭的问题——若不诉诸无穷矩层级（infinite moment hierarchies）便无法闭合。这一根本性障碍阻碍了狄拉克场在弯曲时空背景下的完整流体力学描述。

Method: 在Weyl表象下引入两个独立零矢量（null vectors）$P_L^μ$和$P_R^μ$，解耦左右手征（chiral）分量。由此定义手征测地速度（chiral geodesic velocity）和随机速度（stochastic velocity），建立起恰好由八个实方程组成的封闭系统。

Result: 该形式自然地分离出自旋-轨道耦合项$(q/2)σ^{μν}F_{μν}$，并证明在无挠率广义相对论中自旋-引力耦合（spin-gravity coupling）为零。在施瓦西几何（Schwarzschild geometry）中获得了以合流Heun函数（confluent Heun functions）表示的精确径向解，直接计算了准束缚态谱（fermionic resonances）、准正则模频率（quasinormal mode frequencies）和灰体因子（greybody factors）。建立了精确能量平衡方程——狄拉克场的热力学第一定律，并纯粹从事件视界处的手征流守恒（chiral flux conservation）推导出霍金辐射通量（Hawking radiation flux）。

Conclusion: 该工作不仅为自旋-1/2流体（spin-1/2 fluids）提供了封闭的流体力学理论，同时建立了在强引力背景（strong gravitational backgrounds）下分析量子信息和费米子动力学的统一框架。

Abstract: The hydrodynamic formulation of the Dirac equation has historically been hindered by the inability to close the system of physical variables without resorting to infinite moment hierarchies. We resolve this longstanding issue by developing a fully covariant chiral-hydrodynamic formulation of the Dirac field in curved spacetime. Working in the Weyl representation, we introduce two independent null vectors, $P_L^μ$ and $P_R^μ$, which decouple the left and right chiral components. This allows us to define chiral geodesic and stochastic velocities, yielding a closed system of exactly eight real equations that corresponds directly to the Dirac field degrees of freedom. Remarkably, this formulation naturally isolates the spin-orbit coupling $(q/2)σ^{μν}F_{μν}$ while demonstrating the vanishing of the spin-gravity coupling in torsion-free general relativity. To demonstrate the analytical power of this framework, we specialize to the Schwarzschild geometry. We obtain exact radial solutions in terms of confluent Heun functions and directly compute the quasi-bound state spectrum (fermionic resonances), quasinormal mode frequencies, and greybody factors. Furthermore, by establishing an exact energy balance equation -- representing the first law of thermodynamics for Dirac fields -- we derive the Hawking radiation flux purely from chiral flux conservation at the event horizon. This work not only provides a closed hydrodynamic theory for spin-1/2 fluids but also establishes a unified framework for analyzing quantum information and fermion dynamics in strong gravitational backgrounds.

</details>


### [18] [Greybody Factors, Absorption Cross Sections and Hawking Radiation of Holonomy-Corrected Schwarzschild Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28917)
*Bekir Can Lütfüoğlu,Javlon Rayimbaev,Bekzod Rahmatov,Saidmuhammad Ahmedov,Nuriddin Kurbonov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了圈量子引力启发的全息修正史瓦西黑洞上最小耦合无质量标量场、电磁场和无质量狄拉克场的灰体因子、吸收截面和霍金能量发射率。通过直接数值积分结合一阶和六阶WKB估计求解径向波动方程，发现全息修正增强标量透射但抑制整体霍金辐射，电磁通道受抑制最强，费米子通道在全息参数α显著时占主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究背景为圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity）启发的全息修正（holonomy correction）史瓦西黑洞上，最小耦合无质量标量场、电磁场和无质量狄拉克场的灰体因子（greybody factors）、吸收截面（absorption cross sections）和霍金能量发射率（Hawking energy-emission rates）如何受到全息修正的影响。

Method: 通过直接数值积分求解径向波动方程，并采用一阶和六阶WKB估计（WKB estimates）作为互补验证手段。黑洞几何由无量纲全息参数（holonomy parameter）控制。

Result: 标量、电磁和狄拉克三种通道响应不同：标量主导模透明度增加，电磁阈轻微上移，狄拉克主导模仅被轻微修正。标量吸收截面保持通用低频极限，电磁截面主要在红外区域改变，狄拉克截面则出现强烈抑制的低频尾部。由于霍金温度（Hawking temperature）单调下降，热抑制主导辐射输出，全息修正增强低标量透射但整体抑制霍金辐射，电磁通道抑制最强，费米子通道在全息参数α显著时占主导。

Conclusion: 全息修正对黑洞辐射有选择性影响：增强标量通道透射，但抑制总体霍金辐射，电磁通道受抑最严重，而费米子通道在全息参数较大时成为主导辐射通道。

Abstract: We study greybody factors, absorption cross sections and Hawking energy-emission rates for minimally coupled massless scalar, electromagnetic and massless Dirac test fields on the loop-quantum-gravity-inspired holonomy-corrected Schwarzschild black hole. The geometry is controlled by a dimensionless holonomy parameter, and the radial wave equations are solved by direct numerical integration with first- and sixth-order WKB estimates as complementary checks. The scalar, electromagnetic and Dirac channels respond differently: the dominant scalar mode becomes more transparent, the electromagnetic threshold shifts slightly upward, and the dominant Dirac mode is only mildly modified. The scalar absorption cross section retains the universal low-frequency limit, the electromagnetic cross section changes mainly in the infrared, and the Dirac cross section develops a strongly suppressed low-frequency tail. Since the Hawking temperature falls monotonically, thermal suppression dominates the radiative output. Thus the holonomy correction enhances low-lying scalar transmission but suppresses Hawking radiation overall, with the electromagnetic sector most strongly quenched and the fermionic sector dominant once $α$ is appreciable.

</details>


### [19] [Relativistic Elastic Response to Gravitational Waves: Explicit Solutions for a Rectangular Plate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28932)
*José Natário,Filipe Nazaré*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在相对论性弹性力学（relativistic elasticity）框架下，系统推导了引力波（gravitational waves）与弹性体相互作用的线性化方程，并针对薄矩形弹性板给出了解析解，包括诱导位移、能量沉积以及板自身振荡产生的引力波发射，为共振型引力波探测器提供了完全相对论性的理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究引力波与弹性体的相互作用，并基于相对论性弹性力学（relativistic elasticity）给出完全相对论的推导，摆脱以往唯象有效势方法的局限。

Method: 从相对论性弹性力学的拉格朗日量（Lagrangian formulation）出发，将作用量展开至弹性场导数的二阶和度规扰动（metric perturbation）的一阶，从而线性化控制方程。随后将形式化应用于沿引力波传播和偏振方向放置的薄矩形弹性板，对于泊松比（Poisson ratio）为零的材料求解解耦方程。

Result: 导出了Dyson相互作用项的自然出现。对于短引力波爆发和连续谐波，给出了板内诱导位移和能量沉积的闭式表达式（closed-form expressions）。进一步计算了连续谐波激励下板自身振荡发射的引力波。

Conclusion: 该工作为引力波弹性响应提供了完全相对论性的推导，并给出了与共振型引力波探测器（resonant gravitational wave detectors）相关的显式可解例子。

Abstract: We study the interaction between gravitational waves and elastic bodies within the framework of relativistic elasticity. Starting from the Lagrangian formulation of relativistic elasticity, we derive the linearized equations governing the response of a homogeneous and isotropic solid to a weak gravitational wave by expanding the action to quadratic order in the elastic field derivatives and to linear order in the metric perturbation. In this way, Dyson's interaction term from the effective potential approach emerges naturally from the relativistic theory.
  We then apply the formalism to a thin rectangular elastic plate aligned with the direction of propagation and polarization of a plus-polarized gravitational wave. For a material with vanishing Poisson ratio, the equations decouple and admit simple explicit solutions. We obtain closed-form expressions for the induced displacements and for the energy deposited on the plate by both short gravitational wave bursts and continuous harmonic waves. Finally, we compute the gravitational wave emission generated by the oscillating plate itself under continuous harmonic excitation. These results provide a fully relativistic derivation of the elastic response to gravitational waves together with explicit solvable examples relevant to resonant gravitational wave detectors.

</details>


### [20] [When the Ringing Stops: Purely Imaginary Modes in the Ringdown Spectrum of Dynamical Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28951)
*Lodovico Capuano,Thomas Lovo,Gorka Prieto-Varela,Subhodeep Sarkar,Adrien Kuntz,Enrico Barausse,Dawood Kothawala*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在动态球对称黑洞时空中研究准正则模，发现除标准光环比模式外还存在纯虚特征值，并通过解析（Heun函数连接系数）与数值（超双曲切片谱方法及时间域模拟）方法验证了这些纯虚模式支配晚期信号的指数衰减尾巴，在史瓦西极限下还原为幂律尾巴。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将准正则模（quasinormal modes）的频率域分析扩展至质量恒定速率演化的动态球对称黑洞时空（dynamical, spherically symmetric black hole spacetime），探索非静态背景下频谱的新特征。

Method: 解析计算基于Heun函数（Heun functions）连接系数（connection coefficients）的新形式体系；数值计算采用超双曲切片（hyperboloidal slices）上的谱方法（spectral method）；频率域结果再通过独立的时间域模拟（time-domain simulations）进行交叉验证。

Result: 发现频谱中存在纯虚特征值（purely imaginary eigenvalues）这一新特征；解析与数值结果高度吻合；时间域模拟一致表明纯虚模式通过指数衰减尾巴（exponentially decaying tails）控制晚期信号；在史瓦西极限（Schwarzschild limit）下，纯虚模式退化为熟悉的史瓦西幂律尾巴（power-law tail）。

Conclusion: 动态黑洞时空中除标准光环比模式外还存在纯虚模式，该模式主导晚期信号衰减行为，且在静态史瓦西极限下平滑过渡为已知的幂律衰减形式。

Abstract: We extend the frequency-domain analysis of quasinormal modes in a dynamical, spherically symmetric black hole spacetime undergoing constant-rate mass evolution. In particular, we report a novel feature of the spectrum: the presence of purely imaginary eigenvalues in addition to the usual light-ring modes. We study the frequencies of these modes both analytically and numerically. The analytical calculation uses a novel formalism based on recent advances in connection coefficients of Heun functions. We then compute the frequencies numerically using a spectral method on hyperboloidal slices and find excellent agreement between the two approaches. Finally, we validate the frequency-domain results against an independent set of time-domain simulations. Our analysis shows that the purely imaginary modes govern the late-time signal through exponentially decaying tails. In the Schwarzschild limit, both frequency- and time-domain studies consistently show that the purely imaginary modes give rise to the familiar Schwarzschild power-law tail.

</details>


### [21] [Signatures of loop quantum gravity in primordial black hole cosmologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28953)
*Antoine Dierckx,Sébastien Clesse,Francesca Vidotto*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于圈量子引力（Loop Quantum Gravity）的启发，研究了暗物质（Dark Matter）可能部分或全部由稳定普朗克残骸（Planckian remnants）构成的情景，分析了不同现象学区域，并对原始黑洞（Primordial Black Holes）的初始丰度和残骸的最终丰度给出了新的约束。研究发现，特定质量范围（约10^3 kg）的原始黑洞通过霍金蒸发（Hawking evaporation）自然重新加热宇宙，其残骸可全部构成当代暗物质，且无需精细调节初始丰度。该情景可通过原初引力波（gravitational waves）和有效相对论自由度（effective number of relativistic degrees of freedom）等观测信号进行检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索暗物质是否可能部分或全部由原始黑洞（Primordial Black Holes, PBHs）蒸发后留下的稳定普朗克尺度残骸（Planckian remnants）构成，这一可能性受到圈量子引力（Loop Quantum Gravity, LQG）等理论的启发。

Method: 区分了不同的现象学区域（phenomenological regimes），包括可能触发早期物质主导时代（early matter-dominated epoch）的情景，并基于霍金蒸发（Hawking evaporation）产物和宇宙学约束推导了原始黑洞初始丰度与残骸最终丰度之间的新限制。

Result: 质量轻于10^3 kg的原始黑洞会过度产生普朗克残骸；质量在10^3至10^12 kg之间的原始黑洞的霍金辐射产物意味着普朗克残骸只能构成高度次主导的暗物质组分；质量约为10^3 kg的原始黑洞可自然实现霍金蒸发重新加热宇宙，且其残骸完全构成当代暗物质，初始丰度可在10^-10到量级1之间无需精细调节。

Conclusion: 该早期宇宙学模型会产生独特的观测信号，包括由原初或泊松涨落（primordial or Poisson fluctuations）引发的标量诱导引力波（scalar-induced gravitational waves），这些信号在早期原始黑洞主导时代被放大。LIGO/Virgo/KAGRA、爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）、LISA以及有效相对论自由度（effective number of relativistic degrees of freedom）的探测可用于约束原始黑洞初始丰度和普朗克残骸的当代丰度。

Abstract: The possibility that Dark Matter (DM) is partially or totally constituted by stable Planckian remnants of light Primordial Black Holes (PBHs), suggested for instance by Loop Quantum Gravity (LQG), is investigated. Distinct phenomenological regimes are identified, including scenarios that trigger an early matter-dominated epoch. New constraints are derived on the initial PBH and final remnant abundances. We show that a significant initial abundance of PBHs lighter than $10^3$ kg would overproduce Planckian relics, implying that any observational evidence for such PBHs would challenge models with quasi-stable remnants. Conversely, the products of Hawking radiation from PBHs with masses between $10^3$ and $10^{12}$ kg impose that Planckian relics could only be a highly subdominant DM component. We identify a PBH mass around $10^3$ kg for which Hawking evaporation naturally reheats the Universe while the remnants entirely constitute the present-day DM. Such a scenario does not require fine-tuning the initial abundance of PBH of this mass, which could range from $10^{-10}$ to order one. These early-Universe cosmologies yield distinct observational signatures: scalar-induced gravitational waves sourced by primordial or Poisson fluctuations that are amplified by the early PBH-dominated era. Current and future observations of LIGO/Virgo/KAGRA, the Einstein Telescope and LISA, as well as probes of the effective number of relativistic degrees of freedom, can be used to probe and constrain the initial PBH abundance and the present-day abundance of Planckian relics.

</details>


### [22] [Shadows of naked singularities and superspinars related to the revisited Kerr-de Sitter spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29049)
*Daniel Charbulák,Zdeněk Stuchlík*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过构造回望的Kerr-de Sitter裸奇点（rKdSNS）时空的阴影（shadow），并与标准KdSNS时空对比，发现只有在足够大的宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）下两者的阴影差异才显著；对于观测所给定的宇宙学常数和宇宙中大质量天体，当前仪器无法区分这些差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究回望的Kerr-de Sitter裸奇点（rKdSNS）时空的超自旋体（superspinars）阴影，并与标准KdSNS时空对比，以检验两者在观测上的可区分性。

Method: 针对rKdSNS时空的所有类别，确定与多种基本参考系（包括局部非旋转参考系LNRF、径向逃逸参考系和圆测地参考系）相关的局部逃逸锥（local escape cones）；利用这些局部逃逸锥构建KdS超自旋体的阴影，阴影对应位于静态半径附近的远端静态观测者（LNRF）或因宇宙膨胀而径向接近宇宙视界（cosmic horizon）的超自旋体。

Result: 建立了rKdSNS与标准KdSNS时空阴影的差异，并在足够大的无量纲宇宙学常数下展示了这些差异；对于观测给定的宇宙学常数和宇宙中最大质量天体，当前观测仪器无法分辨这些阴影差异。

Conclusion: 尽管超自旋体阴影在理论上存在差异，但在实际可观测条件下（基于当前宇宙学常数和最大天体质量），这些差异不可观测，表明现有仪器无法区分rKdSNS和标准KdSNS时空的阴影特征。

Abstract: We construct shadows of superspinars described by the revisited Kerr-de Sitter (rKdS) naked singularity (NS) spacetimes and compare them with those of the standard KdSNS spacetimes. For all the classes of the rKdSNS spacetimes we determine local escape cones related to variety of fundamental frames: locally nonrotating frames (LNRFs), radially escaping frames, and circular geodesic frames related to marginally stable obits of the rKdSNS spacetimes. The local escape cones (and their complementary cones) are then applied to construct the shadow of the KdS superspinars related to the distant static observers represented by the LNRFs located near the so-called static radius where the spacetime is close to the asymptotically flat region of the Kerr spacetimes, or the superspinars radially approaching, due to the Universe's expansion, the cosmic horizon of the spacetime. Differences of the shadows in the rKdSNS and standard KdSNS spacetimes are established and demonstrated for sufficiently large values of the dimensionless cosmological constant. For the observationally given cosmological constant and masses of the largest objects in the Universe, the shadow differences are not observable using recent observational instruments.

</details>


### [23] [Quantum transitions of vector vortex light in gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29519)
*Haorong Wu,Xilong Fan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个理论框架，描述矢量涡旋光场与引力波（gravitational waves, GWs）之间的完整相互作用。通过微扰论和电磁场正则量子化，计算出矢量贝塞尔光束在GW中传播时的量子跃迁概率，揭示了十四种不同量子跃迁通道，并提出一种基于量子跃迁的新型腔式GW探测方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力波探测方案（如LIGO）依赖宏观臂长变化，易受位移型噪声（如地震噪声）干扰。本文旨在探索一种基于量子跃迁而非宏观位移的GW探测新机制，从而规避传统方案的噪声瓶颈。

Method: 采用微扰论（perturbation theory）和电磁场的正则量子化（canonical quantization）方法，计算矢量贝塞尔光束（vector Bessel beams）在引力波背景下传播时的量子跃迁概率，分析轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum, OAM）和自旋角动量（spin angular momentum, SAM）的转变规律。

Result: GW诱导出十四种量子跃迁通道，将初态$\ket{σ,l}$映射到$\ket{σ+Δσ,l+j-Δσ}$，其中SAM变化$Δσ\in \{-2, 0, 2\}$，总角动量变化$j\in \{-3,\dots,3\}$。SAM守恒的OAM跃迁（$\ket{σ,l}\rightarrow \ket{σ,l\pm1}$）最具实验可探测性，而自旋翻转跃迁被强烈抑制。SAM反向还会引起OAM跃迁通道的不对称偏移，体现SAM与OAM的耦合。

Conclusion: 基于上述跃迁通道，提出一种新型腔式GW探测构型。该方案依赖量子跃迁而非宏观臂长变化，因此对位移型噪声（如地震噪声）不敏感，为GW观测提供了新范式和新频段。

Abstract: We develop a theoretical framework to describe the full interaction between vector vortex light fields and gravitational waves (GWs). Using perturbation theory and the canonical quantization of the electromagnetic field, we calculate the quantum transition probabilities of vector Bessel beams propagating through GWs. We demonstrate that GWs induce fourteen different quantum transition channels across orbital angular momentum (OAM) $l$ and spin angular momentum (SAM) $σ$, mapping initial states $\ket{σ,l}$ to $\ket{σ+Δσ,l+j-Δσ}$, where $Δσ\in \{-2, 0, 2\}$ represents the change in SAM and $j \in \{-3, \dots, 3\}$ denotes the change in total angular momentum. Among these channels, SAM-conserving transitions between OAM states, specifically $\ket{σ, l}\rightarrow \ket{σ, l\pm 1}$, provide the most viable mechanism for experimental detection. Conversely, spin-flip transitions are shown to be heavily suppressed relative to OAM transitions. Additionally, the reversal of SAM induces an asymmetric shift in the OAM transition channels, reflecting the underlying coupling between SAM and OAM during the gravitational interaction. Based on these transition channels, we propose a new cavity-based GW detection configuration. By relying on quantum transitions rather than macroscopic arm-length changes, this scheme is inherently insensitive to displacement-based disturbances like seismic noise, offering a new paradigm and frequency bands for GW observation.

</details>


### [24] [Decay criteria for asymptotic freedom in plane gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29636)
*Qi-Liang Zhao,Li-Ming Cao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了平面波时空（plane-wave spacetime）中记忆效应（memory effect）在超出理想夹层波近似（sandwich-wave approximation）条件下的成立条件，发现常用的渐近平坦条件不充分，并提出了基于加权衰变标准的渐近自由运动分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在平面波引力波背景中，传统上认为标准出射自由数据（outgoing free data）存在的前提是波剖面（profile）$A(U)$在$U\to\infty$时趋于零。然而，该条件是否严格充分尚不清楚，因此需要更精确地刻画保证记忆效应成立所需的渐近行为条件。

Method: 从横向测地线方程（transverse geodesic equation）的积分形式出发，推导了加权衰变标准（weighted decay criteria），并利用三种典型剖面（Scarf型、反立方型、反平方型）的新解析解，对渐近动力学进行了显式分类。

Result: 将渐近动力学划分为三种类型：强渐近自由（strongly asymptotically free）、弱渐近自由（weakly asymptotically free）和非渐近自由（non-asymptotically free）。值得注意的是，弱渐近自由运动中的漂移修正（drift correction）仅影响非零出射速度的轨迹，因此不妨碍位移记忆（displacement memory）。

Conclusion: 该分类可通过累积潮汐矩阵（accumulated tidal matrix）加以表达，表明上述效应是内在曲率效应（intrinsic curvature effect），而非坐标人为性（coordinate artifact）。

Abstract: We investigate when plane-wave memory admits standard outgoing free data beyond the idealized sandwich-wave approximation. For a Brinkmann plane wave with profile $A(U)$, the commonly used condition $A(U)|_{U\to\infty}=0$ is not sufficient to guarantee ordinary asymptotically free motion. From the integral form of the transverse geodesic equation, we derive weighted decay criteria which divide the asymptotic dynamics into strongly asymptotically free, weakly asymptotically free, and non-asymptotically free motions. These motions are realized explicitly by the new analytical solutions of three typical examples: a Scarf profile, an inverse-cubic profile, and an inverse-square profile. A surprisingly feature is that the drift correction in the weakly asymptotically free motion affects only trajectories with nonzero outgoing velocity and therefore does not obstruct displacement memory. We further express the classification in terms of the accumulated tidal matrix, showing that it is an intrinsic curvature effect rather than a coordinate artifact.

</details>


### [25] [Gyroscopic Precession in Axisymmetric Kerr Spacetime: Horizon Regularity and Coordinate Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29759)
*Paulami Majumder*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用协变Frenet-Serret形式体系（covariant Frenet-Serret formalism）研究了Kerr时空中沿Killing和非Killing类时轨迹的陀螺进动（gyroscopic precession）。通过分析Boyer-Lindquist和Kerr-Schild两种坐标系下的进动频率，证明近地平线处进动频率的发散是坐标人为产物（coordinate artefact），而非事件视界（event horizon）的不变签名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究在强场区域观测到陀螺进动频率在近地平线处出现发散，但该发散是否具有物理实质尚不明确。本文旨在检验该发散是否由坐标选择引起，并探寻其与事件视界结构之间的内在关联。

Method: 采用协变Frenet-Serret形式体系，在Kerr时空下沿Killing与非Killing类时轨迹进行陀螺进动分析。同时在Boyer-Lindquist坐标系（horizon-penetrating性质较弱）和Kerr-Schild坐标系（horizon-penetrating性质较强）中对比研究顺行（prograde）与逆行（retrograde）运动，特别考察一般螺旋轨迹（generic spiral trajectories）下的进动频率行为。

Result: 在Boyer-Lindquist坐标系中，近地平线处进动频率出现发散；而转向Kerr-Schild坐标系后，该发散消失。进动频率的有限性由轨迹的类时性（timelike character）决定，而非事件视界本身的存在性。因此，强场区域陀螺进动的发散是坐标人为产物，不能作为视界结构的不变签名（invariant signature）。

Conclusion: 陀螺进动频率在近地平线区域的表观发散完全源于坐标选择，不具有物理不变性。这一结论否定了此前将该发散作为黑洞视界结构探测工具的提议，强调了在强引力场分析中采用horizon-penetrating坐标系的重要性。

Abstract: We investigate gyroscopic precession along Killing and non-Killing timelike trajectories in Kerr spacetime using the covariant Frenet--Serret formalism. The precession frequency is analyzed for both prograde and retrograde motion in Boyer--Lindquist and horizon-penetrating Kerr--Schild coordinate systems. For generic spiral trajectories, we show explicitly that the divergence of the precession frequency appearing near the horizon in Boyer--Lindquist coordinates disappears in Kerr--Schild coordinates. Our analysis demonstrates that the finiteness of the Frenet--Serret precession frequency is determined by the timelike character of the trajectory rather than by the existence of an event horizon itself. These results indicate that the divergence of gyroscopic precession in the strong-field regime is a coordinate artefact and therefore cannot serve as an invariant signature of horizon structure.

</details>


### [26] [Modified Entropy from Action Principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29814)
*A. Dehyadegari,A. Sheykhi*

TL;DR: 本文通过扩展爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量（Einstein-Hilbert action），引入关于里奇标量（Ricci scalar）和 Kretschmann 标量（Kretschmann scalar）不变量的任意函数，提出了一种修正引力理论。推导了无高阶导数的修正弗裏德曼方程（Friedmann equations），并利用引力-热力学对偶（gravity-thermodynamics conjecture），得到了视界表观视界（apparent horizon）上修正熵（modified entropy）的一般表达式，从而在曲率不变量修正引力与广义熵函数之间建立了自洽的热力学框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力理论在解释宇宙加速膨胀等观测现象时存在局限，因此需要构造更一般的修正引力模型。本文旨在通过引入曲率不变量（curvature invariants）的任意函数拓展作用量，并与热力学框架相结合，以统一描述引力与视界热力学行为。

Method: 采用作用量变分法推导修正 Friedmann 方程；借助引力-热力学猜想分析表观视界的热力学行为；结合热力学第一定律与修正 Friedmann 方程，推导出表观视界熵的一般形式，并应用于多种已知熵模型。

Result: 得到了无高阶导数的修正 Friedmann 方程，该方程在极限情形下回归标准形式；导出了一个通用的表观视界修正熵表达式，适用于多种熵模型。

Conclusion: 本文建立的框架成功地将基于曲率不变量的修正引力理论与宇宙学表观视界上的广义熵函数联系起来，为理解引力的热力学性质提供了统一且自洽的途径。

Abstract: We propose a modified gravity theory by extending the Einstein-Hilbert action with an arbitrary function of the Ricci scalar and the Kretschmann scalar invariants. The resulting modified Friedmann equations for a spatially flat FRW universe are derived, which remain free of higher-order derivatives and reduce to the standard Friedmann equations in the limiting case. Employing the gravity-thermodynamics conjecture, we investigate the thermodynamic behavior at the apparent horizon and derive the corresponding modified entropy. Using the first law of thermodynamics together with the modified Friedmann equations, we obtain a general expression for the apparent horizon entropy. This formalism allows us to compute the modified entropy for various well-known entropy models. Our approach establishes a consistent thermodynamic framework linking modified gravity theories constructed from curvature invariants to generalized entropy functions on the cosmological apparent horizon.

### [27] [Problems of cosmology on small scales of the Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29899)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准宇宙学模型ΛCDM在约1 Mpc的小尺度上，理论预测与观测数据之间存在显著矛盾，有必要系统梳理这些挑战并考察局域宇宙中的观测证据。

Method: 基于局域体积（Local volume，半径12 Mpc）内发光星系与矮星系的多种参数，分析了恒星物质（stellar matter）和暗物质（dark matter）的平均密度随距离的变化；通过邻近星系的角动量（angular momentum）分布数据，以及星系系统中基于内部（维里化，virialized）成员和邻近星系运动得出的暗物质质量估计进行比较研究。

Result: 局域宇宙中暗物质密度测量值$Ω_m = 0.08\pm0.02$显著低于全球值$Ω_m = 0.30\pm0.02$，表明局域尺度上的暗物质分布与宇宙平均存在明显偏差。

Conclusion: ΛCDM模型在小尺度（~1 Mpc）上面临六大挑战，局域宇宙观测数据支持的较低暗物质密度对标准宇宙学模型构成重要约束。

Abstract: Six challenges for the standard cosmological model $Λ$CDM are listed, which arise when comparing theoretical predictions with observational data on scales of ~1 Mpc. Different parameters of luminous and dwarf galaxies in the local sphere with a radius of 12 Mpc are presented. The average densities of stellar matter and dark matter are reproduced depending on a distance in the Local volume. Observational data on distribution of angular momentum of nearby galaxies are considered. A comparison of the dark matter mass estimates for systems of galaxies based on motions of their internal (virialized) members and neighboring galaxies is given. The reasons for the low derived value of the dark matter density, $Ω_m = 0.08\pm0.02$, in the Local Universe with respect to the global value $Ω_m = 0.30\pm0.02$ are discussed

### [28] [Light rings and optical appearances of naked singularities, solitons, and black holes in beyond Horndeski gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29974)
*Hyat Huang,Jutta Kunz,Rashmi Uniyal,Xiao Qian Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过分析超越Horndeski引力（beyond Horndeski gravity）中具有初级标量毛发的致密天体的测地线结构（geodesic structure）与光学图像，发现不同视界结构的天体（如无视界奇异点、规则孤子、规则黑洞及多视界黑洞等）在薄盘光学图像上可能表现出高度相似的观测特征，视界数目并不直接决定光学外观。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究超越Horndeski引力中具有初级标量毛发的致密天体的测地线结构与光学外观，并考察不同视界分支的天体是否可通过光学观测加以区分。

Method: 基于Shkola等人提出的解析解，固定理论参数、变化质量参数以遍历多种时空类型；通过分类视界结构、分析零测地线（null geodesics）与时检测地线（timelike geodesics），重点研究光环（light rings）、最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbits, ISCO）及静态球面（static spheres），并采用光线追踪（ray tracing）计算薄盘光学图像。

Result: 视界数目未直接编码于图像中：无视界天体可呈现类似阴影的中央凹陷，多视界黑洞在外部光环与盘结构相似时可接近单视界黑洞的外观。光学外观主要由光子势（photon potential）与盘内缘决定，深层视界结构仅留下间接印记。定量径向轮廓诊断表明简并性主要是形态上的：在固定碰撞参数下轮廓有差异，但按临界碰撞参数（critical impact parameter）重新缩放后高度接近。

Conclusion: 超越Horndeski引力中不同的致密天体分支可以共享相似的观测信号，这为区分视界结构设定了观测上的简并性限制。

Abstract: We investigate the geodesic structure and optical appearance of compact objects with primary scalar hair in shift- and parity-symmetric beyond Horndeski gravity. The analytic solution considered here depends on a theory parameter and a dimensionless mass parameter \cite{Bakopoulos:2023sdm}. For a fixed theory parameter, varying the mass traces a family of static spacetimes that can interpolate between timelike naked singularities, regular solitons, regular black holes, Reissner-Nordström-like black holes, multi-horizon black holes, and Schwarzschild-like black holes. We classify these branches by their horizon structure and analyze null and timelike geodesics, focusing on light rings, innermost stable circular orbits, and static spheres. We then compute thin-disk optical images by ray tracing. We find that the number of horizons is not directly encoded in the image: horizonless objects can show shadow-like central depressions, while multi-horizon black holes can closely resemble single-horizon black holes when their exterior light ring and disk structures are similar. Thus, the optical appearance is governed mainly by the photon potential and the disk inner edge, with the deeper horizon structure leaving only an indirect imprint. Quantitative radial-profile diagnostics confirm that the degeneracy is mainly morphological: the profiles differ at fixed impact parameter, but become much closer after rescaling by the critical impact parameter. These results provide a concrete example of how distinct compact object branches in beyond Horndeski gravity can share similar observational signatures.

</details>


### [29] [Supermassive black hole seeds from direct collapse of CDM-curvature peaks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30145)
*Marco Galoppo,Marco Bruni,Tomohiro Harada*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在完全非线性相对论框架下，利用 LTB 和准球对称 Szekeres 精确解研究物质主导时期原初扰动非线性增长与坍缩形成的黑洞，发现正弦与高斯型扰动无法形成黑洞，而广泛补偿曲率峰可形成种子黑洞，并给出了坍缩时间与终态奇点类型的判断准则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于物质主导时期原初扰动的非线性坍缩研究黑洞形成过程，并建立从初始曲率扰动数据直接推断坍缩时间与黑洞形成可行性的理论判据。

Method: 采用 Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi（LTB）解和准球对称 Szekeres 解作为平坦 FLRW ΛCDM背景上的精确扰动，将主动引力质量和曲率函数表示为守恒规范不变曲率扰动 $\mathcal{R}_c$ 及其空间导数的函数，据此推导反转点、坍缩和视界形成时间及正则条件。

Result: 正弦与高斯型扰动不构成可行的黑洞形成通道，而广泛的补偿曲率峰（compensated curvature peaks）可以形成黑洞；$10^{3}-10^{6}~\mathrm{M}_\odot$ 级大质量黑洞种子在红移 $z>5$ 完全形成，核心坍缩始于 $10 \lesssim z \lesssim 16$；可从初始随动曲率数据直接区分坍缩终态奇点类型（点状、雪茄状或薄饼状）。

Conclusion: 初始剪切各向异性在确定坍缩终态奇点类型中起关键作用，广泛补偿曲率峰是原初黑洞形成的有效通道。

Abstract: We study black hole (BH) formation from the nonlinear growth and collapse of primordial perturbations during the matter-dominated era. Modelling cold dark matter (CDM) as pressureless dust, we describe the collapse in a fully nonlinear relativistic framework using the Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi (LTB) and quasi-spherical Szekeres solutions as exact perturbations of a spatially-flat Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) $Λ$CDM background. At first order in relativistic scalar perturbation theory, the growing mode of any relevant quantity can be expressed in terms of the conserved gauge-invariant curvature perturbation $\mathcal{R}_c$, which acts as a potential for the 3-curvature of hypersurfaces orthogonal to the matter 4-velocity. We use this result to express the active gravitational mass and curvature functions of the LTB and Szekeres models in terms of the initial values of $\mathcal{R}_c$ and its spatial derivatives. From these initial curvature data we derive: (i) the turn-around, collapse, and apparent-horizon formation times, and (ii) the regularity conditions required for BH formation. We show that sinusoidal and Gaussian profiles do not provide viable BH-forming channels, whereas broad compensated curvature peaks, naturally predicted by peak theory, do. We then estimate the formation times of $10^{3}-10^{6}~\mathrm{M}_\odot$ massive BH seeds produced by the direct collapse of primordial CDM curvature peaks, finding full BH formation at redshifts $z>5$, with core collapse beginning at $10 \lesssim z \lesssim 16$. Finally, we characterize the local dynamics and singularity type of the collapse (point-like, cigar-like, or pancake-like) directly from the initial comoving curvature data, clarifying the role of the initial shear in selecting the collapse end-state.

</details>


### [30] [Primary Constraints of Newer General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30221)
*Carmen Ferrara,Alexey Golovnev,María José Guzmán*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了新型广义相对论（Newer General Relativity）——一种基于无挠远平行几何（torsionless teleparallel geometry）的引力理论——中的初级约束结构（primary constraint structure）。通过将拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）分解为标量、矢量和张量扇区，作者系统刻画了度规共轭动量中出现的初级约束，发现张量扇区有5个约束、矢量扇区有3个约束，并在标量扇区发现了一个此前未被报道的简并性（degeneracy），该简并性依赖于参数条件可产生1个或2个标量初级约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解新型广义相对论（Newer General Relativity）的约束结构是揭示该理论动力学自由度（degrees of freedom）与规范对称性（gauge symmetries）的关键。此前文献仅部分讨论了该理论的约束，而标量扇区中的简并性（degeneracy）尚未被系统研究。

Method: 作者将引力拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）分解，计算了与度规（metric）共轭的正则动量（canonical momenta），并通过判定速度-动量映射是否可逆来识别初级约束（primary constraints）。通过完全非线性的分解将结果组织为标量（scalar）、矢量（vector）和张量（tensor）三个扇区。此外，还研究了对称远平行引力（symmetric teleparallel gravity）协变表述下的初级约束。

Result: 恢复了文献中已有的张量扇区的5个初级约束和矢量扇区的3个初级约束。在标量扇区发现了一个此前未被报道的简并性，依据参数$c_i$条件的不同，可产生1个或2个标量初级约束。同时获得了对称远平行引力协变表述下的初级约束。

Conclusion: 本文完整刻画了新型广义相对论的初级约束结构，特别是发现了标量扇区的新简并性，这有助于更深入地理解该理论的动力学内容与对称性性质。

Abstract: We study the primary constraint structure of Newer General Relativity, a gravity theory based on a torsionless teleparallel geometry. The gravitational action is built from a scalar formed by quadratic combinations of the nonmetricity tensor, with arbitrary coefficients $c_i$ in the Lagrangian. We decompose the Lagrangian and compute the canonical momenta conjugate to the metric. We characterize the primary constraints arising from these momenta by identifying when the map between velocities and momenta becomes non-invertible, and organize the outcome through a fully nonlinear decomposition into scalar, vector and tensor sectors. Comparing with previous results in the literature, we recover five and three primary constraints associated with the tensor and vector sectors, respectively. We also identify a previously unreported degeneracy in the scalar sector, which yields either one or two scalar primary constraints depending on the conditions imposed on the parameters $c_i$. Finally, we obtain the primary constraints associated with the covariant formulation of symmetric teleparallel gravity.

</details>


### [31] [The N--P and 1+1+2 correspondence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30255)
*Abbas M Sherif,Peter K S Dunsby*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了 Newman–Penrose 形式与 1+1+2 半类时协变形式之间的完整对应关系，将所有 Newman–Penrose 自旋系数、Ricci 标量和 Weyl 标量用 1+1+2 分解的标量、矢量和张量变量表达，并应用于推导局部旋转对称 II 类时空中未来外陷获视界存在的必要条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Newman–Penrose 形式和 1+1+2 半类时协变形式是广义相对论中两种广泛使用的形式体系，但二者之间缺乏直接的对应关系，限制了这两种方法之间的交叉应用。

Method: 通过将 Newman–Penrose 形式中的所有自旋系数（spin coefficients）、Ricci 标量（Ricci scalars）和 Weyl 标量（Weyl scalars）逐一表达为 1+1+2 分解下的标量、矢量与张量变量，构建两种形式体系之间的直接“词典”。

Result: 建立了完整的对应字典，并给出了 Newman–Penrose 量在协变定义的 1+1+2 变量下的几何解释；进而以局部旋转对称（locally rotationally symmetric）II 类时空为例，推导了用 Newman–Penrose 标量和宇宙学常数表达的未来外陷获视界（future outer trapping horizon）存在的必要条件。

Conclusion: 该对应关系为两种形式体系的互译提供了系统框架，并为在 1+1+2 形式下利用 Newman–Penrose 标量研究陷获视界等几何结构铺平了道路。

Abstract: In this letter, we establish a complete correspondence between the Newman--Penrose and 1+1+2 semitetrad covariant formalisms by expressing all Newman--Penrose spin coefficients, Ricci scalars, and Weyl scalars in terms of the scalar, vector, and tensor variables of the 1+1+2 decomposition. This provides a direct dictionary between two widely used approaches to general relativity and gives a geometrical interpretation of Newman--Penrose quantities in terms of covariantly defined 1+1+2 variables. As an application, we derive necessary conditions for the existence of future outer trapping horizons in locally rotationally symmetric class II spacetimes, expressed in terms of the Ricci and Weyl Newman--Penrose scalars and the cosmological constant.

### [32] [Carr criterion and mass gaps in non-singular primordial black hole formation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30340)
*Jens Boos,Arif Kağan Gündoğdu,Marek Hartenfels*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文推导了含有引力调节子（gravitational regulator $\ell$）的有效弗里德曼方程（effective Friedmann equations），发现该调节子会在原初黑洞（primordial black hole）质量谱中诱导出一个质量间隙（mass gap），低于该质量的黑洞无法形成；该质量间隙的标度由调节子决定，并导致了一个更强的卡儿判据（Carr criterion），从而直接将原初黑洞丰度与引力调节子的存在联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非奇异引力理论（non-singular gravitational theories）在早期宇宙中具有重要意义，但其对原初黑洞形成过程的具体影响尚不清楚。本文旨在探索引力调节子如何改变原初黑洞的形成条件。

Method: 作者推导了一组描述物质壳层（matter shells）动力学的有效弗里德曼方程，其中引入了引力调节子 $\ell$；通过分析该调节子对方程的影响，得到了原初黑洞质量间隙的存在条件及其标度关系，并进一步推导了修正后的卡儿判据。

Result: 引力调节子会在原初黑洞质量谱中诱导出一个质量间隙 $M_\text{gap}(\ell, R_H)$，低于该质量的黑洞无法形成，其数量级为 $\sim c^2\ell/G$；在物态方程参数 $\omega=0\dots1/3$ 的广泛范围内，该质量间隙给出一个形式为 $\delta_H > 2G M_\text{gap}/R_H - 1$ 的卡儿判据；当视界大小与调节子同量级（$R_H\sim\ell$）时，该新判据强于传统的卡儿判据。

Conclusion: 该工作将原初黑洞的丰度与引力调节子的存在直接联系起来，为非奇异引力理论在早期宇宙中的应用提供了可检验的预言。

Abstract: Non-singular gravitational theories are expected to be relevant in the early universe. In this paper, we derive a set of effective Friedmann equations describing the dynamics of matter shells in the presence of a gravitational regulator $\ell$. We find that such a regulator induces a primordial black hole mass gap such that below a certain mass $M_\text{gap}(\ell, R_H)$ no black holes can form. The order of magnitude of this mass gap is set by the regulator $\sim c^2\ell/G$, with subleading dependence on the horizon radius at time of formation $R_H$. Finally, we show that over a wide range of equation of state parameters $ω= 0 \dots 1/3$, the mass gap implies a Carr criterion of the form $δ_H > 2G M_\text{gap}/R_H - 1$. If the horizon size is of the same order of the regulator, $R_H \sim \ell$, this new criterion is stronger than the traditional Carr criterion for primordial black hole formation. This connects the primordial black hole abundance directly to the presence of gravitational regulators.
