### [33] [Order-disorder trade-off in dirty quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28949)
*Jinmin Yi,Chong Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文证明了一维量子自旋系统中序参量（order parameter）与无序参量（disorder parameter）之间的权衡定理（trade-off theorem）。在具有精确伊辛对称性（Ising symmetry）和平均平移对称性（average translation symmetry）的无序系综中，任何带隙系综必须且仅能拥有一个$O(1)$的爱德沃兹-安德森型（Edwards-Anderson type）序参量或一个偶宇称的$O(1)$无序参量。该结果可推广至包含格里菲斯型（Griffiths-type）稀罕区域效应的近带隙系综，并应用于SPT相的弦序参量、Lieb-Schultz-Mattis型约束以及无序费米子链的拓扑相分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 淬火无序（quenched disorder）对量子多体系统的影响长期依赖微扰方法，缺乏一套严格的、非微扰的理论框架。本文旨在建立序参量与无序参量之间的严格权衡关系，从而系统性地理解无序效应，为超越微扰方法提供严谨工具。

Method: 采用严格的数学证明方法，在一维量子自旋系统中考虑具有精确伊辛对称性和平均平移对称性的无序系综。通过定义并分析$O(1)$的爱德沃兹-安德森型序参量与偶宇称无序参量，证明二者不能同时存在或同时为零的权衡定理，并将结论推广至允许格里菲斯型稀罕区域效应的近带隙系综。

Result: (1) 证明对于严格带隙系综，必须且只能拥有一个$O(1)$的序参量或一个偶宇称的$O(1)$无序参量；(2) 该权衡关系在近带隙系综中同样成立；(3) 成功应用于建立SPT相的弦序参量存在性、导出无序系综的Lieb-Schultz-Mattis型约束（要求近带隙系综自发破缺对称性），以及揭示无序费米子链中的权衡关系，改进了对“内在无序”拓扑相的理解。

Conclusion: 本文提供的权衡定理为理解淬火无序效应建立了一个强大且严格的非微扰框架，不仅在伊辛型自旋系统中获得普适性结论，还成功推广至SPT相、费米子链等更广泛的体系，为无序拓扑相的研究提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: We prove a trade-off theorem for order and disorder parameters in one-dimensional quantum spin systems with quenched disorder. For a disordered ensemble with exact Ising symmetry and average translation symmetry, any gapped ensemble must have one and only one of the following: an $O(1)$ order parameter or an $O(1)$ disorder parameter with even parity, both of the Edwards-Anderson type. The result extends to nearly gapped ensembles that accommodate Griffiths-type rare-region effects. These results offer a powerful and rigorous framework to understand the disorder effects beyond perturbative approaches. As applications, we (1) establish the existence of string order parameters for SPT phases; (2) derive a Lieb-Schultz-Mattis-type constraint for disordered ensembles, which requires a nearly gapped ensemble to spontaneously break the symmetry; and (3) discuss similar trade-off relations for disordered fermion chains, leading to an improved understanding of certain "intrinsically disordered" topological phases.

</details>


### [34] [Geometry and localization: Probing Localization Landscape Theory on the Bethe Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29745)
*Lorenzo Tonetti,Leticia F. Cugliandolo,Marco Tarzia*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文在Bethe格点上对局域化景观理论（LLT）与安德森局域化（Anderson localization）进行了精确解析比较，发现二者相变行为截然不同：LLT渗流跃迁属于标准平均场（mean-field）普适类，而安德森跃迁表现出非传统临界行为。尽管如此，LLT仍能准确再现极低无序区域的若干精确结果，包括孤立本征值位置、最小无序阈值以及Aizenman–Warzel下界。论文还分析了LLT对态密度的预测，并通过极值分析（extreme-value analysis）表明LLT高估了连续谱边界附近的尾态幅度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局域化景观理论（LLT）通过有效限制势（effective confining potential）为理解安德森局域化提供了经典类比，其渗流阈值被认为是迁移率边（mobility edge）的标志。尽管该对应在三维体系中数值吻合惊人，但其理论基础仍是一个开放问题。本研究旨在通过Bethe格点上可精确求解的设定，澄清LLT与安德森局域化之间的理论关系。

Method: 本研究将LLT的分析推广到Bethe格点（Bethe lattice）上，在该设定中安德森局域化转变与LLT渗流问题均存在精确解。通过比较两个相变的临界行为及普适类归属，系统分析了LLT框架的预测能力，包括能量偏移对渗流阈值的影响、态密度（Density of States）的LLT预测，以及控制变量的统计性质。此外，还运用极值分析（extreme-value analysis）检验了LLT对态密度尾部行为的预测。

Result: 分析表明，LLT渗流跃迁与安德森局域化转变是两种不同的相变，临界行为截然不同：LLT渗流属于标准平均场（mean-field）普适类，而Bethe格点上的安德森跃迁表现出非传统临界行为。LLT框架能精确再现极低无序区域的若干结果，包括孤立本征值位置、最小无序阈值及Aizenman–Warzel下界。极值分析显示，LLT对态密度的预测高估了连续谱边界附近的尾态幅度。

Conclusion: 这些发现提供了精确的解析基准，证明尽管LLT具有几何上的直观吸引力，它通常无法再现安德森局域化的量子临界性质，但仍然是理解其极低无序区域的强有力工具。LLT在极低无序区域的有效性与其在临界点附近的偏差并存，表明该理论的应用范围存在明确边界。

Abstract: The Localization Landscape Theory (LLT) offers a classical analogy for understanding Anderson localization through an effective confining potential, whose percolation threshold has been proposed to mark the mobility edge. While this correspondence shows striking numerical agreement in three dimensions, its theoretical foundations remain an open question. In this work, we extend the analysis of the LLT on the Bethe lattice presented in~\cite{Tonetti2026}. In this setting in both the Anderson localization transition and the LLT percolation problem admit exact solutions. Our analysis reveals that the two transitions are distinct, with markedly different critical behaviors. Notably, the LLT percolation transition falls into the standard mean-field universality class, in sharp contrast with the unconventional critical behavior of the Anderson transition on the Bethe lattice. Nonetheless, the LLT framework reproduces several exact results, capturing nontrivial features of the very low-disorder regime: it predicts the position of the isolated eigenvalue, the minimal disorder at which both the LLT percolation curve and the mobility edge first appear, and the Aizenman--Warzel lower bound for localization. We also study the dependence of the LLT percolation threshold on the energy shift, evaluate the LLT prediction for the Density of States, and derive several results on the statistical properties of the variables controlling the problem. Finally, we develop an extreme-value analysis showing that the LLT prediction for the Density of States overestimates the amplitude of the tails close to the boundary of the continuous spectrum. These findings provide an exact analytical benchmark showing that, despite its geometric appeal, the LLT does not generally reproduce the quantum critical properties of Anderson localization, while still offering a powerful tool to understand its very low-disorder regime.

</details>


### [35] [Enhanced Density Fluctuations Near a Disordered Chiral Topological Transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29871)
*Hai-Tao Ding,Sen Mu,Leong-Chuan Kwek,Gabriel Lemarié,Jiangbin Gong*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本研究通过受手征性（chirality）保护的Su-Schrieffer-Heeger链模型，发现无序驱动的拓扑相变（topological phase transition）会增强局域量子态密度对数值涨落的标度指数，并利用能分辨态密度与局域化长度对此行为进行了解释，从而建立波包涨落统计作为无序手征拓扑相变动力学诊断方法的框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局域量子态的密度涨落统计为探究维度、相干性、对称性和无序（disorder）对量子输运的影响提供了新机遇，但拓扑相变（topological phase transition）在该涨落统计中的作用尚未被研究。

Method: 采用受off-diagonal无序（非对角无序）扰动的Su-Schrieffer-Heeger链模型（手征对称性（chiral symmetry）得以保留），数值研究无序驱动的拓扑相变如何影响对数波包密度 $\ln P(r)$ 在距初始激发点距离 $r$ 处的空间涨落。

Result: 远离相变时，拓扑相与平庸局域相中标准偏差均遵循常规一维标度关系 $σ[\ln P(r)]\sim r^θ$ 且 $θ\simeq 1/2$；近相变区域涨落增长增强，拟合指数 $θ$ 呈非单调上升至高于 $1/2$，在临界点处回降至接近 $1/2$。该行为源于相变附近多个能段均携带可观谱权重并表现出竞争性衰减速率，使单一局域化尺度无法主导波包尾部，从而增强 $\ln P(r)$ 的涨落。

Conclusion: 波包涨落统计可作为无序手征拓扑相变（disordered chiral topological transition）的动力学诊断工具，并激励对无序拓扑量子系统中涨落现象的广泛研究。

Abstract: The universal statistics of density fluctuations of localized quantum states may offer unprecedented opportunities to probe and understand quantum transport in connection with dimensionality, coherence, symmetry and disorder. To date, the possible role of topological phase transitions in the fluctuation statistics is not studied yet. Using a Su-Schrieffer-Heeger chain subject to off-diagonal disorder (so that chiral symmetry is preserved), this work investigates how a disorder driven topological phase transition impacts on the spatial fluctuations of the logarithmic wave-packet density $\ln P(r)$ at distance $r$ from the initial excitation. Away from the transition, in both topological and trivial localized phases, the standard deviation follows the conventional one-dimensional scaling $σ[\ln P(r)]\sim r^θ$ with $θ\simeq 1/2$. Near the transition, however, the fluctuation growth is enhanced: the fitted exponent $θ$ increases above $1/2$ in a nonmonotonic manner before returning close to $1/2$ at criticality. We interpret this behavior from the energy-resolved density of states and localization length. Near the transition, several energy sectors carry appreciable spectral weight and exhibit competitive decay rates, preventing a single localization scale from dominating the accessible wave-packet tail and thereby enhancing the fluctuations of $\ln P(r)$. Our results establish wave-packet fluctuation statistics as a dynamical diagnostic of disordered chiral topological transitions and motivate broader studies of fluctuation phenomena in disordered topological quantum systems.

</details>


### [36] [Estimates of ground state energies for the quantum SK and 2D-EA model, using deGennes-Suzuki-Kubo mean-field annealing dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29875)
*Soumyaditya Das,Soumyajyoti Biswas,Bikas K. Chakrabarti*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 通过大规模（N=40000）量子退火（quantum annealing）模拟，利用deGennes-Suzuki-Kubo平均场伊辛动力学（Ising dynamics）求解Sherrington-Kirkpatrick自旋玻璃（spin glass）的基态能量（ground state energy），并扩展至Edwards-Anderson自旋玻璃在方格晶格上的研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在前期工作（Eur. Phys. J. B 98, 226 (2025)）基础上，进一步扩大系统规模至N=40000，以更准确地估计Sherrington-Kirkpatrick自旋玻璃的基态能量。

Method: 数值求解deGennes-Suzuki-Kubo退火动力学（annealing dynamics），从量子顺磁态（quantum paramagnetic state）出发，在退火过程结束时获得自旋构型（spin configurations），进而估计对应系统尺寸下的基态能量；该方法整体算法复杂度为O(N³)。

Result: 该方法展现出高效率，能以O(N³)的算法代价估计Sherrington-Kirkpatrick自旋玻璃的基态能量；并将该方法扩展至方格晶格上的Edwards-Anderson自旋玻璃。

Conclusion: 研究表明，基于deGennes-Suzuki-Kubo平均场伊辛动力学的量子退火模拟在大规模自旋玻璃系统中具有高效性和可扩展性，能够应用于不同类型的自旋玻璃模型。

Abstract: We perform a large scale simulation of quantum annealing in the Sherrington-Kirkpatrick (SK) spin glass up to a system size $N=40000$ to estimate its ground state energy using the deGennes-Suzuki-Kubo mean-field Ising dynamics, extending the earlier results (reported in Eur. Phys. J. B {\bf 98}, 226 (2025)). Here we numerically solve the deGennes-Suzuki-Kubo annealing dynamics to obtain the spin configurations and subsequently the ground state energy for a given system size at the end of the annealing (to the desired quantum system at the corresponding values of the transverse field), starting from a quantum paramagnetic state. The method shows high efficiency, with an overall algorithmic cost of $O(N^3)$ in estimating the energy of the ground state. We later extend this method to study the ground state energy of the Edwards-Anderson (EA) spin glass on a square lattice.

</details>

### [37] [Quantum Light Nano-Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28987)
*Michael Dapolito,Matthew Fu,Fuyang Tay,Suheng Xu,Yuchen Lin,Neil Hazra,Adam K. Williams,Samuel L. Moore,Rocco A. Vitalone,Jonas Kolker,Thomas Cherradi,Aaron Holman,Thomas P. Darlington,Mark E. Ziffer,Xavier Roy,Sebastian Will,Cory R. Dean,Mengkun Liu,A. J. Millis,Abhay N. Pasupathy,P. J. Schuck,D. N. Basov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种量子光散射型扫描近场光学显微镜（q-SNOM），能够在衍射极限以下的尺度探测固体中的量子效应，首次实现了对单个光-物质混合准粒子（hybrid light-matter quasiparticles）自干涉的实空间成像，并利用纠缠光子（entangled photons）的时间关联实现飞秒级准粒子传播动力学观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子纠缠和量子关联（quantum correlations）是量子材料物理的核心，但在实验上极难探测。在固体中探测这些现象需要能够在材料激发本征长度和时间尺度上工作的量子光学探针（quantum optical probes），且必须突破光的衍射极限（diffraction limit），而现有量子光源强度极弱且近场光-物质相互作用效率极低，使相关工具开发此前不可行。

Method: 本文通过克服上述挑战，开发了一种量子光散射型扫描近场光学显微镜（q-SNOM），在衍射极限以下的长度尺度上探索固态量子效应。具体包括利用该显微镜实现单混合光-物质准粒子的自干涉（self-interference）实空间成像，并引入了一种极化激元飞行时间计量术（polaritonic time-of-flight metrology），利用纠缠光子（entangled photons）之间的时间关联来观测准粒子传播动力学。

Result: 首次在实空间中对范德瓦尔斯半导体（van der Waals semiconductor）中的单个混合光-物质准粒子自干涉进行了成像，实现了波粒二象性（wave-particle duality）的纳米尺度直接可视化。同时，利用极化激元飞行时间计量术，以飞秒（femtosecond）时间分辨率观测了准粒子的传播动力学。

Conclusion: 该工作为在纳米尺度上探索和控制材料中的量子效应奠定了基础。

Abstract: Entanglement and quantum correlations are central to the physics of quantum materials, yet they have remained notoriously difficult to probe experimentally. Probing these phenomena in solids requires quantum optical probes that operate at the native length and time scales of material excitations, below the diffraction limit of light. Developing the requisite tools has previously been infeasible due to the extremely weak intensities of state-of-the-art quantum light sources and extreme inefficiency of near-field light-matter interactions. In this work, we circumvent these challenges and develop a quantum light scattering-type scanning near-field optical microscope (q-SNOM) that can explore the broad domain of solid-state quantum effects at length scales below the diffraction limit. In its first application, we image in real space the self-interference of single hybrid light-matter quasiparticles in a van der Waals semiconductor, providing a direct nanoscale visualization of the wave-particle duality. We also introduce a polaritonic time-of-flight metrology that exploits the temporal correlations among entangled photons to observe the quasiparticle propagation dynamics with femtosecond resolution. This work sets the stage for nanoscale exploration and control of quantum effects in materials.

</details>


### [38] [Reinterpreting Memory Effects in Nonequilibrium Systems: From Temporal Dynamics to Steady-State Signatures via NEGF](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28993)
*Pragya Chaudhary*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在非平衡格林函数（NEGF）和Schwinger-Keldysh非平衡量子场论框架下，系统研究了二维晶格系统中的记忆效应与量子输运，发现静态无序导致马尔可夫（Markovian）动力学，而电子-声子耦合产生非马尔可夫（Non-Markovian）行为，并探讨了谱函数作为非平衡记忆效应诊断探针的可能性，以及1PI和2PI有效作用的粗粒化行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解二维晶格系统中散射机制与记忆效应之间的内在联系，以及它们如何影响非平衡量子输运过程，特别是在低维体系中的动态行为特征。

Method: 基于二维紧束缚哈密顿量（tight-binding Hamiltonian），在Keldysh contour上应用Dyson展开，采用二阶Born近似（second-order Born approximation）和自洽Born近似（self-consistent Born Approximation）推导弹性与非弹性散射相关的电子自能；进一步分析1PI和2PI有效作用（effective actions）的粗粒化行为。

Result: 静态无序产生局域自能和快速衰减的记忆核，表现为马尔可夫动力学；电子-声子耦合则产生时间非局域自能和真正的非马尔可夫行为。这些记忆特征直接反映在谱函数中。不同微观哈密顿量（Hofstadter模型和RKKY耦合系统）对马尔可夫与非马尔可夫性质有显著影响。

Conclusion: 散射机制、记忆效应与量子输运之间在低维系统中存在统一的理论联系；谱函数可作为非平衡记忆效应的有效诊断探针。

Abstract: We investigate memory effects and quantum transport in two-dimensional lattice systems within the framework of non-equilibrium Green's functions and Schwinger-Keldysh non-equilibrium quantum field theory. Starting from a 2D tight-binding Hamiltonian, we employ the Dyson expansion on the Keldysh contour and the second-order Born and self-consistent Born Approximation to derive the electronic self-energies associated with elastic and inelastic scattering mechanisms.Static disorder produces a local self-energy and a rapidly decaying memory kernel, characteristic of Markovian dynamics, whereas electron-phonon coupling generates temporally nonlocal self-energies and genuine Non-Markovian behavior. We demonstrate that these distinct memory signatures are directly reflected in the spectral function, which we propose as a diagnostic probe of non-equilibrium memory effects. Further we explore 1PI and 2PI effective actions to see their memory perspectives studying their coarse-graining behavior. Building on this theoretical framework, we further apply the conventional NEGF formalism to two paradigmatic two-dimensional models-the Hofstadter and an RKKY-coupled system to explore how different microscopic Hamiltonians influence Markovian and Non-Markovian nature. Our results provide a unified connection between scattering mechanisms, memory effects, and quantum transport in low-dimensional systems.

</details>


### [39] [Measuring anyon dispersion with tunneling probes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29017)
*Taige Wang,T. Senthil*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出两种隧穿探针技术——扫描隧道谱学（scanning tunneling spectroscopy）和量子扭转显微术（quantum twisting microscopy）——可用于测量分数量子霍尔效应的晶格模型（如分数量子陈绝缘体）中任意子（anyon）的色散关系（dispersion），从而区分紧致电子型激发、束缚任意子分子与自由任意子连续谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在分数陈绝缘体（fractional Chern insulator, FCI）等晶格系统中，任意子不仅是拓扑激发，也是可移动的准粒子，其运动决定了掺杂稀薄任意子气体的基态性质（如可能的超导态），但现有手段难以直接测量任意子的色散关系。

Method: 利用扫描隧道谱学中弱无序产生的空间振荡准粒子干涉图案（quasiparticle-interference pattern），分析其分支结构以提取分数化成分的色散；利用量子扭转显微术中平面动量守恒隧穿选择注入电子的总动量，通过分数化电子谱的连续阈值反推任意子的色散。

Result: 两种隧穿探针均可区分三种激发类型：紧致电子型激发（compact electron-like excitation）、束缚任意子分子（bound anyon molecule）以及自由任意子连续谱（unbound anyon continuum）。

Conclusion: 隧穿探针为测量晶格系统中任意子的运动与色散提供了实验可行的方法，为理解掺杂FCI中稀薄任意子气体的基态行为（包括超导态）提供了关键探测手段。

Abstract: Anyons are usually characterized by their topological data and their fractional quantum numbers under global symmetries. In lattice systems such as fractional Chern insulators (FCI), they are also mobile quasiparticles. Their motion controls the possible ground states of the dilute anyon gas obtained by doping an FCI, including possible superconducting states. We show how tunneling probes can measure this motion. In scanning tunneling spectroscopy, weak disorder produces spatially oscillating quasiparticle-interference patterns whose branches reveal the dispersion of fractionalized constituents. In quantum twisting microscopy, planar momentum-conserving tunneling selects the total momentum of the injected electron, so the continuum thresholds of fractionalized electron spectra encode the dispersion of the constituent anyons. The resulting spectra distinguish compact electron-like excitations, bound anyon molecules, and unbound anyon continuum.

</details>


### [40] [Critical states and anomalous wave transport in an aperiodic polariton monotile](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29023)
*Valtýr Kári Daníelsson,Helgi Sigurðsson*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了“帽子”（the Hat）单一瓷砖（Monotile）准晶格中的二维波输运、横向局域化与量子模式标度性质。通过可重构光学晶格中的腔极化激元（cavity-polaritons）系统，直接对角化薛定谔方程证实了局域态与临界态的存在。波函数分布矩的标度分析揭示了与Monotile希尔伯特空间分形结构相关的异常输运行为（超扩散与近亚扩散），并提出了利用共振激发极化激元流体验证理论预测的实验策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最近“帽子”单瓷砖被引入非周期拼砌（aperiodic tilings）与准晶家族，这类材料展现出位于有序与无序系统边界的物理性质。本文旨在系统研究该新型非周期拼砌结构中的量子波输运与局域化特性。

Method: 基于可重构光学晶格中的腔极化激元系统，通过直接对角化薛定谔方程确认Monotile准晶格中的局域态与临界态；利用波函数分布矩的标度分析（scaling analysis）表征输运行为。

Result: 证实了Monotile准晶格中存在局域态（localized states）与临界态（critical states）。标度分析揭示了与Monotile希尔伯特空间分形结构相关的异常输运机制：超扩散（super-diffusive）与近亚扩散（near sub-diffusive）极化激元输运。

Conclusion: 提出利用共振激发极化激元流体的实验策略来验证上述理论发现，为研究非周期拼砌体系中的波动力学与强非线性现象提供了新途径。

Abstract: Recently "the Hat" monotile was introduced into the family of aperiodic tilings and quasicrystals boasting physical properties lying at the boundary of ordered and disordered systems. Here we study the two-dimensional wave transport, transverse localization and scaling properties of the quantum modes in a Monotile quasilattice. Our system is based on reconfigurable optical lattices for cavity-polaritons which provide flexible means to study wavepacket dynamics, strong nonlinear phenomena, and power-driven condensation in this new type of an aperiodic tiling. We confirm the existence of localized and critical states in the Monotile through direct diagonalization of the Schrödinger equation. Scaling analysis on the moments of the wavefunction distribution reveals anomalous transport regimes of super-diffusive and near sub-diffusive polariton transport associated with the fractal structure of the Monotile Hilbert space. We propose a strategy using resonantly excited polariton fluids to verify our findings.

### [41] [Long-Range Fermi-Polaron Blockade in Monolayer MoSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29067)
*Jonas Peterson,Shibalik Lahiri,Monique Tie,Shibin Deng,Jierong Wang,Minxue Wang,Luke Holtzman,James Hone,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Tony Heinz,Valentin Walther,Libai Huang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过飞秒泵浦-探测瞬态吸收显微镜直接成像单层MoSe₂中激子-费米极化激元（exciton-Fermi polarons）的空间分辨非线性光学响应，观察到吸引性费米极化激元共振吸收的显著空间抑制，并提取出比中性激子大十倍以上的光学阻断半径。微观分析表明这种扩展非线性主要源于费米子介导的激子-费米极化激元间相互作用。该结果确立了二维半导体中激子-费米极化激元作为电可调、强相互作用的准粒子，是实现超低功耗非线性光电器件的理想平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 少光子层次的强光学非线性（strong optical nonlinearities）是量子光子学（quantum photonics）的核心目标，但在固态体系中难以实现。本文旨在探索掺杂二维半导体中激子-费米极化激元这一多体准粒子的非线性光学响应，以寻找实现强相互作用的可调光学准粒子平台。

Method: 采用飞秒泵浦-探测瞬态吸收显微镜（femtosecond pump-probe transient absorption microscopy）技术，直接对单层MoSe₂中激子-费米极化激元（exciton-Fermi polarons）的空间分辨非线性光学响应进行成像。

Result: 观察到吸引性费米极化激元（attractive Fermi polaron）的共振吸收存在显著的空间抑制，从中提取出的光学阻断半径比中性激子大十倍以上。微观分析表明，这种扩展的非线性主要源自费米子介导的激子-费米极化激元间相互作用。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了二维半导体中的激子-费米极化激元作为电可调、强相互作用的准粒子，并指出其是实现超低功耗非线性光电器件（ultralow-power nonlinear optical devices）的有前景平台。

Abstract: Strong optical nonlinearities at the few-photon level are a central goal for quantum photonics, yet they remain difficult to realize in solid-state systems. In doped two-dimensional semiconductors, coupling between excitons and a degenerate Fermi sea gives rise to exciton-Fermi polarons, many-body quasiparticles whose optical response is governed by fermionic correlations. Here, using femtosecond pump-probe transient absorption microscopy, we directly image the spatially resolved nonlinear optical response of exciton-Fermi polarons in monolayer MoSe$_2$. We observe a pronounced spatial suppression of resonant absorption associated with the attractive Fermi polaron, from which we extract an optical blockade radius that is more than ten times larger than that of the neutral exciton. Microscopic analysis indicates that this extended nonlinearity arises primarily from fermion-mediated interactions between exciton-Fermi polarons. Our results establish exciton-Fermi polarons in two-dimensional semiconductors as electrically tunable, strongly interacting optical quasiparticles, and identify them as a promising platform for ultralow-power nonlinear optical devices.

</details>


### [42] [Nanoparticle manipulation with a carbon fiber tip in an electron microscope for $μ$-SQUID magnetometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29550)
*Umesh Chandra Thuwal,Sumanta Maity,Clemens B. Winkelmann,Hervé Courtois,Anjan Kumar Gupta*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种集成于扫描电子显微镜中的碳纤维尖端纳米操纵系统，能够以约100 nm的精度在表面上对单个纳米颗粒（约100 nm）进行可靠定位，并通过在超导量子干涉器件上精确放置Fe₃O₄磁性纳米颗粒，验证了其用于优化磁耦合与探测单颗粒磁性的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在表面上对单个纳米颗粒进行精确操纵与定位，是研究其物理性质（如磁学特性）的关键需求。然而，传统操纵手段在精度、灵活性以及减少粘附力方面仍面临限制，因此需要开发一种高刚性、低粘附、亚微米级精度的可靠操纵系统。

Method: 该系统采用电化学刻蚀制备的非晶碳纤维尖端（amorphous carbon fiber tip），具备优异的机械刚性和亚100 nm的尖端半径，有效降低了范德华粘附力（van der Waals adhesion）。系统结构包括用于垂直运动的压电双晶片（piezoelectric bimorph）、用于二维精细控制的四象限压电管（four-quadrant piezo-tube），以及用于粗调横向移动的二维压电步进器（two-dimensional piezoelectric walker），并集成于扫描电子显微镜中实现实时观测。

Result: 实现了对约100 nm尺寸的纳米颗粒（NP）以约100 nm的精度进行可靠定位。成功将单个Fe₃O₄磁性纳米颗粒精确放置于微米级超导量子干涉器件（superconducting quantum interference device, SQUID）上，实现了二者之间的最优磁耦合，并进一步探测了单个纳米颗粒的磁学性质。

Conclusion: 该碳纤维尖端基纳米操纵系统为在表面上精确操控单个纳米颗粒提供了一种有效技术方案，尤其适用于在微纳器件上定向组装纳米材料以实现功能耦合与物性探测，展示了在单纳米颗粒磁学测量中的实际应用价值。

Abstract: We report a carbon-fiber-tip based nanomanipulation system integrated into a scanning electron microscope for individual nanoparticle (NP) manipulation on a surface. Electrochemically etched amorphous carbon fiber tips with excellent mechanical rigidity and sub-100 nm apex radii effectively reduce the van der Waals adhesion and enable reliable positioning of about 100 nm size NPs with about 100 nm precision. This system combines a piezoelectric bimorph for vertical tip motion, a four-quadrant piezo-tube for two-dimensional fine tip control and a two-dimensional piezoelectric walker for coarse lateral translation. Using this setup, we successfully position single Fe$_3$O$_4$ magnetic NPs on micron sized superconducting quantum interference devices for optimal magnetic coupling between them and probe a NP's magnetism.

</details>


### [43] [Revealing quantum metric multipoles in magnetic topological insulator MnBi2Te4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29595)
*Lars Sjöström,Prasanna Rout,Shahid Sattar,Alexander Tyner,Maurice E. Bal,Ankit Khola,Elias Rasmussen,Khadiza Ali,Arumugum Thamizhavel,Uli Zeitler,Carlo M. Canali,Saroj P. Dash*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在多层磁性拓扑绝缘体MnBi₂Te₄中观测到高达七阶谐波的非线性电子输运现象，发现奇阶分量主导而偶阶分量被抑制的奇偶行为，并通过标度分析和理论计算将量子度量多极子（quantum metric multipoles）和非线性Drude电导率（nonlinear Drude conductivities）识别为非线性输运的微观起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性电子输运（nonlinear electronic transport）已成为探测拓扑量子材料中量子几何（quantum geometry）的有力手段，但高阶输运（higher-order transport）此前主要停留在实验不可及的状态，限制了量子几何更精细特征的探索。

Method: 在多层磁性拓扑绝缘体（magnetic topological insulator）MnBi₂Te₄中进行非线性电子输运实验测量；结合温度与磁场依赖测量分析非线性输运与磁相（magnetic phases）的关联；采用标度分析（scaling analysis）与理论计算手段。

Result: 观测到高达第七谐波阶次（seventh harmonic order）的高阶非线性电子输运；发现奇阶非线性输运分量主导、偶阶分量被抑制的奇偶行为（even-odd behavior）；非线性输运与MnBi₂Te₄的磁相之间存在强关联。

Conclusion: 量子度量多极子和非线性Drude电导率被识别为所观测非线性输运现象的微观起源（microscopic origins）。

Abstract: Nonlinear electronic transport has emerged as a powerful probe of the quantum geometry in topological quantum materials, where the band topology and broken symmetries facilitate power law current voltage responses beyond Ohms law. While nonlinear transport of the second and third orders has been studied in several quantum materials, higher-order transport has so far mainly remained experimentally inaccessible, leaving more detailed features of the quantum geometry unexplored. Here, we observe higher order nonlinear electronic transport up to the seventh harmonic order in multilayer magnetic topological insulator MnBi2Te4. We find an even-odd behavior where the odd order nonlinear transport components dominate while the even-order ones are suppressed. Temperature and magnetic field dependent measurements show a strong correlation between the nonlinear transport and the magnetic phases of MnBi2Te4. Through scaling analysis and theoretical calculations, quantum metric multipoles and nonlinear Drude conductivities are identified as the microscopic origins of the nonlinear transport.

### [44] [Disentangling Spin Pumping and Two-Magnon Scattering Contributions to Gilbert Damping in YIG/V Bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29597)
*S. Elkady,A. Tlais,H. Reslan,S. Isber,M. Haidar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过宽带铁磁共振（broadband ferromagnetic resonance, FMR）测量，研究了基于钇铁石榴石（YIG）/钒（V）双层膜中的磁阻尼和自旋泵浦（spin pumping）响应，发现双磁子散射（two-magnon scattering, TMS）在纳米尺度阻尼中占主导作用，并在分离该贡献后提取了厚度无关的有效自旋混合电导（effective spin-mixing conductance）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在铁磁/重金属（FM/HM）双层膜体系中，准确分离自旋泵浦与其它弛豫机制（如双磁子散射）对正确提取自旋输运参数至关重要，但此前对YIG/V体系中双磁子散射的主导作用缺乏系统研究。

Method: 采用宽带铁磁共振测量，以YIG厚度为变量，对YIG/V双层膜进行系统表征；应用同时考虑自旋泵浦和双磁子散射贡献的厚度依赖阻尼模型，分离不同的弛豫贡献。

Result: YIG/V双层膜中Gilbert阻尼的表观增强不能仅归因于自旋泵浦；双磁子散射在纳米厚度范围内主导阻尼的厚度依赖性。忽略双磁子散射会导致自旋泵浦贡献被高估，进而得到不合理的有效自旋混合电导值。分离内在自旋泵浦贡献后，提取出的有效自旋混合电导为厚度无关的 $g^{\uparrow\downarrow}_{\mathrm{eff}} = 1.33 \times 10^{18}~\mathrm{m^{-2}}$。

Conclusion: 该研究为FM/HM体系中自旋输运参数的量化提供了更精确的分析框架，强调在解释自旋泵浦和逆自旋霍尔效应（inverse spin Hall effect, ISHE）实验时必须考虑本征阻尼机制之外的散射贡献。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the magnetic damping and spin pumping response of YIG-based bilayers incorporating vanadium (V) as the normal metal layer via broadband ferromagnetic resonance (FMR) measurements as a function of YIG thickness. We show that the apparent enhancement of the Gilbert damping in YIG/V bilayers cannot be solely attributed to spin pumping. Instead, two-magnon scattering (TMS) plays a dominant role in governing the thickness dependence of the damping in the nanometer regime. By applying a thickness-dependent damping model that accounts for both spin pumping and two-magnon scattering contributions, we successfully disentangle the different relaxation contributions. Our analysis reveals that neglecting two-magnon scattering leads to an overestimation of the spin-pumping contribution and consequently to unphysically large values of the effective spin-mixing conductance. After isolating the intrinsic spin pumping contribution, we extract a thickness-independent effective spin-mixing conductance of $g^{\uparrow\downarrow}_{\mathrm{eff}} = 1.33 \times 10^{18}~\mathrm{m^{-2}}$. These findings provide a more accurate framework for quantifying spin transport parameters in FM/HM systems and emphasize the necessity of accounting for extrinsic damping mechanisms when interpreting spin pumping and inverse spin Hall effect experiments.

</details>


### [45] [Generation of Bloch Points with Controlled Spin Texture Using Geometrical Boundary Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29672)
*Naëmi Leo,Daniel Wolf,Alicia Estela Herguedas Alonso,Oleksandr Zaiets,Jakub Jurczyk,Takeaki Gokita,John Fullerton,Dedalo Sanz-Hernandez,Claire Donnelly,Andrea Sorrentino,Eva Pereiro,Lucia Aballe,Peter Fischer,Rachid Belkhou,Claas Abert,Dieter Suess,Axel Lubk,Aurelio Hierro-Rodriguez,Amalio Fernández-Pacheco*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过设计三维纳米磁体中的几何边界条件，在具有相反手性的双螺旋纳米线之间的手性界面处，实现了对布洛赫点（Bloch point）自旋织构（spin texture）的确定性控制。该方法能够生成具有确定极性（polarity）、环量（circulation）和螺旋性（helicity）的布洛赫点畴壁（Bloch-point domain wall），并通过饱和磁场在界面处成核头对头（head-to-head）或尾对尾（tail-to-tail）的磁畴构型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 布洛赫点是磁化强度场（magnetization field）中三维拓扑奇点（three-dimensional topological singularities），在斯格明子（skyrmion）产生与湮灭等自旋织构拓扑变换中起关键作用。尽管拓扑学通常强制在圆柱纳米线等受限几何结构中存在布洛赫点，但对其位置和磁构型（magnetic configuration）进行确定性控制仍具挑战性。

Method: 通过在两个相反手性的三维双螺旋纳米线之间引入手性界面（chirality interface），形成扭结状非共线结构（kinked, non-collinear structure）。这种几何设计施加了相互竞争的拓扑约束（competing topological constraints），从而唯一地定义了布洛赫点周围的磁化构型。随后施加饱和磁场（saturating magnetic field），在手性界面处成核头对头或尾对尾的磁畴构型。

Result: 该方法生成了具有确定性极性、环量和螺旋性的布洛赫点畴壁，实现了对布洛赫点自旋织构及其与电流诱导奥斯特场（current-induced Oersted fields）选择性耦合的完全三维控制。

Conclusion: 该几何方法实现了对布洛赫点畴壁的完全三维控制，能够确定性地设计其自旋织构，并选择性调控其与电流诱导奥斯特场的耦合，为三维纳米磁体中拓扑自旋织构的操控提供了新途径。

Abstract: Bloch points are three-dimensional topological singularities in magnetization that play a key role in topological transformations of spin textures, such as skyrmion creation or annihilation. While topology often enforces the existence of Bloch points in confined geometries like cylindrical nanowires, deterministic control over their position and magnetic configuration remains challenging. Here we demonstrate the generation of Bloch points with controlled spin texture by engineering geometrical boundary conditions in three-dimensional nanomagnets. By introducing a chirality interface between two three-dimensional double-helix nanowires of opposite handedness, forming a kinked, non-collinear structure, we impose competing topological constraints that uniquely define the magnetization configuration surrounding the Bloch point. A saturating magnetic field nucleates head-to-head or tail-to-tail domain configurations at the chirality interface, producing a Bloch-point domain wall with deterministic polarity, circulation and helicity. This geometrical approach enables full three-dimensional control of Bloch point domain walls allowing deterministic engineering of their spin texture and its selective coupling to current-induced Oersted fields.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用SO(5)赝自旋（pseudo-spin）运动方程，在有效哈密顿量中引入偶极相互作用（dipolar interaction），并通过自洽方法计算基态；实际数值模拟采用26点Lebedev求积法（Lebedev quadrature）观测实时耦合振荡。

Result: 激发出的重希格斯模具有扭角度动量为J=2且投影J_z=0，与已知的轻希格斯模（J=1, J_z=0）发生耦合；数值模拟展示了两种模式的实时耦合振荡行为。

Abstract: Based on equations of motion of an SO(5) pseudo-spin, we demonstrate a quantum quench protocol using the magnetic pulse to excite an $\textit{undamped}$ heavy Higgs boson in the Balian--Werthamer superfluid (or superconductor). To achieve that, it is essential to include the dipolar interaction in the effective Hamiltonian and to calculate the ground state self-consistently. The pumped heavy Higgs mode has the twisted angular momentum $J=2$ with the projection $J^{\,}_z=0$ and couples to a well-known light Higgs mode ($J=1$, $J^{\,}_z=0$). The numerical method of 26-point Lebedev quadrature is implemented concretely so as to observe the real-time coupled oscillation.

### [47] [Thermodynamic and magnetocaloric properties of a triangular spin-1/2 cluster with Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29989)
*Jordana Torrico,Romulo A. Silva,S. M. de Souza,Onofre Rojas*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文基于自旋-1/2海森堡哈密顿量（Heisenberg Hamiltonian）与反对称交换相互作用（Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction），理论研究了三角自旋-1/2团簇的磁学与热力学性质，揭示了铁磁（FM）、亚铁磁（FI）和阻挫（FR）相，分析了磁化曲线、熵、比热及磁卡效应（MCE），并指出DM相互作用增强了MCE的复杂性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用含反对称交换相互作用的自旋-1/2海森堡哈密顿量（Heisenberg Hamiltonian）描述三角团簇，通过求解能谱与基态相图，分析总自旋和DM相互作用（Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction）的影响，并计算磁化率、熵、比热及MCE。

Result: 系统存在铁磁（FM）、亚铁磁（FI）和阻挫（FR）三相；低温下出现特征性的1/3磁化平台（magnetization plateau）；熵与比热展现残余熵（residual entropy）、肖特基型异常（Schottky-type anomaly）及低温相变特征；DM相互作用使MCE呈现直接与逆双重模式，并增强其复杂性。

Conclusion: 阻挫与各向异性在调控三角自旋团簇的MCE中起关键作用，DM相互作用丰富了熵变行为，对Cu₃基分子磁体的设计具有参考价值。

Abstract: We present a theoretical investigation of the magnetic and thermodynamic properties of the triangular spin-1/2 cluster with Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya (DM) interaction, described by a spin-1/2 Heisenberg Hamiltonian with antisymmetric exchange interactions. The energy spectrum and ground-state phase diagram reveal the presence of ferromagnetic (FM), ferrimagnetic (FI), and frustrated (FR) phases, strongly influenced by the total spin and the DM interaction. We analyze magnetization and susceptibility, showing that at low temperatures the system exhibits a characteristic 1/3 magnetization plateau, while thermal fluctuations suppress magnetic order at higher temperatures. The entropy and specific heat display residual entropies due to ground-state degeneracies, Schottky-type anomalies at intermediate temperatures, and additional low-temperature features related to phase transitions. Particular attention is given to the magnetocaloric effect (MCE), characterized by both direct and inverse regimes depending on the magnetic field variation. We find that the DM interaction enhances the complexity of the MCE, leading to nontrivial entropy variations as a function of the magnetic field. These results provide insights into the role of frustration and anisotropy in tuning the MCE of properties triangular spin clusters, with relevance to \mathrm{Cu}_{3}-based molecular magnets.

### [48] [Engineering Quantum Criticality in the Integer Quantum Hall Regime through a Screening Layer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30129)
*C. T. Tai,P. T. Madathil,A. Gupta,L. N. Pfeiffer,K. W. Baldwin,M. Shayegan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过在GaAs双量子阱器件中直接调控层间库仑屏蔽，实验证实了短程电子-电子相互作用下量子霍尔平台-平台相变的动态临界指数z=2（相应临界指数k≈0.22），而长程库仑相互作用下z=1（k≈0.42），首次提供了电子-电子相互作用决定量子霍尔区临界行为的直接实验证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子无序诱导局域化与电子-电子相互作用是凝聚态物理（condensed matter physics）中最基本的问题之一。在二维电子系统中，标度理论（scaling picture）通过一组普适临界指数描述整数量子霍尔平台之间的相变。实验普遍报告临界指数k≈0.42，对应动态临界指数（dynamic exponent）z=1，这与电子具有长程1/r相互作用的理论图像一致；理论同时预测短程电子相互作用下z=2，但一直缺乏实验验证。本文旨在直接探测库仑相互作用对这些相变的影响。

Method: 研究使用限制在GaAs双量子阱器件中的双层电子系统。两层之间距离接近相关磁场下的磁长度（magnetic length）。通过调节顶层电子密度，使其在磁场下进入绝缘相或金属相，从而原位调控底层经历平台-平台相变时的不屏蔽与屏蔽相互作用强度。

Result: 在未屏蔽（unscreened）的长程库仑相互作用条件下，测量得到k≈0.42，与广泛报道的值一致。当引入屏蔽（screening）导致电子相互作用变为短程时，k值降至约0.22，对应z=2。

Conclusion: 实验结果直接证明了电子-电子相互作用在决定量子霍尔区域临界行为中的关键作用，并展示了利用屏蔽效应作为调控量子临界性（quantum criticality）的有效参数。

Abstract: Disorder-induced localization of electrons and electron-electron interaction are among the most fundamental problems in condensed matter physics. In two-dimensional electron systems, extensive studies have led to the emergence of a scaling picture, characterized by a set of universal critical exponents that govern the transitions between the integer quantum Hall plateaus. From the temperature dependence of the plateau-to-plateau transitions, experiments primarily report k ~ 0.42, implying a dynamic exponent z = 1, consistent with a theoretical picture where electrons have a long-range (1/r) interaction. Theory also predicts that z = 2 for short-range electron interaction, but an experimental verification has remained elusive. Here, we directly probe the influence of Coulomb interaction on these transitions using a bilayer electron system confined to a GaAs double quantum well device. The two layers are in close proximity, with an interlayer distance approximately equal to the magnetic length at the relevant magnetic fields. By tuning the electron density in the top layer, we access both insulating and metallic phases of the electrons in this layer as a function of magnetic field, allowing in-situ control of the unscreened and screened interaction strengths in the bottom layer as it goes through its plateau-to-plateau transitions. In the unscreened case, we measure k ~ 0.42 consistent with the widely reported value. More importantly, when screening is introduced, k is reduced to ~ 0.22, implying z = 2. Our results provide direct experimental evidence for the role of electron-electron interaction in determining critical behavior in the quantum Hall regime, and demonstrate screening as a powerful tuning parameter for engineering quantum criticality.

</details>

*Md. Shaikot Alam Shakil,Ting-Hsuan Wu,Xing He,Abu Montakim Tareq,Zhenjia Zhou,Libo Gao,Naihao Chiang,Ding-Shyue Yang*

Result: 实验发现异质结中因范德华（van der Waals, vdW）异质结间的层间电荷转移（interlayer charge transfer）而激发出超快载流子耦合的层内原子运动，该运动在单层中不存在。此外，载流子-声子耦合与声子散射导致不同的能量流动路径，并给出各自的**特征时间**（characteristic times）。在更长的时间尺度上，热化原子运动的弛豫可被热输运模型充分描述。MoS₂/WS₂异质结的**热边界电导**（thermal boundary conductance, TBC）高于单层-基底界面，但不同vdW接触间的TBC数值相近，表明声子耦合强度相当。

Conclusion: 这些结果揭示了垂直堆叠的范德华异质结构（vdW HSs）在光学、声子及界面热性质方面的关键特征，为相关光电器件设计提供了物理依据。

Abstract: Understanding the electronic coupling and energy flow across layered two-dimensional heterostructures (HSs) is crucial to the exploitation of carrier and phonon transports as well as thermal management in next-generation optoelectronic devices. By using reflection ultrafast electron diffraction, we directly examine photoinduced out-of-plane structural dynamics of supported MoS2/WS2 bilayer HSs and their individual monolayers. Experimental evidence reveals the launch of ultrafast carrier-coupled intralayer atomic motions due to interlayer charge transfer across the van der Waals (vdW) heterojunctions that is absent for individual monolayers. Such a notable carrier-lattice correlation is in addition to the electronic coupling manifested in the enhanced optical absorption for HSs. Also, different pathways of energy flow as a result of carrier-phonon coupling and phonon scattering are reported with the corresponding characteristic times. On longer timescales, relaxation of thermalized atomic motions can be sufficiently described by a thermal transport model. A higher thermal boundary conductance (TBC) across MoS2/WS2 HSs is obtained compared to those at the monolayer-substrate interfaces; however, the similar TBC values suggest comparable couplings of phonons across vdW contacts. These results further shed light on the optical, phonon, and interfacial thermal properties of vertically-stacked vdW HSs.

Abstract: A differential phase shift of a low-power spin wave (SW) induced by a high-power pumping wave co-propagating at different frequencies in perpendicularly magnetized magnetic films has been studied. The results show that the induced nonlinear phase shift up to 180° takes place for pumping wave power of a few milliwatts. The phenomenon paves the way for fast and energy-efficient control of one-dimensional magnon transport.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验已在电子掺杂菱面体多层石墨烯中观察到四分之一金属态和零电阻态（被归因于手性超导，chiral superconductor），但其轨道磁性特征和超导态的手性本质尚缺乏直接实验证据，且电阻率随机开关的机制、以及手性超导的正常态磁性行为仍未明确。

Method: 采用纳米SQUID探针磁力测量技术（nanoSQUID-on-tip magnetometry），对厚度在3至13层之间的电子掺杂菱面体石墨烯器件进行轨道磁化成像，并结合输运测量与局域磁力测量数据进行关联分析。

Result: 1) 四分之一金属相（quarter metal）的磁化在有限密度处达到峰值，与Berry曲率集中在有限动量“火环”（ring of fire）一致；2) 四层样品中超导态具有有限轨道磁矩，直接证实其手性（chiral）本质；3) 电阻率随机开关源于密度调控的谷分辨总磁矩（valley-resolved total magnetic moment）符号变化，导致亚稳态磁畴形成；4) 手性超导体的正常态存在独特的磁不均匀性，暗示应变调制的磁性与非磁性基态竞争。

Conclusion: 结果揭示了菱面体多层石墨烯中手性超导现象背后存在微妙的能量竞争，该超导仅在较窄的层数范围内出现；同时提供了超导态手性本质的直接磁学证据，并提出利用电场控制整个器件轨道磁矩翻转的潜在机制。

Abstract: Electron doped rhombohedral multilayer graphene at high displacement field features an exceptionally flat band minimum with near-ideal quantum geometry. Experiments in this regime observe the formation of a 'quarter metal,' in which the electron liquid condenses into a single spin- and valley flavor. Remarkably, recent experiments have found a zero resistance state in the same region of the density- and displacement-field-tuned parameter space, attributed to the formation of a chiral superconductor characterized by a finite-momentum Cooper pair condensate. Here, we use nanoSQUID-on-tip magnetometry to map the orbital magnetization of electron-doped rhombohedral graphene devices ranging in thickness between 3 and 13 layers. Magnetization within the quarter metal phases peaks at finite density, consistent with concentration of the Berry curvature in a finite-momentum 'ring of fire'. Correlating transport and local magnetometry data in a tetralayer sample reveals that the superconducting state has a finite orbital magnetic moment, providing direct evidence of its chiral nature. We further show that widely observed stochastic switching of the resistivity in the metallic regime arises from a density-tuned sign change in the valley-resolved total magnetic moment. This leads to the formation of metastable magnetic domains under typical gate control sequences and can also be harnessed for electric-field controlled switching of orbital moment across the entire device. Unexpectedly, we find magnetic inhomogeneity specific to the apparent normal state of the chiral superconductor, suggestive of a strain-tuned competition between magnetic and non-magnetic ground states. Our results point to a subtle energetic competition underlying the observation of chiral superconductivity in a narrow range of layer numbers.

</details>

# stat.AP [[Back]](#toc)

### [52] [Model-free estimation in scattering analysis of microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29424)
*Tong Lin,Jinseok Lee,Matt Helgeson,Megan T. Valentine,Yimin Luo,Mengyang Gu*

Main category: stat.AP

TL;DR: 本文提出MF-AIUQ，一种基于概率框架的无模型方法，通过散射分析直接从显微镜视频中估计均方位移（MSD），无需粒子追踪或轨迹链接，并在多种模拟和实验系统中验证了其在全滞后时间范围内的平滑稳定估计能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于粒子追踪的MSD估计方法需要手动调参，在高密度或低对比度场景下不稳定，且无法覆盖整个滞后时间（lag time）范围。本文旨在开发一种无需粒子分离与轨迹链接、无需预设模型的无模型方法，以克服上述局限。

Method: MF-AIUQ基于累计量定理（cumulant theorem）建立的中间散射函数（intermediate scattering function, ISF）与MSD的关系，采用边际极大似然估计（marginal maximum likelihood estimator）估计MSD。似然函数通过对数间隔的傅里叶基函数与滞后时间点的傅里叶变换强度子集进行近似，以降低计算成本。

Result: 在涵盖多种代表性随机过程的模拟研究及三个实验系统（牛顿流体、凝胶化体系、蜗牛粘液生物聚合物）中，MF-AIUQ均能在全滞后时间范围内提供平滑稳定的MSD估计，并在粒子追踪不可靠或MSD参数模型不可得/不可验证的场景中展现出补充价值。

Conclusion: MF-AIUQ作为一种无模型、免追踪的MSD估计方法，能够稳定处理高密度和低对比度的显微镜视频数据，是对传统粒子追踪方法的有效补充。

Abstract: The mean squared displacement (MSD) of particles or probes is commonly estimated from microscopy videos using particle tracking approaches, which rely on tuning parameters manually, and are often unstable over the entire lag time range, especially in dense or low-contrast situations. In this work, we propose model-free ab initio uncertainty quantification (MF-AIUQ), a model-free method for scattering analysis of microscopy video based on a probabilistic framework, which estimates MSD without isolating particles and linking their trajectories. Based on the relationship between the intermediate scattering function (ISF) and the MSD derived from the cumulant theorem, MF-AIUQ estimates the MSD values by the marginal maximum likelihood estimator. To reduce the computational cost, the likelihood function is approximated by a subset of Fourier-transformed intensities. These intensities are equally spaced at the logarithmic values of Fourier basis functions and lag time points. We found that the ISF is smooth in this logarithmic input space, and the information of the ISF can be captured by this subset of inputs. We examine the method through simulation studies covering several representative stochastic processes and three experimental systems: a Newtonian fluid for evaluating performance in optically dense and bright-field settings, a gelation system with an evolving MSD shape, and snail mucin, a viscoelastic biopolymer, for modulus estimation. Across these studies, MF-AIUQ provides smooth and stable MSD estimates over the full lag time range and serves as a useful complementary approach in settings where particle tracking is unreliable or a parametric model of MSD is unavailable or unverifiable.

</details>

### [53] [Material selection for mid-infrared thin-film coatings and windows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29079)
*Jin-Woo Cho,Tanuj Kumar,Hongyan Mei,Mikhail A. Kats*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文总结了红外透明材料（infrared-transparent materials）的室温光学性质，针对薄膜涂层（thin-film coatings）和窗口（windows）两种应用场景分别定义了透明度窗口（transparency window），并按化学类别、结晶度和沉积技术对材料进行分类，提供了实用性能对比和可复现的数据集与绘图脚本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 红外光学设计中，不同应用场景（如薄膜涂层与窗口）对材料透明度的要求差异显著，但目前缺乏一个清晰、实用且可自定义的透明度窗口参考标准，以帮助研究者快速筛选合适的红外透明材料。

Method: 首先，根据两种应用场景（薄膜涂层和窗口）分别设定透明度判据：薄膜涂层要求吸收系数（absorption coefficient）α < 10 cm⁻¹，窗口要求 α < 1 cm⁻¹。然后，按化学类别（chemical group）、结晶度（crystallinity）和典型沉积技术（typical deposition technique）对材料进行分类，并讨论化学稳定性、热稳定性、机械硬度和成本等实用优缺点。最后，提供数据集和绘图脚本，允许用户针对不同应用重新生成透明度窗口图。

Result: 明确了薄膜涂层对透明度的要求远低于窗口（允许多个数量级的吸收系数差异），因此同一波长范围内可使用的光学材料种类显著增多。通过系统的分类和性能对比，生成了易用的参考数据集和可复现的透明度窗口图。

Conclusion: 该工作为红外光学设计提供了实用参考，建议设计者直接打印相关图表作为日常工具。公开的数据和脚本支持按需定制透明度窗口图，增强了结果的可复用性。

Abstract: We summarized the room-temperature optical properties for infrared-transparent materials, defining transparency windows for two different applications: thin-film coatings (absorption coefficient $α< 10 cm^{-1}$) and windows ($α< 1 cm^{-1}$). The transparency requirements for thin films are substantially less stringent, enabling the use of many more optical materials for a given wavelength range. To make an easy-to-use reference, we categorized materials by chemical group, crystallinity, and typical deposition technique, and discussed practical pros and cons such as chemical and thermal stability, mechanical hardness, and cost. The datasets and plotting scripts are provided so that users can regenerate transparency-window maps for different applications. If you do optical design at infrared wavelengths, we recommend that you print out the figures and stick them on your wall.

</details>


### [54] [Giant Photon Superbunching from Weak Nonlinearity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29596)
*You Wang,Xu Zheng,Timothy C. H. Liew,Y. D. Chong*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文预测，通过干涉工程精细调控弱非线性光子腔间的耦合与驱动参数，可在弱非线性光子腔系统中实现极端光子超聚束（superbunching），数值计算显示四谐振子系统中可达到 g^(2)(0)=135，且该机制与集成光子平台高度兼容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统光子超聚束（g^(2)>2）通常依赖于强光学非线性或集体多光子发射过程，而弱非线性系统中的超聚束效应尚未被充分探索。本文旨在揭示弱非线性光子腔系统中亦可产生极端超聚束，并探索其在集成光子平台上的实现潜力。

Method: 通过干涉工程（interference engineering）精细调节腔间耦合（inter-cavity couplings）与驱动参数，在弱非线性光子腔系统中创建压缩真空态（squeezed vacuum），从而实现光子超聚束。采用数值计算方法对包含四个含代表性能尔介质（Kerr media）的光子谐振子系统进行模拟分析。

Result: 数值计算表明，在包含四个弱非线性谐振子的系统中，二阶关联函数在零延迟时刻可达 g^(2)(0)=135，同时发射率（emission rate）为 80 kHz，实现了极端光子超聚束。

Conclusion: 本文提出的机制无需强光学非线性或集体多光子发射，即可在弱非线性光子腔系统中实现极端超聚束，且与采用常规光学介质的集成光子平台（integrated photonic platforms）高度兼容，为该效应的实用化提供了新途径。

Abstract: Photon superbunching, which occurs when the second-order correlation satisfies $g^{(2)}> 2$, is typically associated with strong optical nonlinearities or collective multi-photon emission processes. We predict that extreme superbunching can also arise in systems of weakly-nonlinear photonic cavities, via the creation of a squeezed vacuum through interference engineering by fine-tuning inter-cavity couplings and drive parameters. We present numerical calculations indicating that a system of four photonic resonators containing representative Kerr media can achieve $g^{(2)}(0) = 135$ with a $80\,\text{kHz}$ emission rate. Unlike earlier superbunching schemes, this mechanism is highly compatible with integrated photonic platforms constructed using conventional optical media.

### [55] [Common Noise-Induced Group-Level Synchronization Between Uncoupled Groups of Oscillators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29529)
*Tae-Wook Ko*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 本文研究了在无组间耦合条件下，由共同噪声（common noise）驱动的振荡器组之间的组级同步（group-level synchronization）现象。通过数值模拟和理论分析，发现当各组受到相同的共同噪声驱动时，代表各组集体振荡的复序参量（complex order parameter）能够实现同步，即使在组内无耦合或振荡器非全同的情况下也是如此。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在不存在组间直接耦合时，共同噪声是否能够诱导不同振荡器组之间的组级同步现象，从而理解噪声驱动下集体行为的基本机制。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，研究系统包含全同与非全同振荡器、有/无组内耦合等多种情形；通过推导相位密度演化映射（phase density evolution mapping）进行解析分析。

Result: 各组内部的同步程度（由复Kuramoto序参量的绝对值衡量）通常表现出显著的时间涨落；但重要的是，当各组被相同的共同噪声驱动时，代表各组集体振荡的复序参量之间能够实现同步。

Conclusion: 通过推导相位密度演化映射，从解析角度解释了在无组内耦合条件下组级同步如何实现，揭示了共同噪声在诱导高阶集体行为中的关键作用。

Abstract: We investigate group-level synchronization between oscillator groups induced by common noise in the absence of inter-group coupling. Each group receives a common noise shared by all its oscillators and independent local noise inputs to individual oscillators. The same common noise is applied to all groups. The system is studied with both identical and nonidentical oscillators, and with and without intra-group coupling. In the nonidentical case, natural frequencies are drawn from the same distribution for both groups, making them statistically equivalent. Through numerical simulations of this system, we find that the degree of synchronization within each group, measured by the absolute value of a complex Kuramoto order parameter, typically shows significant temporal fluctuations. Importantly, the complex order parameters representing the collective oscillations of the groups synchronize when the groups are driven by the same common noise. By deriving a phase density evolution mapping, we analytically explain how this group-level synchronization is achieved in the absence of intra-group coupling.

</details>

### [56] [A non-commutative discrete first Painlevé hierarchy: the Lax pair approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29722)
*Irina Bobrova*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文通过引入等单色问题（isomonodromic problem）的非对易类比，构建了离散第一潘勒韦（Painlevé）层次结构的非对易版本 $\text{d-PI}_m^{\text{nc}}$，并证明该层次结构与经典版本均可由 Svinin 多项式 $S_s^k(n)$ 表达；同时推导了非对易 Volterra 格点层次结构到 $\text{d-PI}_m^{\text{nc}}$ 的约化，并给出了前三个成员的连续极限，恢复了微分第一潘勒韦层次结构前三个成员的非对易类比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典离散第一潘勒韦层次结构（d-PI_m）推广到非对易（non-commutative）情形，以探索非对易可积系统（non-commutative integrable systems）的代数结构与动力学行为。

Method: 采用等单色问题的非对易类比（non-commutative analogue of the isomonodromic problem），构造非对易版本的离散第一潘勒韦层次结构 $\text{d-PI}_m^{\text{nc}}$，并利用 Svinin 多项式 $S_s^k(n)$ 统一表达经典与非对易层次结构；进一步推导非对易 Volterra 格点层次结构到 $\text{d-PI}_m^{\text{nc}}$ 的约化，并计算前三个成员的连续极限。

Result: 成功构造了 $\text{d-PI}_m^{\text{nc}}$ 层次结构；证明了 $\text{d-PI}_m$ 与 $\text{d-PI}_m^{\text{nc}}$ 均可由 Svinin 多项式 $S_s^k(n)$ 表达；得到了非对易 Volterra 格点层次结构到 $\text{d-PI}_m^{\text{nc}}$ 的约化；给出了 $\text{d-PI}_m^{\text{nc}}$ 前三个成员的显式连续极限，恢复了微分第一潘勒韦层次结构前三个成员的非对易类比。

Conclusion: 非对易离散第一潘勒韦层次结构 $\text{d-PI}_m^{\text{nc}}$ 具有良好定义的代数结构和约化关系，其连续极限与微分情形一致，表明该方法可以系统地将经典可积层次结构推广至非对易框架。

Abstract: Using a non-commutative analogue of the isomonodromic problem associated with the discrete first Painlevé hierarchy, we construct a non-commutative version of this hierarchy, denoted by $\text{d-PI}_m^{\text{nc}}$. We show that both hierarchies, $\text{d-PI}_m$ and $\text{d-PI}_m^{\text{nc}}$, can be expressed in terms of the polynomials $S_s^k(n)$, which we call the Svinin polynomials. We also derive a reduction of the non-commutative Volterra lattice hierarchy to the $\text{d-PI}_m^{\text{nc}}$ hierarchy and present explicit continuous limits for the first three members of the $\text{d-PI}_m^{\text{nc}}$, thereby recovering non-commutative analogues of the first three members of the differential first Painlevé hierarchy.

</details>

### [57] [Multi-Loop Negative Geometries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28926)
*Lance J. Dixon,Umut Oktem,Shruti Paranjape,Jaroslav Trnka,Yongqun Xu,Shun-Qing Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过 Amplituhedron 和负几何（negative geometries）框架，研究平面 N=4 超对称杨-米尔斯理论中散射振幅与 Wilson 环的对偶关系。作者对负几何进行了三圈显式计算，揭示了图内部圈数与多重对数（polylogarithms）深度之间的关联；通过积分得到尖点异常维度（cusp anomalous dimension）；并展示了高圈图在奇偶zeta贡献分离下的抑制行为，同时完成了单圈图收敛无穷级数的全阶重求和。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 散射振幅与零多边形 Wilson 环期望值之间存在对偶性，而 Amplituhedron 为全圈积分核（integrand）提供了几何构造。本文旨在通过 Amplituhedron 和负几何框架，进一步探索一个与散射振幅对数密切相关的红外有限量 F(g,z) 在四点的性质，包括其圈图结构、多重对数深度特征以及尖点异常维度的计算。

Method: 利用负几何（negative geometries）构造红外有限的积分单元，对三圈所有负几何进行显式计算；通过分析图内部圈数与多重对数深度之间的数值关系，区分奇偶zeta贡献；对单圈图收敛无穷级数进行全阶重求和。

Result: 三圈计算表明，图中内部圈数与多重对数深度紧密相关。在分离奇偶zeta贡献后，高圈图被抑制。通过对 F(g,z) 关于交叉比 z 积分，得到了尖点异常维度 Γ_cusp。对单圈图收敛无穷级数的全阶重求和给出了解析结果。

Conclusion: 负几何框架为红外有限量的圈图计算提供了自然且有效的工具。内部圈数与多重对数深度的关联揭示了该理论的代数结构，而奇偶zeta分离揭示了一种新的抑制机制。全阶重求和的结果为进一步理解该理论的非微扰行为提供了线索。

Abstract: Scattering amplitudes in planar ${\cal N}=4$ supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory are dual to expectation values of null polygonal Wilson loops. The Amplituhedron provides a geometric construction for the all-loop integrand as the canonical form on the geometric region in the Grassmannian defined by a certain set of inequalities. For a closely related object, the logarithm of the scattering amplitude, the integrand is reproduced in a similar way using negative geometries. When integrated over all loop momenta except one, the result is infrared (IR) finite and equal to the expectation value of a certain Wilson loop with a Lagrangian insertion. At four points, this quantity, ${\cal F}(g,z)$ only depends on a single cross ratio $z$ and the 't Hooft coupling $g$. At weak coupling, it is known up to three loops from perturbative Wilson loop computations and at strong coupling through the AdS/CFT correspondence at leading order. In this paper, we explore this object further through the lens of the Amplituhedron and negative geometries, which provide very natural IR finite building blocks. We perform an explicit three-loop computation of all negative geometries and show that the number of internal cycles in the diagram is closely linked to the depth of polylogarithms. We calculate the cusp anomalous dimension $Γ_{\rm cusp}$ by integrating ${\cal F}(g,z)$ over $z$. We show that the higher-cycle diagrams are suppressed if we consider separate odd and even zeta contributions. Furthermore, we focus on certain convergent infinite series of one-cycle diagrams, perform all-loop order resummations of such contributions, and discuss various features of the result.

</details>


### [58] [Analytic Bootstrap for $O(N)$ Boundary Conformal Field Theories with Interacting Boundaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28933)
*Xinyu Sun,Shao-Kai Jian,Hong Yao*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过解析自举（analytic bootstrap）结合微扰重整化群（renormalization group）分析，系统研究了d=4-ε和d=3-ε中具有边界相互作用的O(N)边界共形场论（BCFTs），识别了全新的边界不动点并首次提取了三临界O(N)模型的边界共形数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边界共形场论（BCFT）中具有相互作用的边界通常难以解析处理，现有方法对边界不动点和共形数据的系统确定仍不充分，特别是对于非幺正（non-unitary）情形和高阶临界点。

Method: 采用解析自举（analytic bootstrap）导出共形数据上的普适约束，使无限多算符展开可用有限输入表示；再结合微扰重整化群（perturbative renormalization-group）分析，在d=4-ε中识别由边界三次耦合（boundary cubic coupling）生成的全新边界不动点。

Result: 在d=4-ε中发现全新的边界不动点（含非幺正情形），并计算了其共形数据至领头阶；在d=3-ε中首次提取了三临界O(N)模型（tricritical O(N) model）的边界共形数据。

Conclusion: 该工作为具有相互作用的边界BCFT提供了统一的理论框架，简化了体算符展开（bulk operator expansion）和边界算符展开（boundary operator expansion）的确定过程。

Abstract: We investigate $O(N)$ boundary conformal field theories (BCFTs) with boundary interactions in $d=4-ε$ and $d=3-ε$ employing the analytic bootstrap. By deriving universal constraints on conformal data, we show that infinitely many operator expansions can be expressed in terms of a finite set of inputs. Complementing the analytic bootstrap with a perturbative renormalization-group analysis, we identify totally new boundary fixed points in $d=4-ε$, including non-unitary ones, generated by a boundary cubic coupling, and compute their conformal data to leading order. Moreover, we leverage our solution in $d=3-ε$ to extract, for the first time, the boundary conformal data for the tricritical $O(N)$ model. Altogether, our approach provides a unified prescription for BCFTs with interacting boundaries and streamlines the determination of bulk and boundary operator expansions.

### [59] [Gravity Decoupling and Axionic Shift Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28938)

Abstract: We analyse the rôle of approximate axionic shift symmetries in gravity-decoupling limits arising in type II Calabi-Yau compactifications. Associated with each shift symmetry there is an axionic string whose tension constrains the gradient of the Kähler potential, as expected in regimes where gravity becomes weakly coupled. ### [60] [Dynamical Entanglement Phase Transitions in Holographic CFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28939)

Method: 以两个空间区间之间的互信息作为探针，在全息对偶框架下利用大中心荷极限分析互信息的动力学演化；结合共形块展开和测地线组态来分析相位结构；运用群论方法识别动力学对称性；并通过数值研究临界自旋链（critical spin chains）考察有限中心荷效应。

Abstract: We study the time evolution of the entanglement structure of holographic conformal field theories after a local quench. Using the mutual information between two spatial intervals as a probe, we find that $1+1$-dimensional conformal field theories exhibit a rich pattern of dynamical phase transitions. In the large-central-charge limit, mutual information develops sharp non-analyticities at critical times, providing a concrete entanglement-based realization of dynamical quantum phase transitions. We find that the dynamics organize into six distinct phases of mutual information, each controlled by the dominance of a different conformal block, or equivalently, a different holographic geodesic configuration. This phase structure goes beyond the standard quasi-particle picture, explaining non-analytic features that are not captured by simple light-cone propagation from the quench points. We further identify a dynamical $D_4$ symmetry acting on the interval endpoints that controls the presence or absence of mutual information. The onset of mutual information is governed by the breaking of this symmetry to a $\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$ subgroup, suggesting a symmetry-based characterization of non-equilibrium entanglement dynamics analogous to the role of symmetry in equilibrium critical phenomena. Finally, numerical studies of critical spin chains indicate that finite-$c$ effects smooth out the sharp large-$c$ transitions between different mutual-information phases, while the transitions between phases with and without mutual information appear to remain non-analytic. These results offer a unifying perspective on real-time entanglement dynamics and their critical features in conformal many-body systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 88字母表可能成为四点形状因子的自然普适字母表（universal alphabet）。该工作为研究多圈形状因子的物理与数学结构（包括对跖对偶性）及其与QCD希格斯-部分子振幅的联系提供了新数据。

Abstract: We bootstrap the two-loop four-point next-to-maximally helicity-violating (NMHV) ratio function for the chiral stress-tensor form factor in planar maximally supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory (sYM) at the symbol level. Starting from an ansatz built from NMHV leading singularities and the known two-loop five-point one-mass integral function space, we impose finiteness, dihedral symmetry, parity and Galois symmetry, spurious-pole cancellation, collinear limits, and finally triple-collinear consistency, which together fix the result uniquely.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用椭圆数据（度量与场值或其对偶，但不同时取两者）定义紧致 d 维流形；通过将带椭圆数据的流形对粘（gluing）形成闭边界条件，利用引力路径积分（gravitational path integral）评估内积与迹；对子区域 Rényi 熵给出 prescription，并通过解析延拓（analytic continuation）得到 von Neumann 熵。

Conclusion: 基于椭圆数据的紧致流形量子态制备方案无需渐近结构，且其熵计算与已知的最小面 prescription 一致，为该框架的物理一致性提供了支持。

Abstract: We propose that any compact $d$-manifold with elliptic data, $\mathcal{J}$, prepares a quantum state $|\mathcal{J}\rangle$ on its $(d-1)$-boundary $σ$. Elliptic data consists of metric and field values, or their conjugates, but not both. No asymptotic structure is required. Inner products and traces are evaluated by the gravitational path integral with closed boundary conditions obtained by gluing elliptic data manifolds. In particular, we give a prescription for the Rényi entropies $S_n$ of a subregion of $σ$. In a class of examples, we find that $S_n$ is nonnegative and nonincreasing with $n$, as required for consistency. We obtain the von Neumann entropy by analytic continuation and find agreement with the minimal surface prescription of Bousso and Penington.

### [64] [Asymptotic Quantum Dynamics of Ghost Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29047)
*Luca Buoninfante*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个与普通场耦合的鬼场（ghost field）的戴森传播子（dressed propagator）在多粒子阈值以上第一黎曼叶（first Riemann sheet）上出现的一对复共轭极点。研究表明，这一极点结构导致鬼场的渐近态不存在自由的单粒子鬼态，因为复数质量的虚部倒数决定了非正交性的时间尺度，从而使得鬼粒子在远大于其逆宽度的时空尺度上无法被孤立地观测到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解多粒子阈值以上鬼场传播子中复共轭极点（complex conjugate poles）的结构及其物理含义，尤其是对渐近场（asymptotic field）和负模单粒子态（negative-norm one-particle state）的影响。

Method: 采用局部量子场论（local quantum field theory）的算符形式（operator formalism），分析鬼场与多粒子态组成的复合场在渐近时间处的相互作用，以及由此产生的量子干涉效应（quantum interference effects）。

Result: 渐近时间处鬼场与复合场的持续相互作用使得负模单粒子态与正模多粒子态的叠加态之间非正交（non-orthogonal），导致二者不可区分。复数质量（complex mass）的实部与虚部具有清晰的物理诠释，其中虚部的倒数设定了非正交性开始显现的时间尺度。

Conclusion: 不存在自由的渐近单粒子鬼态（free asymptotic one-particle ghost state）。鬼粒子的自由传播仅限于远小于其逆宽度的时间区间，因此探测器无法在渐近区域观测到孤立的鬼粒子。文章在结论部分讨论了开放问题与潜在应用。

Abstract: The dressed propagator of a ghost coupled to ordinary fields develops a pair of complex conjugate poles in the first Riemann sheet above the multi-particle threshold. We study the implications of this pole structure for the asymptotic field and its negative-norm one-particle state. Within the operator formalism of local quantum field theory, we show that interactions between the ghost field and the composite field of the multi-particle state persist at asymptotic times. These induce quantum interference effects that render the negative-norm one-particle state non-orthogonal to, and thus indistinguishable from, a superposition of positive-norm multi-particle states. As a result, no free asymptotic one-particle ghost state exists. The real and imaginary parts of the complex mass admit a clear physical interpretation; in particular, the inverse imaginary part sets the timescale for the onset of non-orthogonality. A freely propagating ghost is therefore confined to time intervals much shorter than its inverse width, so that a detector can never observe an isolated ghost particle asymptotically. Open questions and potential applications are discussed in the conclusions.

### [65] [Asymptotically Safe Gravitational Form Factors from the Proper-Time Flow Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29159)
*Emiliano Maria Glaviano*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在四维量子引力的规范时形式（proper-time formalism）中，研究了曲率展开至二次阶的非局域形状因子（non-local form factors）的重整化群（renormalization group）流。结果表明，流方程可积分至 $k=0$，从而重建形状因子的完整动量依赖，并在此框架下构造了渐近安全（asymptotically safe）解。然而，渐近安全并不自动保证积分解在 $\\Lambda\\to\\infty$ 时具有有限且与截断无关的极限；只有当紫外边界条件选择非高斯不动点（non-Gaussian fixed point）时，才能实现有限极限，从而得到重整化后的渐近安全形状因子，其在紫外区呈幂律衰减 $\\sim1/q^2$，在红外区呈现预期对数结构，普朗克尺度取代重整化尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究四维量子引力中非局域形状因子的重整化群流，并试图在该框架下构造渐近安全解，以理解引力在紫外完备性下的动量依赖行为。

Method: 采用规范时形式（proper-time formalism），在曲率展开（curvature expansion）至二次阶（quadratic order）的框架下推导重整化群流方程，并将流方程积分至 $k=0$，以重建形状因子（form factors）的完整动量依赖（full momentum dependence）。

Result: 渐近安全并不自动保证积分解在 $\\Lambda\\to\\infty$ 时具有有限且与截断无关的极限；解通常发展出对数发散 $\\ln(q^2/\\Lambda^2)$，仍需额外的重整化条件（renormalization condition）。仅当紫外边界条件（ultraviolet boundary condition）选择非高斯不动点（non-Gaussian fixed point）时，才能获得有限极限。重整化后的渐近安全形状因子在紫外区呈幂律衰减 $\\sim1/q^2$，在红外区呈现预期对数结构，且普朗克尺度（Planck scale）取代了重整化尺度（renormalization scale）$\\mu$。

Conclusion: 在四维量子引力的二次曲率展开阶，渐近安全解的存在并不足以确保紫外截断极限的有限性；必须通过非高斯不动点作为紫外边界条件来实现有限且重整化尺度无关的物理形状因子。所得形状因子在紫外和红外区域分别呈现幂律和对数行为，普朗克尺度在其中扮演关键角色。

Abstract: We study the renormalization group flow of non-local form factors in four-dimensional quantum gravity within the proper-time formalism at quadratic order in the curvature expansion. We show that the flow equations can be integrated down to $k=0$, allowing the reconstruction of the full momentum dependence of the form factors. Within this framework, we construct asymptotically safe solutions at this order. We find that asymptotic safety of the flow does not automatically ensure a finite cutoff-independent $Λ\to\infty$ limit for the integrated solutions, which in general develop a logarithmic divergence $\ln(q^2/Λ^2)$, so that a renormalization condition is still required. A finite $Λ\to\infty$ limit compatible with asymptotic safety is obtained only when the ultraviolet boundary condition selects the non-Gaussian fixed point. This yields finite dimensionful form factors, removes UV logarithmic contributions, and ensures independence from the renormalization scale $μ$. The resulting renormalized asymptotically safe form factors display a power-law decay $\sim1/q^2$ in the ultraviolet and reproduce the expected logarithmic structure in the infrared, with the Planck scale replacing the renormalization scale.

### [66] [Higher Wess-Zumino-Witten term from semistrict higher Chern-Simons theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29282)
*Mengyao Wu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，在任意 $2n+2$ 维中，由半严格李2-代数（semistrict Lie 2-algebra）构造的高阶陈-西蒙斯作用量（higher Chern-Simons action）在高阶规范变换（higher gauge transformation）下会产生一个非平凡的高阶Wess-Zumino-Witten (WZW) 项。核心机制在于非零的Jacobiator（Jacobiator）直接生成了这一高阶WZW项，而在退化为严格情形时该项消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高阶规范理论中非平凡拓扑项（topological term）——即高阶WZW项——的生成机制，特别是考察半严格李2-代数中非零Jacobiator的作用。

Method: 基于半严格李2-代数构建任意 $2n+2$ 维的高阶陈-西蒙斯作用量，并分析其在高阶规范变换下的行为，通过比较严格与半严格情形来揭示Jacobiator的角色。

Result: 半严格情形下的非零Jacobiator直接导致了高阶WZW项的产生；而当李2-代数退化为严格情形时，该项消失。

Conclusion: 半严格李2-代数中的非零Jacobiator是生成非平凡高阶WZW项的关键结构要素，这为理解高阶规范理论中的拓扑项来源提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We show that in any $2n+2$ dimensions, the higher Chern-Simons action built from a semistrict Lie 2-algebra gives a non-trivial higher Wess-Zumino-Witten (WZW) term under a higher gauge transformation. The key point is that the non-zero Jacobiator directly generates the higher WZW term, hereas it vanishes when reduced to the strict case.

</details>

Abstract: A non-Abelian gauge field framework is proposed using the hypercomplex ring formalism. ### [68] [Magic Relations and Critical Varieties of Feynman Integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29789)
*Giulio Crisanti,Hjalte Frellesvig,Andrzej Pokraka,Sid Smith*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文首次对费曼积分计算中导致常规方法失效的“魔法关系”（magic relations）进行了系统性刻画，发现其出现与生成扇区中高维权变簇（higher-dimensional critical varieties）的存在密切相关，并提出了一个可用于检测和寻找魔法关系的实用计算测试方法，同时在配套的 Mathematica 文件 Magic-Test.m 中实现了该方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 魔法关系是一种特殊的分部积分恒等式（integration-by-parts identities），其存在会导致费曼积分计算管线（Feynman-integral computational pipeline）中多种成功的方法失效，因此有必要对其进行检测和理解。目前尚缺乏对这类恒等式的系统性刻画，本文旨在迈出这一方向的第一步。

Method: 通过观察和论证，指出魔法关系的出现总是伴随生成扇区（generating sector）中存在高维权变簇（higher-dimensional critical varieties）。据此提出了一个实用的计算测试，用于判断费曼积分族是否可能包含魔法关系并定位它们；该测试已在附属的 Mathematica 文件 Magic-Test.m 中实现。此外，还讨论了在存在高维权变簇时主积分（master integrals）数量的计数方法、魔法关系在对称性下的行为分类，以及其与切割（cuts）之间的相互作用。

Result: 建立了魔法关系与高维权变簇之间的关联，并提供了相应的计算检测方法。

Conclusion: 魔法关系的出现与高维权变簇的存在一致，这一发现为检测和理解魔法关系提供了理论基础和实用工具。文中还给出了主积分计数、对称性分类以及切割关系等方面的讨论，丰富了对此类恒等式的整体认识。

Abstract: Magic relations are a class of integration-by-parts identities where all integrals in the generating sector drop out. Since their presence causes several otherwise successful methods in the Feynman-integral computational pipeline to break down, they are important to detect and understand. In this paper, we take a first step toward a systematic characterization of such identities. Specifically, we observe and argue that the occurrence of magic relations always coincides with the presence of higher-dimensional critical varieties in the generating sector. This provides a practical computational test to check if a family of Feynman integrals can contain magic relations and to find them, which we implement in the ancillary Mathematica file Magic-Test.m. Additionally, we discuss how to count the number of master integrals in the presence of higher-dimensional critical varieties, classify the behavior of magic relations under symmetries, and we discuss their interplay with cuts.

### [69] [Five-dimensional Geometry from Spinning Amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29831)
*Lucile Cangemi,Iustin Surubaru*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在五维时空中引入了三点旋量-螺旋度振幅（spinor-helicity amplitude）的经典极限研究，建立了旋量不变量与自旋算符期望值之间的映射，并通过引入霍奇对偶自旋张量（Hodge dual of the classical spin tensor）来推广多极展开结构，最终识别出描述Myers-Perry黑洞的振幅类别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 四维大质量旋量-螺旋度变量（massive spinor-helicity variables）已被证明是研究高自旋场与引力子之间振幅的有效工具，其中一类特殊振幅在经典极限下能够再现Kerr黑洞的线性化应力-能量张量。作者希望将这一研究纲领推广到五维，系统建立五维三点振幅的经典极限理论框架。

Method: 建立了旋量不变量（spinor invariants）与自旋算符期望值（expectation values of spin operators）之间的映射关系，将振幅构建模块与多极展开（multipole expansion）的构建模块进行匹配。为了处理一般振幅的经典极限，引入了霍奇对偶自旋张量来扩充多极结构。通过放松自旋张量的正交性条件，模型化具有单一旋转等距（single rotational isometry）的时空。

Result: 发现在一般振幅的经典极限中，需要将霍奇对偶自旋张量纳入多极结构。研究了非全对称极化积（fully-symmetric products of polarisations）描述的自旋态，并表明它们可以描述相同的时空。通过放松自旋张量正交性条件，能够建模允许内部自旋偏移（internal spin shift）的时空。识别出描述Myers-Perry黑洞的振幅类别，并评论了向任意维度的推广。

Conclusion: 五维三点旋量-螺旋度振幅的经典极限理论框架得以建立，为研究更高维时空中的自旋体-引力相互作用提供了新工具；Myers-Perry黑洞振幅的识别及其向任意维度的推广展望为后续研究开辟了方向。

Abstract: Massive spinor-helicity variables in four dimensions are a useful tool for studying amplitudes between higher-spin fields and gravitons. Among them a special, simple set of amplitudes reproduces the linearized stress-energy tensor of a Kerr black hole in the classical limit. In this work we initiate the study of the classical limit of three-point spinor-helicity amplitudes in five dimensions. We introduce the map between the spinor invariants and the expectation values of spin operators and match the amplitude building blocks with those of the multipole expansion. Interestingly, in order to take the classical limit of a general amplitude, we need to augment the multipole structures with the Hodge dual of the classical spin tensor. We study the classical limit of alternative spinning states not described by fully-symmetric products of polarisations and conclude that they can describe the same spacetimes. Finally, by relaxing the orthogonality condition of the spin tensor we are able to model spacetimes with a single rotational isometry and match these to the classical limit of amplitudes allowing for an internal spin shift. Along the way we also identify the class of amplitudes describing the Myers-Perry black hole and comment on its generalization to arbitrary dimensions.

### [70] [Black Hole Photon Rings Saturate the Quantum Chaos Bound](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29923)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了黑洞周围光子环（photon ring）区域的量子混沌界（quantum chaos bound），发现不稳定零测地线的Lyapunov指数（Lyapunov exponent）在光子环的赤道圆轨道上恰好饱和该界限，并通过out-of-time-order关联子（OTOC）验证了这一结果。进一步表明，光子环对量子混沌界的饱和隐含了Bekenstein界（Bekenstein bound）在准正则模（quasi-normal modes）eikonal极限下的饱和，从而拓展了黑洞热力学与混沌动力学之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索黑洞附近光子环区域是否能够饱和量子混沌界，并进一步揭示该饱和与Bekenstein信息发射速率界之间的关系，以深化对黑洞热力学和混沌动力学（chaotic dynamics）联系的理解。

Method: 计算广义Kerr几何（generalized Kerr geometries）中不稳定零测地线（unstable null geodesics）相关的Lyapunov指数，以及弦探针（string probe）诱导的温度；利用近环区域的out-of-time-order关联子（out-of-time-order correlator, OTOC）独立导出相同指数以验证结果。

Result: 在光子环的赤道圆轨道上，量子混沌界被精确饱和；该饱和进一步导致准正则模在eikonal极限下Bekenstein信息发射速率界的饱和。

Conclusion: 光子环区域是检验热化（thermalization）与信息扰乱（information scrambling）基本极限的有效探针，研究结果拓展了黑洞热力学与混沌动力学之间的已知对应关系。

Abstract: We study the quantum chaos bound in the photon ring region surrounding black holes. By evaluating the Lyapunov exponent associated with unstable null geodesics in a broad class of generalized Kerr geometries, as well as the temperature induced by a string probe, we show that the quantum chaos bound is exactly saturated on equatorial circular orbits of the photon ring. We confirm our result by deriving the same exponent from out-of-time-order correlators in the near ring region. As a byproduct, we show that the photon ring saturation of the quantum chaos bound implies the saturation of the Bekenstein bound on the rate of information emission from the ringdown phase through the quasi-normal modes in the eikonal limit. Our results extend the known correspondence between black hole thermodynamics and chaotic dynamics, highlighting the role of the photon ring as a probe of the fundamental limits on thermalization and information scrambling in black holes.

### [71] [Perturbative Nicolai-Map Diagrammatics: Application to Poincaré Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29990)
*Ji-Seong Chae,Hun Jang,Junhyeok Lee*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种微扰图框架来构造Nicolai映射，并将其应用于四维 $\mathcal{N}=1$ 庞加莱超引力（Poincaré supergravity）在平坦闵可夫斯基时空背景下的展开。该框架克服了耦合流-算符构造在局域超对称情形下的障碍，并通过联合展开引力耦合常数 $\kappa$ 和圈计数参数 $\hbar$，逐阶推导出Nicolai映射的定义条件。分析表明，爱因斯坦-希尔伯特引力子（graviton）扇区要求Rarita–Schwinger引力微子（gravitino）的参与，从而确认了Nicolai关于超对称性（supersymmetry）的刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的耦合流-算符构造在推广到局域超对称（local supersymmetry）时遇到多重障碍，因此需要一种替代方法来构建Nicolai映射。本文旨在发展一种微扰图方法，以系统性地构造四维 $\mathcal{N}=1$ 庞加莱超引力的Nicolai映射。

Method: 采用微扰图框架，将玻色有效作用量（bosonic effective action）和Nicolai映射联合在引力耦合常数 $\kappa$ 和圈计数参数 $\hbar$ 下展开。通过有效作用量图列举Nicolai映射 Ansatz 中所有允许的局域项，将构造简化为有限非线性多项式方程组，并逐阶推导自由作用量条件和行列式匹配条件。

Result: 在阶 $κ^2$ 下，所得约束条件与具体玻色输入细节无关且具有层级结构：阶 $κ^2$ 的一致性进一步限制了阶 $κ$ 的数据。发现爱因斯坦-希尔伯特引力子扇区在 $κ^2$ 阶即要求引入Rarita–Schwinger引力微子，表明纯爱因斯坦引力仅在其 $\mathcal{N}=1$ 超对称完备化——庞加莱超引力——框架下才存在Nicolai映射。

Conclusion: 纯爱因斯坦引力无法独立支持Nicolai映射，该映射的存在性要求 $\mathcal{N}=1$ 超对称性，从而验证了Nicolai关于超对称性本质特征的论断。所发展的微扰图框架为构建局域超对称理论中的Nicolai映射提供了可行的替代方案。

Abstract: We develop a perturbative, diagrammatic framework for constructing Nicolai maps and apply it to four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=1$ Poincaré supergravity expanded around flat Minkowski space. It provides an alternative to the coupling-flow-operator construction, which faces several obstructions when extended to local supersymmetry. Expanding the bosonic effective action and the Nicolai map jointly in the gravitational coupling $κ$ and the loop-counting parameter $\hbar$, we derive the Nicolai-map defining conditions, i.e. the free-action and determinant-matching conditions, order by order. The diagrammatics enumerates all admissible local terms in the Nicolai-map ansatz from the effective-action diagrams and reduces the construction to a finite system of nonlinear polynomial equations. Carried through order $κ^{2}$, the resulting constraints are found to be independent of the detailed bosonic input and hierarchical, order-$κ^{2}$ consistency further restricting the order-$κ$ data. A consistent Nicolai-map construction for the Einstein--Hilbert graviton sector is found to require the Rarita--Schwinger gravitino already at this order: Einstein gravity admits a Nicolai map only through its $\mathcal{N}=1$ supersymmetric completion, Poincaré supergravity, supporting Nicolai's characterization of supersymmetry.

### [72] [Coupling Higher Form Structures of the EFT of Force Free Electrodynamics to Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30098)
*Harsh Anand*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将爱因斯坦-希尔伯特（Einstein-Hilbert）作用量中的麦克斯韦场强项替换为规范不变组合(b-da)²，引入高形式对称性（higher-form symmetry），由此得到一种推广的带电Reissner-Nordström黑洞度规，且在特定超曲面上局域退化为有效电荷依赖于(r-t)常数的Reissner-Nordström几何。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受无作用力电动力学（Force Free Electrodynamics）有效场论中高形式对称性结构的启发，作者希望将这种对称性引入引力理论，从而推广标准的Reissner-Nordström黑洞解。

Method: 在爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量中，将麦克斯韦场强项F²=(da)²替换为规范不变组合(b-da)²，其中a_μ为世界sheet规范场（worldsheet gauge field），b_{μν}为背景二形式场（background two-form field），使新作用量具有b→b+dΛ, a→a+Λ的高形式对称性；随后固定a_μ和b_{μν}的特定规范，得到推广的黑洞度规。

Result: 得到的广义度规在(r-t)=常数的超曲面（hypersurface）上局域退化为Reissner-Nordström几何，但有效电荷（effective charge）依赖于该常数(r-t)。

Conclusion: 通过引入高形式对称性，可以在引力理论中构造出一类推广的黑洞解，其在特定超曲面上表现为有效电荷可变的Reissner-Nordström度规，暗示高形式对称性可能为黑洞物理提供新的自由度与几何结构。

Abstract: We know that the charged Reissner Nordstr$ö$m black hole metric is obtained from the Einstein Hilbert gravitational action. This action has the kinetic term $F^2 = (da)^2$. Motivated by the higher-form symmetry structure of the EFT of Force Free Electrodynamics, we replace the Maxwell field-strength contribution in the Einstein Hilbert action by the gauge-invariant combination $(b-da)^2$, where $a_μ$ is the worldsheet gauge field and $b_{μν}$ is a background two-form field. This ensures that the new action has a higher form symmetry $b \rightarrow b+dΛ, a\rightarrow a+Λ$. Here, unlike in qed, $Λ$ may be any one form (not necessarily a differential one form $\partial_μφ$). The higher form symmetry here is one with the conserved current being a two form and the charge integrated on surfaces. Intuitively, it is the number/current of vector field lines that is conserved here, not the current of particles. Thus, integrating over a surface through which the field lines pierce is sufficient to find the number of these lines that are passing through; so the charge is integrated on surfaces, rather than on the volume. After fixing a particular gauge for the fields $a_μ$ and $b_{μν}$, we obtain a generalized black-hole metric. We find that on hypersurfaces satisfying $(r-t)=$ constant, this metric reduces locally to a Reissner Nordstr$ö$m geometry with an effective charge parameter depending on the constant $(r-t)$.

Abstract: Self-dual theories, being UV-finite, should have their own AdS/CFT dualities. Higher-spin extensions of self-dual theories are attractive to simplify the CFT duals. The maximal self-dual theory is Chiral higher-spin gravity, which should be dual to a subsector of Chern--Simons matter theories. As a step toward establishing self-dual holography, we develop the Fefferman--Graham expansion and holographic dictionary for arbitrary spin self-dual theories. As an application, we derive bulk-to-bulk propagators and compute three- and four-point AdS/CFT correlators in a contraction of Chiral higher-spin gravity, which is a higher-spin extension of self-dual Yang--Mills theory.

### [74] [Quiver Approach to Symmetry Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30354)
*Vivek Chakrabhavi,Mirjam Cvetič,Jonathan J. Heckman,Shani Meynet*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于探针膜路径代数（path algebra）的代数方法，用于从M-理论背景的卡拉比-丘锥（Calabi-Yau cone）中提取5D超共形场论（SCFT）的整体对称性反常（global symmetry anomalies），并将其封装为高维对称性理论（SymTh）的耦合，适用于几何计算未知或复杂的情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子场论（QFT）的整体对称性反常可以封装为高维对称性理论（SymTh）的特定耦合。然而，对于从M-理论背景$X$（一个卡拉比-丘锥（Calabi-Yau cone））构造的5D超共形场论（SCFT），提取该数据的现有几何计算方法——包括解析几何中的三重交点数（triple intersection numbers）和从边界几何$\partial X$提取的$\eta$-不变量（$\eta$-invariants）——在某些情形下未知或组合计算上过于复杂，因此需要一种替代的代数方法。

Method: 所提出的方法利用探针膜路径代数（path algebra of branes）从M-理论背景$X$中提取反常数据。这是一种代数方法，与基于几何计算（如解析几何中的三重交点数或边界几何$\partial X$的$\eta$-不变量）的方法互补。作者在多个环面三维流形（toric threefold）实例上进行了验证，包括轨道折叠$\mathbb{C}^{3} / \Gamma$以及更一般的萨萨-爱因斯坦五流形（Sasaki-Einstein five-manifolds）上的非轨道折叠卡拉比-丘锥。

Result: 该方法成功应用于环面三维流形的多种情形，包括轨道折叠$\mathbb{C}^{3} / \Gamma$和更一般的非轨道折叠卡拉比-丘锥。在几何计算未知或组合上难以处理的情况下，该代数方法依然有效。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一种互补的代数途径来提取5D SCFT的整体对称性反常，扩展了传统几何计算方法的适用范围，尤其适用于几何计算无法进行或过于复杂的场景。

Abstract: Global symmetry anomalies of a quantum field theory (QFT) can be packaged as specific couplings of a higher-dimensional symmetry theory (SymTh). In this work we show that for 5D superconformal field theories (SCFTs) engineered from M-theory backgrounds $X$ a Calabi-Yau cone, this data can be extracted from the path algebra of branes probing $X$. This provides a complementary algebraic approach compared with more geometric computations based on the explicit calculation of triple intersection numbers in a resolved geometry and / or $η$-invariants extracted from the boundary geometry $\partial X$. Our method applies in situations where the counterpart geometric computation is either unknown or combinatorially unwieldy. We illustrate with several toric threefold examples, including orbifolds $\mathbb{C}^{3} / Γ$ and more general non-orbifold Calabi-Yau cones of Sasaki-Einstein five-manifolds.

</details>

### [75] [Critical exponents for planar random-cluster model with cluster-weight $q=4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30030)

TL;DR: 本文通过 Baxter-Kelland-Wu 耦合以及六顶点模型高度函数收敛到高斯自由场（Gaussian Free Field）的方法，提取了 q=4 时平面临界随机簇模型（random-cluster model）和平面四态 Potts 模型（four-state Potts model）的临界指数（critical exponents）。
