Abstract: Using the Baxter-Kelland-Wu coupling and the convergence of the height function of the six-vertex model to the Gaussian Free Field, we extract critical exponents for the planar critical random-cluster model at $q=4$, and the planar four-state Potts model.

### [76] [Cosmo-PINN: A Physics-Informed Neural Network for Cosmological Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30139)
*Andronikos Paliathanasis*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出Cosmo-PINN，一种基于物理信息神经网络（Physics-Informed Neural Network）的宇宙学理论重建框架，通过将物理约束作为硬约束直接嵌入损失函数，利用重子声学振荡（Baryon Acoustic Oscillation, BAO）、宇宙计时器（Cosmic Chronometers）及超新星数据，重建暗能量状态方程参数$w_{DE}(z)$，并同时训练宇宙学参数$H_0$、$\Omega_{m0}$和$r_{\mathrm{drag}}$。重建结果显示$w_{DE}(z)$在红移$z=0.27-0.42$范围内穿越了幻象分界线（phantom divide），且与Chevallier-Polarski-Linder模型一致；在高红移的quintessence场景中，暗能量$\Omega_{DE}(z)$对宇宙流体提供了无压非零贡献，暗示了统一场景（unified scenario）。与纯数据驱动神经网络的对比证明了物理约束的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的高斯过程（Gaussian Process）和人工神经网络（Artificial Neural Network）重建方法存在一个主要局限性：恢复的解由数据驱动，未必保证物理一致性（physically consistent）。本文旨在通过将宇宙学约束直接嵌入损失函数来克服这一局限。

Method: 采用物理信息神经网络（Physics-Informed Neural Network, PINN）框架Cosmo-PINN，将宇宙学约束作为硬约束（hard constraints）直接嵌入损失函数，确保重建量在训练过程中每个点都满足物理定律。网络训练使用背景数据，包括DESI DR2的重子声学振荡（Baryon Acoustic Oscillation, BAO）、宇宙计时器（Cosmic Chronometers）以及三种不同的超新星汇编数据，同时将宇宙学参数$H_0$、$\Omega_{m0}$和$r_{\mathrm{drag}}$作为可训练参数引入。

Result: 重建的$w_{DE}(z)$在红移范围$z=0.27-0.42$内穿越幻象分界线（phantom divide），该结果与Chevallier-Polarski-Linder (CPL)模型获得的数值一致。在quintessence场景下，高红移时暗能量密度参数$\Omega_{DE}(z)$对宇宙流体提供无压非零贡献，暗示了统一场景（unified scenario）。与具有相同架构的纯数据驱动神经网络的对比表明，物理约束的施加对重建结果具有显著影响。

Conclusion: Cosmo-PINN通过将物理约束嵌入损失函数，有效克服了纯数据驱动方法缺乏物理一致性的问题，成功实现了暗能量状态方程参数的宇宙学理论重建。研究结果支持暗能量在红移约$0.27-0.42$范围内穿越幻象分界线的行为，并提示可能存在暗能量与暗物质的统一场景。

Abstract: We introduce Cosmo-PINN, a Physics-Informed Neural Network for reconstruction of the cosmological theory. In this work we demonstrate the application of the Cosmo-PINN in the reconstruction of the dark energy equation of state parameter $w_{DE}\left( z\right) $ directly from late-time cosmological observations. This framework overcomes the main limitation shared by Gaussian Process and Artificial Neural Network reconstruction approaches, where the recovered solution is driven by the data and it is not necessarily true that it is physically consistent, by embedding the cosmological constraints directly into the loss function as hard constraints, ensuring that the reconstructed quantities satisfy the physical laws at every point during the training. For the training of the network, we employed background data, and specifically the Baryon Acoustic Oscillation from DESI DR2, the Cosmic Chronometers and three different Supernova compilations, while we simultaneously introduce the cosmological parameters $H_{0},~Ω_{m0}$ and $r_{\mathrm{drag}}$ as trained parameters. The reconstruction shows that the trained $w_{DE}\left( z\right) $ crosses the phantom divide within the redshift range $z=0.27-0.42$ in agreement with the value obtained by the Chevallier-Polarski-Linder model. In the quintessence scenario, for large redshifts the dark energy $Ω_{DE}\left( z\right) $ provides a pressureless nonzero contribution to the cosmological fluid suggesting a unified scenario. Finally, we demonstrate the significance of imposing the physical constraints within the loss function by comparing the Cosmo-PINN reconstruction against a purely data-driven neural network with the same architecture.

</details>


### [77] [Late-time Quantum Vacuum Decay and its Cosmological Implications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30259)
*Yang Bai,Sida Lu,Nicholas Orlofsky*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了宇宙晚期亚稳态真空量子衰变（quantum vacuum decay）的可检验性，通过构建包含真空能变化、暗物质转化为暗辐射及畴壁（domain-wall）产生的唯象模型，结合DESI DR2重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillations, BAO）、超新星距离数据及压缩的宇宙微波背景（CMB）似然函数，发现该模型可缓解与ΛCDM的张力，并给出了CMB各向异性对气泡成核（bubble nucleation）和畴壁网络的约束边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚稳态真空景（landscape of metastable vacua）的存在暗示宇宙可能在晚期经历量子真空衰变，但该过程目前缺乏直接的观测检验。本研究旨在为这种晚期量子隧穿（quantum tunneling）过程建立可与宇宙学观测数据对比的理论框架，以检验其在真实宇宙中的发生可能性。

Method: 构建了一组晚期量子隧穿的唯象模型，其中包括真空能变化、暗物质子组分转化为暗辐射（dark radiation）并可能伴随畴壁产生。将这些模型预测的哈勃膨胀历史与DESI DR2 BAO数据、DES-Dovekie/Pantheon+/Union3超新星距离测量以及压缩的CMB似然函数进行统计比较，并进一步推导了来自气泡成核和畴壁网络的CMB各向异性约束。

Result: 在纯量子隧穿模型下，当前宇宙学距离测量仍允许在跃迁红移$z_t<1$时总真空能减少50%。对于包含暗物质转化和畴壁产生的模型，跃迁的优选红移约为$z_t \sim 7$，约10%的暗物质参与该过程，可有效缓解宇宙学观测与ΛCDM之间的张力。CMB各向异性约束强烈限制缓慢或稀疏的晚期跃迁，但暗物质密度依赖的隧穿机制可快速完成跃迁从而规避这些约束。

Conclusion: 晚期量子真空衰变是一个可检验的宇宙学现象，本文提供了从景观场景（landscape scenarios）中受启发的亚稳态真空物理的具体观测约束手段。最简量子隧穿模型允许真空能在红移$z_t$量级为1时发生约10%的下降，而非最简模型可规避CMB的强约束。

Abstract: The existence of a landscape of metastable vacua raises the possibility that our Universe may have undergone quantum vacuum decay at late times. This work explores how such a transition can be tested with cosmological observables, focusing on precision distance measurements and cosmic microwave background (CMB) anisotropies. A set of phenomenological models is constructed in which late-time quantum tunneling changes the vacuum energy and may convert a subcomponent of dark matter into dark radiation, possibly accompanied by domain-wall production. The resulting expansion histories are compared with DESI DR2 baryon acoustic oscillation data; supernova distance measurements from DES-Dovekie, Pantheon+, and Union3; and a compressed CMB likelihood. For quantum-tunneling models, current cosmological distance measurements still allow a 50% decrease in the total vacuum energy for a transition redshift $z_t<1$. The model with dark-matter conversion and domain-wall production provides a good fit to resolve the tension between cosmological observables and the $Λ$CDM model, with a preferred transition around $z_t \sim 7$ and about 10% of dark matter participating in the transition. Additionally, CMB anisotropy constraints from bubble nucleation and the associated domain-wall network are derived and shown to strongly restrict slow or sparse late transitions. Applied to the minimal quantum-tunneling model, these constraints allow an $\mathcal{O}(10\%)$ decrease in the total vacuum energy for a transition redshift $z_t$ of order unity. For nonminimal models, dark-matter-density-dependent tunneling can proceed rapidly enough to evade such bounds. These results demonstrate that late-time quantum vacuum decay is a testable cosmological phenomenon and provide a concrete observational handle on metastable-vacuum physics motivated by landscape scenarios.

### [78] [Bistability of midpoint-fused arches with pinned-pinned boundary conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29239)
*Rajat Goswami,Safvan Palathingal*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种称为中点融合拱（midpoint-fused arches, MFA）的三维结构，通过最小势能法建立了解析模型，分析了其在集中载荷下的双稳态（bistability）行为，并通过有限元模拟和实验验证了模型的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索中点融合拱（MFA）这一新型三维构型的结构双稳态（structural bistability），即其在无外力下可维持两种不同的稳定平衡状态的能力，为可变形结构设计提供理论基础。

Method: 基于最小势能原理（principle of minimum total potential energy）建立受集中载荷的固支-固支（pinned-pinned）MFA的解析模型，将单个拱视为空间变形体，并在融合点处推导运动学相容关系（kinematic compatibility relations），利用变形对称性简化问题。

Result: 对双拱MFA的力-位移响应进行表征，识别出不同的变形路径及路径转变；三拱MFA展现了更丰富的耦合变形行为。非线性有限元模拟（nonlinear finite-element simulations）和桌面实验（table-top experiments）与解析预测在平衡状态及转变响应上高度吻合。

Conclusion: 所提出的解析框架能够有效预测MFA在不同构型下的双稳态行为与变形路径转换，具有通用性，可推广至更复杂的多拱结构。

Abstract: Arranging multiple arches in a circular pattern and fusing them at their midpoint yields a three-dimensional configuration that we refer to as midpoint-fused arches (MFA). This study investigates the structural bistability of MFA, i.e., their ability to admit two distinct, force-free stable equilibrium states. Starting from an as-fabricated, stress-free configuration, MFA can invert into a stressed, toggled state reminiscent of an umbrella's ribs. We develop an analytical model for the response of a pinned-pinned MFA subjected to a concentrated mid-span load by minimizing the total potential energy. Individual arches are treated as spatially deforming, and kinematic compatibility relations are derived at the fusion point to couple their deformations. Various deformation symmetries are then exploited to simplify the problem.
  We demonstrate the model's utility by characterizing the force-displacement response of a two-arch MFA, identifying distinct deformation pathways and discussing the pathway transitions that occur during toggling. In particular, we show how the structure switches between symmetric and asymmetric deformation modes as it moves between stable configurations. The generality of the framework is further established through analysis of a three-arch MFA, which exhibits richer coupled deformation behaviour. Nonlinear finite-element simulations and table-top experiments corroborate the analytical predictions, showing close agreement in both equilibrium states and the associated transition responses.

</details>


### [79] [Theory of distribution skewness effect on polydisperse random close packing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30185)
*Vinay Vaibhav,Carmine Anzivino,Alessio Zaccone*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文基于拥挤平衡模型（equilibrium model of crowding）推导出多分散硬球系统随机密堆积密度（$φ_\textrm{RCP}$）的闭式解，揭示了多分散性（$δ$）和偏度（$S$）对堆积密度的影响，并通过修正理论使其满足极端尺寸不对称的已知极限行为，预测了之前未探索的参数空间区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多分散硬球系统的随机密堆积密度是颗粒物质科学中的核心问题，但此前缺乏一个统一的解析框架来系统描述粒径分布的多分散性（polydispersity）和偏度（skewness）对堆积密度的影响。

Method: 采用基于拥挤平衡模型（equilibrium model of crowding）的理论框架，推导出以粒径分布矩（moments of the diameter distribution）表示的$φ_\textrm{RCP}$闭式解（closed-form solution）；通过对二元混合物（binary mixture）的理论分析，将连续分布情形下的$φ_\textrm{RCP}$对偏度的依赖关系映射到一条主曲线（master curve）上；并对理论进行修正使其满足极端尺寸不对称下的已知极限行为。

Result: 对于二元混合物，可在给定偏度下探索$φ_\textrm{RCP}$对多分散性的依赖，或在给定多分散性下探索其对偏度的依赖。多种连续分布下$φ_\textrm{RCP}$对偏度的依赖关系均塌缩到由二元混合物推导出的理论主曲线上。修正后的理论预测不仅与已有的数值结果一致，还预测了$φ_\textrm{RCP}$参数空间中此前未被探索的区域。

Conclusion: 所提出的理论框架能够有效地描述并预测多分散硬球系统的随机密堆积密度，在解析层面统一了不同分布类型下的堆积行为，并为探索极端粒径不对称等情形提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: We investigate the random close packing density, $φ_\textrm{RCP}$, of polydisperse hard sphere systems using a theoretical framework based on the equilibrium model of crowding. We derive a closed-form solution for $φ_\textrm{RCP}$ in terms of the moments of the diameter distribution, enabling an analytical exploration of the effects of polydispersity ($δ$) and skewness ($S$) on packing density. For a binary mixture, it is possible to explore a broader range of dependence of $φ_\textrm{RCP}$ on $δ$ for a given $S$ or on $S$ for a given $δ$. We show that the dependencies of $φ_\textrm{RCP}$ on skewness for a variety of continuous distributions collapse onto a theoretical master curve obtained for the binary mixture case. By correcting the theory so that it obeys known exact limiting behaviours for extreme size asymmetry, our analytical predictions not only agree with previously obtained numerical results, but also predict previously unexplored regions of the $φ_\textrm{RCP}$ parameter space.

### [80] [Geometry-based Discovery of Calcium Battery Cathodes Accelerated by Foundational Machine-Learned Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29029)
*Dereje Bekele Tekliye,Achinthya Krishna Bheemaguli,Gopalakrishnan Sai Gautam*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过结合几何描述符（Voronoi多面体体积）与机器学习（ML）工作流，对Materials Project（MP）数据库中的52,945种结构进行高通量筛选，最终鉴定出37种有前景的钙电池（CB）正极候选材料，其中CaSc₂V₂O₈和CaVSO₄F₃展现出极低的Ca²⁺迁移势垒（E_m），Ca₃(CoO₂)₄等四种候选材料具有热力学稳定的带电态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钙电池（calcium batteries, CBs）作为后锂离子技术具有吸引力，但实际应用受限于缺乏支持可逆Ca²⁺（脱）插层的正极材料，亟需系统筛选新型宿主结构。

Method: 以Voronoi多面体体积（Voronoi polyhedral volume）作为位点兼容性描述符，结合电荷中性、无非Ca移动阳离子、热力学（亚）稳定性、平均电压和基于基础机器学习（machine learning, ML）模型预测的Ca迁移势垒（E_m）等逐级筛选标准，最终对子集候选材料进行密度泛函理论（DFT）的微动弹性带（nudged elastic band, NEB）计算验证。

Result: 从52,945种初始结构中鉴定出37种有前景的Ca正极候选材料，其中CaSc₂V₂O₈和CaVSO₄F₃具有极低的Ca²⁺迁移势垒，Ca₃(CoO₂)₄、Ca₃Mn₄(TeO₆)₂、CaVF₅和CaVSO₄F₃四种候选材料具有热力学稳定的带电态。

Conclusion: 本研究建立的几何描述符和基于ML的筛选工作流是一种可迁移的高通量方法，适用于快速发现电池及其他应用的新型材料。

Abstract: Calcium batteries (CBs) are an attractive post-Li-ion technology, offering the appeal of Ca's natural abundance and high volumetric energy density. However, practical realization of CBs remains limited by the scarcity of positive electrode (cathode) materials that support reversible Ca$^{2+}$ (de)intercalation under electrochemical conditions. To address this challenge, we screen the materials project (MP) database for novel host structures that can intercalate Ca using geometry- and chemistry-based design principles. Specifically, we employ the Voronoi polyhedral volume as a descriptor of site compatibility for hosting Ca in potential frameworks. Further, we down-select candidate structures progressively through criteria including charge neutrality, absence of non-Ca mobile cations, thermodynamic (meta)stability, average voltage, and Ca migration barriers ($E_m$) using foundational machine-learning (ML) models. Subsequently, we validate the ensemble-ML-predicted $E_m$ in a subset of the final candidates using density functional theory based nudged elastic band calculations. Overall, from an initial pool of 52,945 MP structures, our workflow identifies 37 promising Ca cathode candidates, several of which exhibit favorable combinations of thermodynamic (meta)stability, voltage, and Ca-mobility, marking them as strong candidates for synthesis and electrochemical characterization. Particularly, we identify two Ca cathode candidates with markedly low Ca$^{2+}~E_m$ (CaSc$_2$V$_2$O$_8$ and CaVSO$_4$F$_3$), and four cathode candidates with thermodynamically stable charged states (Ca$_3$(CoO$_2$)$_4$, Ca$_3$Mn$_4$(TeO$_6$)$_2$, CaVF$_5$, and CaVSO$_4$F$_3$). Beyond identifying Ca-cathodes, our work establishes geometry-based descriptors and ML-based workflows as transferable methods for high-throughput screening, enabling the rapid discovery of novel materials for battery and other applications.

### [81] [Field-Driven Hybrid Filament Formation Governs Switching in Ta-HfO$_2$-Pt Memristors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29127)
*Ashutosh Krishna Amaram,Aditya Koneru,Subramanian KRS Sankaranarayanan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用带动态电荷转移（dynamic charge transfer）的分子动力学（MD）模拟，揭示了Ta/HfO₂/Pt忆阻器件中钽阳离子（Ta-cation）与氧空位（oxygen vacancy）共同形成导电细丝（conductive filament）的原子机制，阐明了初始氧空位浓度与空间构型对细丝形态的影响，并通过与实验结果的吻合验证了模型的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管实验证据表明Ta/HfO₂/Pt忆阻器件的开关机制涉及氧空位细丝与金属阳离子扩散共同作用的双机制（dual-regime），但金属阳离子迁移的精确原子机制以及氧空位缺陷对导电细丝最终尺寸与形状的影响尚不明确。

Method: 采用带动态电荷转移的分子动力学模拟，对钽阳离子与缺氧细丝（oxygen-deficient filament）的共形成过程进行原子尺度的详细分析。

Result: 开关行为由场驱动（field-driven）的混合型富钽阳离子-缺氧细丝在HfO₂中的形成与断裂所主导；初始氧空位浓度和空间构型显著影响导电细丝的最终形貌与尺寸。

Conclusion: 模拟结果与实验高度吻合，验证了该模型作为理解氧化物忆阻器开关机制（switching mechanism）的稳健框架，并为降低周期间（cycle-to-cycle）与器件间（device-to-device）变异性提供了设计指导。

Abstract: Memristive devices have gained significant attention for their potential in next-generation non-volatile memory and neuromorphic computing architectures. Among emerging candidates, transition metal oxides have proven particularly promising. While the switching mechanism in Ta/HfO$_2$/Pt devices was long attributed solely to oxygen vacancy based filaments, recent experimental evidence suggests a more complex dual-regime: the diffusion of metal cations also contributes to the formation of a conductive bridge. However, the precise atomistic mechanisms governing this metal cation migration remain poorly understood. Additionally, the role of defects such as oxygen vacancies present in the transition metal oxide in determining the final filament size and shape is also not well understood. Here, we employ molecular dynamics (MD) simulations with dynamic charge transfer to provide a detailed analysis of the atomistic mechanisms governing the co-formation of Ta-cation and oxygen-deficient filaments. We clearly show how varying the initial oxygen vacancy concentrations and spatial configurations within the HfO$_2$ matrix influences the final morphology and dimensions of the conductive filament. The switching is governed by field-driven formation and rupture of a hybrid Ta-cation-rich, oxygen-deficient filament in HfO$_2$. Our simulations closely match experiment, validating the model as a robust framework for understanding switching in oxide memristors and guiding designs that reduce cycle-to-cycle and device-to-device variability -- key barriers to high-performance devices.

### [83] [Topological Lifshitz transition-induced bipolarity of anomalous Nernst effect in kagome magnet YCo3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29297)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 上述输运异常可归因于拓扑Lifshitz转变，该转变由Co磁矩演化导致费米能级相对于Weyl节点（Weyl nodes）的移动所驱动；YCo₃是一类原型kagome磁体，温度和磁性可直接调控Weyl节点拓扑与双极型ANE，为在拓扑量子材料中实现磁性调控热电输出开辟了路径。

Abstract: The kagome lattice, renowned for hosting topological band structures and rich magnetic behaviors, offers an exceptional setting to investigate unconventional transport in magnetic topological systems. Controlling the polarity of the anomalous Nernst effect (ANE) is crucial for designing flexible thermoelectric devices, such as thermopiles, where the ability to switch the thermoelectric voltage sign can dramatically enhance energy conversion efficiency and output. Here, we demonstrate such a bipolar ANE in the kagome magnet YCo3, driven by a temperature-induced topological Lifshitz transition. With a Curie temperature TC~225 K, sizable anomalous Hall and Nernst effects emerge below TC. Supported by the first-principles calculations, the AHE and ANE are suggested to be dominated by the intrinsic mechanism. Furthermore, the intrinsic anomalous Hall conductivity exhibits a piecewise-linear dependence on magnetization, with an abrupt slope change near 100 K, consistent with the Karplus-Luttinger mechanism. Concurrently, the anomalous Nernst coefficient SAyx reverses its sign around the same temperature, realizing the crucial bipolarity. These anomalies could be interpreted as a topological Lifshitz transition, enabled by the evolution of Co moments that could shift the Fermi level relative to Weyl nodes. Our work reveals YCo3 as a prototypical kagome magnet where temperature and magnetism directly govern both Weyl node topology and the bipolar ANE, opening a pathway to magnetically control thermoelectric output in topological quantum materials.

Conclusion: 准确预测极性材料在热激发（thermal excitation）下的红外光学性质需要显式处理动态电荷演化（dynamic charge evolution）。

Abstract: Predictive modeling of the infrared dielectric function in polar materials is crucial for thermal management and infrared devices design. Here, we employ a machine-learning neuroevolution potential with dynamic charges (qNEP) combined with Green-Kubo MD to investigate the dynamic charge effect on the infrared dielectric response of rutile TiO$_2$, a material with large Born effective charges (BEC). Our results show that dynamic charge effects become increasingly important at elevated temperatures and are essential for accurately predicting longitudinal optical phonon features and infrared reflectance. This work establishes that accurate prediction of infrared optical properties in polar materials under thermal excitation requires explicit treatment of dynamic charge evolution.

### [85] [Synthesizability, hardness, and stacking order in multicomponent transition metal carbides from machine-learned potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29482)
*Xin Liu,Anirudh Raju Natarajan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过对MACE机器学习原子间势（interatomic potential）进行微调，结合约28,000个密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，预测多组分过渡金属碳化物（multicomponent transition metal carbides）的热力学稳定性和弹性性质。研究筛选了1500多种等原子比成分，发现群组数（group number）主导稳定性和硬度，并识别出一类新的堆垛有序相（stacking-ordered phases），其形成能显著低于无序岩盐或六方结构，实验可行性得到DFT计算支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在约28,000个DFT计算结果上微调MACE机器学习原子间势，覆盖第4-6族过渡金属与碳的成分空间。利用微调后的模型预测形成能和弹性性质，结合自由能模型和基于弹性的硬度代理指标（hardness surrogate），对岩盐（rocksalt）、六方（hexagonal）和hcp三种原型结构中超过1500种等原子比成分进行筛选。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了一个筛选可合成多组分材料并靶向目标性质的框架，在全九组分空间中识别了有前景的碳化物成分，并揭示了一类仅在多组分成分中才能实现的堆垛有序碳化物。

Abstract: Multicomponent transition metal carbides are promising for extreme-environment applications, but identifying compositions that are both synthesizable and hard remains challenging. We fine-tune the MACE machine-learned interatomic potential on approximately 28,000 density functional theory calculations spanning the composition space of groups 4-6 transition metals and carbon to predict the thermodynamic stability and elastic properties of multicomponent carbides. The fine-tuned model achieves formation energy errors of ~ 10 meV/atom for thermodynamically relevant structures with only 20% of the training data. We screen over 1500 equiatomic compositions across rocksalt, hexagonal, and hcp prototypes, combining free energy models with elasticity-based hardness surrogates. Synthesizability predictions at 1500°C agree well with experimental reports for both single-phase and multiphase carbides. The group number of the constituent metals governs both stability and hardness. Free energy contributions from short-range order are small, typically a few meV/atom, indicating that a perfectly disordered solid solution provides a reasonable approximation for high-throughput screening. For compositions mixing group 4/5 and group 6 metals, we identify a new family of stacking-ordered phases with formation energies well below those of disordered rocksalt or hexagonal structures. DFT calculations corroborate these predictions and suggest that stacking-ordered phases should be experimentally accessible in multicomponent carbides. This study provides a framework for screening synthesizable multicomponent materials with target properties, identifies promising carbide compositions across the full nine-component space, and reveals a new class of stacking-ordered carbides accessible only in multicomponent compositions.

### [86] [Alternative origins of polarity in compressively strained SrTiO3-RENiO3 capacitors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29499)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Since its original prediction 25 years ago, room-temperature out-of-plane ferroelectricity in compressively strained SrTiO3 remains an ongoing pursuit. In this work, we investigate the structural, electrical and electromechanical properties of highly strained epitaxial SrTiO3 capacitors with rare earth nickelate electrodes. The SrTiO3 layers experience compressive strains up to -3% and exhibit pronounced tetragonality, comparable to that of bulk PbTiO3. Variable-temperature electrical measurements and room-temperature piezoresponse force microscopy reveal butterfly-shaped capacitance-voltage hysteresis and domain-like electromechanical response typical of ferroelectric materials. However, the overall behavior is inconsistent with a stable ferroelectric state. We therefore propose an alternative mechanism for the observed polarity in our samples based on spatially inhomogeneous internal fields. Our first-principles calculations show that such fields may arise from charge discontinuities between the formally charged NdNiO3 layers and charge-neutral SrTiO3 layers.

### [87] [Finite-temperature micromagnetic model bridging atomic- and macro-scale magnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29617)
*R. Kiefe,J. S. Amaral*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于朗道-利夫希茨方程（Landau-Lifshitz equation）和伯努利微分方程（Bernoulli differential equation）的多尺度有限温度微磁模型（LLBe模型），该模型能够统一描述从低温铁磁态到高温顺磁态的磁性行为，并通过热辅助磁记录（Heat-Assisted Magnetic Recording）模拟展示了其多尺度有限温度能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该模型将Landau-Lifshitz方程与伯努利微分方程（Bernoulli differential equation）耦合，形成Landau-Lifshitz-Bernoulli（LLBe）模型。在高温下精确再现顺磁体的经典麦克斯韦静磁学（Maxwell magnetostatics），在低温下精确再现传统Landau-Lifshitz模型描述的微磁学行为。

Result: LLBe模型经过两个已建立求解器的验证：针对零温微磁学验证使用MUMAX3，针对高温经典静磁学验证使用FEMCE。通过模拟局部加热薄磁轨道上的热辅助磁记录过程，展示了模型的多尺度有限温度能力。

Conclusion: LLBe模型能够直接耦合原子尺度模拟与微磁学，在从低于到高于材料居里温度的有限温度范围内输出一致的体磁性质预测，为多尺度有限温度磁性模拟提供了一种统一建模框架。

Abstract: A multi-scale finite-temperature micromagnetic model is presented, based on the Landau-Lifshitz equation and the Bernoulli differential equation. This model accurately reproduces classic Maxwell magnetostatics of paramagnets for high temperatures and accurately reproduces standard micromagnetics described by the conventional Landau-Lifshitz model in ferromagnets. The Landau-Lifshitz-Bernoulli (LLBe) model can, by design, directly couple atomic-scale simulations with micromagnetics and output consistent predictions of bulk magnetic properties at finite temperatures, from below to above the material's Curie temperature. The LLBe model is validated against established solvers: MUMAX3 for zero-temperature micromagnetics, and FEMCE for high-temperature classic magnetostatics. We present an application of the LLBe model by simulating Heat-Assisted magnetic recording on a thin magnetic track with local heating, demonstrating the multi-scale finite-temperature capabilities of the LLBe.

### [88] [Transition metal (group V) doping induced spin and valley polarization in MoS$_2$ monolayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29718)

Motivation: 二维材料（two-dimensional materials）的掺杂已被证明是调控其电子性质并实现多功能应用的有效手段。然而，如何同时实现磁性、谷极化和压电性等多重耦合自由度，并探索其在量子与纳电子器件中的潜力，仍是需要深入研究的核心问题。

Method: 采用第一性原理（first-principles）计算方法，对MoS₂单层进行第5族过渡金属（V、Nb、Ta）的替代掺杂，系统分析了掺杂后体系的电子结构、磁矩、自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）效应、谷极化以及压电系数等物理性质。

Result: V掺杂诱导了半金属性，总磁矩为0.922 μB；Nb和Ta掺杂则呈现金属性，Ta掺杂总磁矩为0.624 μB。V和Ta掺杂体系中，强自旋-轨道耦合、破缺的反演对称性（inversion symmetry）与结构不对称性共同导致了永久谷极化，其值分别为121 meV和21 meV。此外，所有掺杂体系的压电系数均高于纯净MoS₂。

Conclusion: V掺杂MoS₂同时展现出半金属性、显著谷极化与增强压电性，可作为下一代自旋电子学、谷电子学及压电纳米器件的多功能平台。该研究为在二维材料中工程化耦合的自旋-谷-机械自由度（spin-valley-mechanical degrees of freedom）提供了基础性见解，对先进量子与纳电子应用具有重要意义。

Abstract: Doping in two-dimensional materials has emerged as an effective tool for modulating their electronic properties and thereby enabling their multifunctional applications. In this work, we present a first-principles study on induced effective magnetic moment and metallicity in MoS$_2$ monolayer by substitutional doping of group-5 transition metal (TM) elements -- V, Nb and Ta. From our study, we observe that the V doping induces half-metallicity, whereas metallic characteristics are observed in the case of Nb and Ta doping. Moreover, V and Ta-doped MoS$_2$ monolayers are observed to show total induced magnetic moments of 0.922 and 0.624 $μ_{\rm B}$, respectively. Importantly, the combined effects of strong spin-orbit coupling (SOC), broken inversion symmetry, and structural asymmetry is observed to lead to a permanent valley polarization in the V- and Ta-MoS$_2$ systems. In particular, we observed a valley polarization of 121 and 21 meVs for V and Ta-doped MoS$_2$, respectively. Furthermore, an enhanced piezoelectric coefficient for the doped systems is observed compared to pristine MoS$_2$. Notably, the simultaneous presence of half-metallicity, substantial valley polarization, and enhanced piezoelectricity in V-doped MoS$_2$ establishes this system as a promising multifunctional platform for next-generation spintronic, valleytronic, and piezoelectric nanodevices. Overall, our findings provide fundamental insights into engineering coupled spin-valley-mechanical degrees of freedom in two-dimensional materials for advanced quantum and nanoelectronic applications.

</details>


### [89] [Spin-Orbit Coupling Effects on the Structural and Electronic Properties of Planar Pentagonal p-MS$_{2}$ (M = Si, Ge, and Pb)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29730)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）对二维平面五边形材料的结构与电子性质具有重要影响，但相关机制尚不明确，有必要系统研究 SOC 在 p-MS₂ 体系中的作用。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算，并结合 j 分辨（j-resolved）的总角动量（total angular momentum）轨道分析，系统考察 SOC 效应。

Conclusion: SOC 驱动的结构及电子态重构为理解平面五边形硫族化物 p-MS₂ 提供了新见解，p-PbS₂ 可能成为气体传感（gas-sensing）领域的潜在候选材料。

Abstract: Spin-orbit coupling (SOC) plays an important role in determining the structural and electronic properties of recently proposed two-dimensional planar pentagonal materials. In this work, density functional theory calculations are employed to investigate SOC effects in p-MS$_{2}$ systems (M = Si, Ge, and Pb). Our results indicate that the p-SiS$_{2}$ structure is likely unstable, except for p-GeS$_{2}$ and p-PbS$_{2}$. A detailed j-resolved (total angular momentum) orbital analysis reveals that SOC enhances electronic localization, leading to a slight structural contraction and a reconstruction of electronic states near the Fermi level, this effect becoming stronger for heavier M atoms. While p-GeS$_{2}$ remains metallic, SOC drives a metal-semiconductor transition in p-PbS$_{2}$ and opening a quasi-direct band gap of about 0.475 eV. In addition, the conduction band minimum state of p-PbS$_{2}$ exhibits pronounced anisotropy along the S-S bonds. These findings provide insight into SOC-driven structural and electronic reconstruction in planar pentagonal chalcogenides p-MS$_{2}$ and suggest that p-PbS$_{2}$ may be a promising candidate for gas-sensing applications.

### [90] [Breaking Bipartite and Time Reversal Symmetries by Fusing Porphine Unit in-between two Zigzag-edge Graphene Nanoribbons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29817)
*R. K. Rohit,Jisvin Sam,Sudipta Dutta*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文研究由两个锯齿形石墨烯纳米带（zigzag-edge graphene nanoribbon）与一个卟啉环（porphine ring）杂化组成的准一维结构。该结构产生两种近简并基态——半导体反铁磁态与导电铁磁态（后者中多数自旋与少数自旋具有相反的不等费米速度），且卟啉环中嵌入过渡金属原子可降低两者能量差。该体系的铁磁态因多数自旋通道对边缘无序不敏感，有望应用于双自旋过滤器件。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过构建两个锯齿形石墨烯纳米带中间融合一个卟啉环的杂化结构模型，分析其电子结构；并在卟啉空腔中嵌入不同过渡金属原子，研究其对基态性质的影响。

Result: 该杂化结构产生两种近简并基态：半导体反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）态与导电铁磁（ferromagnetic）态，其中多数自旋与少数自旋具有相反且不等的费米速度，反铁磁态稳定性略高。卟啉环引起的破缺二分对称性是这些基态的来源。嵌入过渡金属原子可减少两者能量差，但基本不改变电子性质。卟啉环畸变四方平面配体场使d轨道分裂，产生高自旋基态并打破全局时间反演对称性（time reversal symmetry, $\mathcal{T}$）。

Conclusion: 铁磁基态中多数自旋与少数自旋具有相反的费米速度，且导电的多数自旋通道对边缘无序的敏感性较低，使得这类准一维杂化结构在双自旋过滤器件（dual spin-filtering device）中具有应用前景。

Abstract: Hybrid structure of two zigzag-edge graphene nanoribbons with a fused porphine ring in between, results in two distinct nearly degenerate ground states: a semiconducting antiferromagnetic state and a conducting ferromagnetic state with unequal and opposite Fermi velocities of majority and minority spins, the former having slightly higher stability. Such ground states result from the broken bipartite symmetry induced by the porphine ring. The incorporation of different transition metal atoms in the porphine cavity reduces their energy difference but keeps their electronic properties mostly unchanged. The splitting of the $d$-orbitals in the distorted square-planar ligand field of porphine produces a high spin ground state that breaks the global time reversal symmetry ($\mathcal{T}$). The opposite Fermi velocities of the majority and minority spins in the ferromagnetic ground state and lower sensitivity of the conducting majority spin channel to the edge disorder, make this class of quasi-one-dimensional hybrid structures promising for dual spin-filtering device applications.

Abstract: The hydrogen evolution reaction (HER) is central to sustainable hydrogen production, and nitrogen coordinated dual atom catalysts (DACs) offer a promising route to noble metal activity at low cost. ### [92] [Optical Cooling of Nuclear Spins in a CdTe/CdZnTe Quantum Well: The Impact of Kinetic Local Fields on Cooling Efficiency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29855)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究光学冷却核自旋（optical cooling of nuclear spins）的效率随外磁场的变化关系，并验证是否存在最优外磁场。

Method: 通过实验测量CdTe/CdZnTe量子阱中核自旋光学冷却效率与外磁场的依赖关系；提出一种用于测量动力学局域场（kinetic local field）$B_{KL}$的实验技术；并与理论计算进行比较，理论计算中考虑了Cd和Te核自旋的间接自旋-自旋相互作用（indirect spin-spin interactions）及其显著不同的超精细常数（hyperfine constants）。

Result: 存在一个最优外磁场用于光学冷却，该最优场被关联于$B_{KL}$。对样品测得$B_{KL}=1.0\pm0.4$ G，且该值与电子极化率（electron polarization）和泵浦功率（pump power）无关。理论计算$B_{KL}=0.7$ G，与实验结果吻合良好。此外，估算了CdTe中Cd和Te磁性同位素的超精细常数。

Conclusion: 光学冷却核自旋的最优外磁场可由动力学局域场$B_{KL}$描述；所提出的测量技术可有效测定$B_{KL}$；间接自旋-自旋相互作用和超精细常数的差异对于理解核自旋动力学至关重要。

Abstract: The efficiency of optical cooling of nuclear spins in a CdTe/CdZnTe quantum well is investigated as a function of an external magnetic field. Our results confirm that there is indeed an optimal external magnetic field for optical cooling. We associate it with the kinetic local field $B_{KL}$ defined by the heating rate of the spin-spin reservoir due to the fluctuations of the hyperfine interaction. We also propose an experimental technique for measuring $B_{KL}$. For our sample we find that $B_{KL}=1.0\pm0.4$ G and it is independent of the electron polarization and pump power. The measured values of the kinetic local fields are in good agreement with a theoretical calculation $B_{KL} = 0.7$ G, taking into account indirect spin-spin interactions of Cd and Te nuclear spins and their considerably different hyperfine constants. The hyperfine constants of the magnetic isotopes of Cd and Te in CdTe are estimated.

Abstract: Nontrivial topological spin-textures, such as skyrmions, merons, bimerons, and skyrmioniums, are envisioned as robust building blocks for future memory and logic devices. Controllable transformations between these states require a quantum-mechanical description of electronic degrees of freedom and atomic-scale insight beyond existing phenomenological models. Here, we report an atomic-scale investigation of topological phase transitions and their protection in the two-dimensional van der Waals ferromagnet Fe$_3$GeTe$_2$ (FGT) using a combined experimental-theoretical approach. Synchrotron-based Fourier transform holography directly images labyrinth domains, isolated skyrmions, mixed labyrinth-skyrmion phases, and skyrmion bags with high spatial resolution. We compare these observations to simulations based on an electronic lattice Hamiltonian that captures both metallicity and relativistic spin-orbit coupling in FGT. By systematically exploring a broad range of temperatures and magnetic fields, we map the mechanisms governing topological transitions and their stability. This sequential-integrated experimental-theoretical framework advances understanding of spin-texture interactions and enables precise control of external tuning parameters. Our results establish a platform for creating, stabilizing, and manipulating topological states, paving the way for engineered spin-texture transitions in next-generation spintronic technologies.

### [94] [Carrier Localization in Pnictogen-Based Chalcohalides from Defect-Bound Hot Polarons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29925)
*Xiaoyu Guo,Junzhi Ye,Cibrán Lopez Alvarez,Maciej Oskar Liedke,Maik Butterling,Mutibah Alanazi,Yi-Teng Huang,Jiajie Wu,Zhilong Zhang,Lars Van Turnhout,Yorrick Boeije,Bofeng Xue,Qingyu Wang,Hugh Lohan,Seán R. Kavanagh,Andreas Wagner,Eric Hirschmann,Robert A. Taylor,Akshay Rao,Edgardo Saucedo,Claudio Cazorla,Robert L. Z. Hoye*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文揭示了缺陷诱导的 extrinsic 载流子局域化机制：在原本无本征载流子局域化的 pnictogen 硫卤化物 BiSBr 中，合成或后处理引入的空位通过形成缺陷束缚的热极化子（defect-bound hot polarons），使热载流子偏离冷却至能带边缘的路径，导致可移动载流子数量减少，从而解释了该类材料光伏性能受限于载流子局域化的根本原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: pnictogen 基太阳能吸收材料虽是有毒铅卤钙钛矿（lead-halide perovskites, LHPs）的有前景替代品，但其性能严重受限于载流子局域化（carrier localization）。先前研究仅考虑了本征（intrinsic）因素，未涉及缺陷对载流子动力学的影响。本文旨在弥补这一空白，系统考察缺陷对冷载流子和热载流子的作用。

Method: 以结构上一维的 pnictogen 硫卤化物 BiSBr 为研究对象，通过理论分析，考察合成或后处理过程中引入的空位缺陷对激发态载流子行为的影响，重点关注缺陷束缚的热极化子（defect-bound hot polarons）的形成机制。

Result: BiSBr 本征上不存在载流子局域化现象；但空位缺陷会通过形成缺陷束缚的热极化子（即激发态载流子与局域缺陷诱导的振动模式强耦合）导致显著的 extrinsinc 自陷（self-trapping）。这些超带隙缺陷态（above-gap defect states）使热载流子偏离冷却至带边的路径，从而耗尽可移动载流子群体。

Conclusion: 缺陷束缚的热极化子在介导 extrinsic 载流子局域化中起关键作用；缺陷、晶格耦合与激发态载流子输运之间的相互作用为设计高效的类钙钛矿太阳能吸收材料提供了新的机理见解。

Abstract: Pnictogen-based solar absorbers have gained prominence as promising nontoxic and stable alternatives to lead-halide perovskites (LHPs), but are severely limited by carrier localization, preventing their performance from approaching those of LHPs. Recent efforts have uncovered routes to overcome carrier localization, but these early efforts only considered intrinsic factors. Herein, we push beyond these limited early efforts, examining the role of defects, not only on cold carriers but also hot carriers. Focusing on the structurally one-dimensional pnictogen chalcohalide BiSBr, we find that whilst this material intrinsically does not exhibit carrier localization, vacancies introduced during synthesis or post-treatment lead to pronounced extrinsic self-trapping via the formation of defect-bound hot polarons-excited charge-carriers strongly coupled to local defect-induced vibrational modes. These above-gap defect states divert hot carriers from cooling to the band edge, thus depleting the mobile carrier population. Our findings establish the key role of defect-bound hot polarons in mediating extrinsic localization and offer new mechanistic insights into the interplay between defects, lattice coupling, and excited-state charge-carrier transport, which are critical to designing efficient perovskite-inspired solar absorbers.

### [95] [Prototype-Guided Latent Alignment for Data-Efficient Fine-Tuning of Molecular Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29969)
*Rushikesh Pawar,Harshit Rawat,Ayush Kumar,Phani Motamarri*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于原型对齐（prototype-based alignment）的方法，用于机器学习原子间势（MLIPs）的数据高效微调，通过在低数据（low-data）条件下将目标域原子的能量贡献对齐到源域原型，缓解过参数化图神经网络（GNN）在小样本场景下的过拟合问题，在rMD17和SPICE基准上能量MAE最多降低18%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模预训练的基础模型（foundation models）在预测材料性质时难以泛化到分布外（out-of-distribution, OOD）目标系统，而微调（fine-tuning）虽为标准补救手段，但生成密度泛函理论（DFT）标记数据的成本高昂，导致数据稀缺（data-scarce）条件下过参数化GNN过拟合严重，目标域性能下降。

Method: 提出一种基于原型对齐的方法：通过潜表示（latent representation）对具有相似化学环境的原子进行分组，识别源域与目标域之间的局部结构相似性；将目标域每个原子的能量贡献对齐到其对应的源域原型（prototype），引入归纳偏置（inductive bias），使微调后的表示锚定在预训练结构上，在不限制目标化学体系的前提下促进已学习交互的有效复用并改善泛化。

Result: 在rMD17基准上采用等变MACE（equivariant MACE）和不变SchNet（invariant SchNet）进行不同数据预算下的评估，并扩展至SPICE数据集上的MACE-OFF基础模型。所提方法在低数据（low-data）场景下持续提升预测精度，能量平均绝对误差（energy MAE）相较标准微调基线最多降低18%。

Conclusion: 该原型对齐方法能够在数据稀缺条件下有效提升机器学习原子间势的微调效果，为复杂材料体系的泛化提供了一种轻量级且无需强假设的解决方案。

Abstract: Machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) have transformed materials discovery by leveraging graph neural networks (GNNs) to predict material properties with near density functional theory (DFT) accuracy. While large-scale pretrained foundation models offer transferable baseline representations, they frequently struggle to generalise to out-of-distribution (OOD) target systems -- a common challenge in modelling complex or chemically diverse materials. Fine-tuning is the standard remedy, but the high cost of generating DFT-labelled configurations confines adaptation to data-scarce regimes, where over-parameterised GNNs amplify overfitting and degrade target-domain performance. To address this, we propose a prototype-based alignment approach for data-efficient fine-tuning of MLIPs. Our method identifies local structural similarities between the source and target domains by grouping atoms with analogous chemical environments based on their latent representations. Each target-domain atom's energy contribution is aligned to its source-domain prototype, introducing an inductive bias that anchors fine-tuned representations to the pretrained structure, encouraging effective reuse of learned interactions and improving generalisation without restrictive assumptions on the target chemistry. We evaluate our method on the rMD17 benchmark using equivariant MACE and invariant SchNet across varying data budgets, and extend evaluation to the MACE-OFF foundation models on the SPICE dataset. Our approach consistently improves predictive accuracy in the low-data regime, reducing energy MAE by up to 18% over standard fine-tuning baselines.

</details>


### [96] [Magnetic precession induced spin accumulation in collinear antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30016)
*Q. Xue,J. Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过微扰理论、群论对称性分析、低能及第一性原理模拟，提出在反铁磁半导体中，靠近平衡磁轴的磁进动可在相反磁子晶格上产生均匀和交错的有限自旋极化，并识别了对称性约束与响应类型，发现一种隐藏的自旋积累模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在反铁磁（antiferromagnetic, AFM）中产生并表征均匀与交错自旋极化（staggered spin polarization）是反铁磁自旋电子学技术的关键挑战之一。现有方法多依赖于异质结（heterojunction）结构，存在晶格失配问题。

Method: 采用微扰理论（perturbative theory）、群论对称性分析（group-theoretical symmetry analysis）、低能模拟（low energy simulation）及第一性原理（ab initio）模拟相结合的方法进行研究。通过审查所有对称性保护的消磁矩群（vanishing magnetic moment groups），并重点关注宇称-时间（parity-time, PT）不变群，识别对称性约束条件。

Result: 揭示了反铁磁半导体中一种隐藏的自旋积累模式（hidden spin accumulation mode）。发现该响应无需异质结结构，可消除结区晶格失配问题；明确了响应的类场（fieldlike）和类阻尼（dampinglike）特征。

Conclusion: 电门控场（electric gate field）和Floquet光修饰（Floquet light-dressing）可有效调控该自旋极化响应，为反铁磁自旋电子学器件的实现提供了新途径。

Abstract: Generating and characterizing uniform and staggered spin polarization in antiferromagnets is one of the key challenges for antiferromagnetic spintronic technology. Here, we perform perturbative theory, group-theoretical symmetry analysis, low energy and ab initio simulations to propose that the magnetic precession near the equilibrium magnetic axis could generate finite uniform and staggered spin polarization at the opposite magnetic sublattices (referring to total magnetic and Néel vector generation) in a single AFM semiconductors. This response does not require the heterojunction setup and could eliminate the lattice mismatch issues at the junction. Through scrutinizing all symmetrically-protected vanishing magnetic moment groups and especially focusing on parity-time (PT ) invariant groups, we identify the symmetry constraints that describe the staggered spin accumulation responses, and disclose their fieldlike and dampinglike characters. This unravels a hidden spin accumulation mode in AFM semiconductors. Furthermore, we simulate such an effect using a perturbative approach and suggest that electric gate field and Floquet light-dressing can effectively manipulate these responses.

### [97] [Towards exascale fully relativistic pseudopotential density functional theory calculations enabled by mixed-precision computation and compressed-communication using residual based subspace iteration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30128)
*Nikhil Kodali,Gourab Panigrahi,Nishant Gupta,Kartick Ramakrishnan,Sundaresan G,Rudra Panch,Sambit Das,Vishwas Rao,Phani Motamarri*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套以GPU为中心的、用于非共线磁性与自旋轨道耦合密度泛函理论（NC-SOC DFT）的高性能计算框架，通过结合有限元离散、基于残差的切比雪夫滤波子空间迭代、无矩阵策略、混合精度计算与块浮点压缩MPI通信，以及能带划分算法，实现了在百亿亿次架构上对多达10万电子体系的完全相对论赝势DFT模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非共线磁性（noncollinear magnetism）与自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）对于具有显著相对论效应和磁阻挫（magnetic frustration）的第一性原理（ab initio）材料模拟至关重要，但它们在立方缩放（cubic-scaling）的密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）中引入了每电子双分量波函数（2-component wavefunctions），导致本征问题规模大幅增加，计算成本显著上升。因此需要一种高效的计算框架来降低这一开销。

Method: 该框架包含五项关键技术：(i) 求解有限元（finite-element, FE）离散化DFT方程的算法改进；(ii) 基于残差的切比雪夫滤波子空间迭代（residual-based Chebyshev filtered subspace iteration, R-ChFSI），对不精确的矩阵-向量积具有容忍性，用于求解稀疏广义本征问题；(iii) 无矩阵（matrix-free）策略加速有限元泊松求解器；(iv) R-ChFSI使能的混合精度计算，结合块浮点（block floating-point）压缩MPI通信，压缩比超过4倍，在保持双精度鲁棒性的同时减少计算与数据搬运成本；(v) 通信高效的能带划分（band-partitioning）算法以提升可扩展性。

Result: 数值结果表明，该方法在百亿亿次（exascale）架构上实现了更快的求解时间（time-to-solution）和优异的可扩展性（scaling），能够对多达100,000个电子的体系进行完全相对论赝势DFT模拟。

Conclusion: 所提出的GPU中心高性能框架有效克服了NC-SOC DFT的高计算成本难题，为大规模相对论效应材料模拟提供了可行的计算方案。

Abstract: Noncollinear (NC) magnetism and spin-orbit coupling (SOC) are indispensable for predictive ab initio materials simulations with pronounced relativistic effects and magnetic frustration, yet they significantly increase the cost of cubic-scaling density functional theory (DFT) by introducing complex 2-component wavefunctions per electron and consequently much larger eigenproblems. We present a GPU-centric high-performance framework for NC-SOC DFT that combines: (i) algorithmic advances for solving finite-element (FE) discretized DFT equations; (ii) residual-based Chebyshev filtered subspace iteration (R-ChFSI), tolerant to inexact matrix-vector products, for the resulting sparse generalized eigenproblem; (iii) a matrix-free strategy for accelerating FE Poisson solver; (iv) R-ChFSI-enabled mixed-precision computation with block floating-point compressed MPI communication at compression ratios over 4x, preserving double-precision robustness while reducing compute and data movement costs; and (v) a communication efficient band-partitioning algorithm to improve scalability. Numerical results demonstrate improved time-to-solution and excellent scaling on exascale architectures, enabling fully relativistic pseudopotential DFT simulations of up to 100,000 electrons.

### [98] [What drives performance in molecular MPNNs? An operator-level factorial benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30195)
*Panyu Jiao,Shuizhou Chen,Yiheng Shen,Yuyang Wang,Runhai Ouyang,Wei Xie*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过算子级析因基准测试，将二维分子消息传递神经网络（MPNN）分解为三类算子（消息种子初始化、节点-边融合、节点更新），在84种配置下系统评估了各算子对分子属性预测性能的影响，发现消息构建（而非更新复杂度）是性能差异的主因，并提出基于拼接的混合策略在区分化学异质原子和抗过平滑方面具有优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MPNN在分子属性预测中被广泛使用，但其作为整体架构难以识别具体消息传递算子对性能的影响，缺乏系统性的算子级分析方法。

Method: 将二维分子MPNN分解为消息种子初始化（message-seed initialization）、节点-边融合（node-edge fusion）和节点更新（node update）三类算子，构建84种配置，在10个MoleculeNet数据集上统一实验设置和统计分析。

Result: 性能差异主要与消息构建相关而非更新复杂度；消息种子初始化对回归和分类均有显著族级效应；节点-边融合对回归有显著效应且拼接混合优于Hadamard门控；节点更新无统计显著性；拼接混合能更好区分化学异质原子并抵抗过平滑；按分类/回归选取的配置在8/10个数据集中排名数值最优。

Conclusion: 研究提供了分子MPNN的经验设计启发，将模型设计从整体架构搜索转变为对化学信息进入消息传递管道的环节和方式进行精准评估。

Abstract: Message-passing neural networks (MPNNs) are widely used for molecular property prediction, but their deployment as monolithic architectures makes it difficult to identify how specific message-passing operators affect performance. We present an operator-level factorial benchmark that decomposes 2D molecular MPNNs into the three families of message-seed initialization, node-edge fusion, and node update operators. The resulting 84 configurations are benchmarked on ten MoleculeNet datasets under a shared experimental setup and statistical analysis protocol. Across this controlled design, performance variation is associated primarily with message construction rather than update complexity. Message-seed initialization shows significant family-level effects for both regression and classification, node-edge fusion shows a significant family-level effect for regression with descriptive advantages for concatenation-based mixing, and the update family shows no statistically supported effect for either endpoint family. A representation probe into the Quinethazone molecule further demonstrates that concatenation-based mixing can better differentiate chemically distinct heteroatoms and withstand oversmoothing than Hadamard gating. Representative configurations selected separately for classification and regression recover competitive performance relative to established molecular graph neural network (GNN) baselines, ranking numerically best on eight of ten benchmark datasets. These empirical results are interpreted through concise mechanistic analyses of representative node-edge fusion and update operators. Our findings provide empirical design heuristics for molecular MPNNs by turning model design from a search over monolithic architectures into a targeted assessment of where and how chemical information enters the message-passing pipeline.

</details>


### [99] [Role of structure and charge trapping on the bipolaron formation and magnetic-field response of gated conjugated polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30196)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 观察到普遍的正磁电阻；模拟表明双极化子优先形成于非晶区的短共轭片段上；不同聚合物间的比较显示电荷捕获增强伴随磁电阻增大；模型表明电荷陷阱可提升双极化子密度。

Conclusion: 电荷捕获促进双极化子形成，从而增强磁电阻；该研究阐明了共轭聚合物中磁电阻、电荷捕获与双极化子形成之间的内在关联。

Abstract: Conjugated polymers exhibit unique spin-dependent phenomena arising from weak yet critical hyperfine interactions. Understanding these spin effects, particularly the spin-dependent formation and decay of correlated spin pairs, is important for advancing both organic electronics and polymer-based spintronics. Intrinsic magnetic-field responses such as magnetoresistance have primarily been investigated in diode architectures, where electrons and holes coexist. However, such systems are less suitable for probing bipolaron formation in unipolar transport, and the relationship between polymer structure and bipolaron formation in lightly doped polymers remains unclear. Here, we systematically investigate intrinsic magnetoresistance in representative conjugated polymers using field-effect transistors and observe a generally positive magnetoresistance. First-principles simulations reveal that bipolarons preferentially form on short conjugated segments associated with amorphous regions. Moreover, comparisons across these polymers show that enhanced charge trapping correlates with stronger magnetoresistance, implying promoted bipolaron formation. Bipolaron-incorporated energylevel-alignment modeling near metal/polymer interfaces suggests that charge traps can increase the bipolaron density.

### [100] [Exploring the Origins of Anti-Ambipolarity in BBL Polymer: Links to Redox Chemistry, Electronic Structure, and Structural Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30270)
*Maryam Ghotbi,Alejandro Aviles,Perla B. Balbuena*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算（密度泛函理论、从头算分子动力学、含时密度泛函理论和Marcus理论）研究了共轭梯形聚合物BBL在电子转移过程中的物理化学性质，揭示了其非线性响应的反双极性行为源于奇偶交替的能隙变化模式，证实了电导率钟形曲线源自BBL的电子结构与超分子组织。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究者希望解释共轭梯形聚合物BBL在电子转移过程中表现出的反双极性（anti-ambipolar）行为的内在物理化学起源，即该材料在特定器件架构下非线性响应背后的根本原因。

Method: 采用基于第一性原理（first principles）的理论与计算方法，包括密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）优化、从头算分子动力学（ab initio molecular dynamics, AIMD）、含时密度泛函理论（time-dependent DFT）以及Marcus理论（Marcus theory）分析。

Result: BBL的氧化还原响应并非简单的单调变化，而是呈现交替的奇偶模式（odd/even pattern），其中能隙（gap）先缩小后重新打开，并在高电荷态下接近无带隙（near-gapless）行为。

Conclusion: BBL电导率的钟形曲线（bell-shaped conductivity）起源于其基本电子结构（electronic structure）和超分子组织（supramolecular organization），而非单纯的外在器件因素。

Abstract: We examine the intrinsic physical-chemical properties of the conjugated ladder-type polymer poly(benzimidazobenzophenanthroline) (BBL) in response to electron transfer. We aim at explaining the origin of the anti-ambipolar behavior behind the observed BBL nonlinear response associated with specific device architectures. To elucidate this point, we use theory and computation based on first principles, including density functional theory optimizations, ab initio molecular dynamics, time-dependent DFT, and Marcus-theory analysis. Our results reveal that this redox response is not simply monotonic but follows an alternating odd/even pattern in which gap narrowing and reopening occur sequentially before near-gapless behavior emerges at high charging. Converging theoretical evidence in this work demonstrates that bell shaped conductivity in BBL originates in its fundamental electronic structure and supramolecular organization.

### [101] [Inverse scattering for the linear system associated with the coupled Gerdjikov--Ivanov equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28856)
*Ramazan Ercan*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类与导数非线性薛定谔（DNLS）III系统（即Gerdjikov–Ivanov系统）相关的一阶线性常微分方程组的正散射和逆散射问题，建立了类似于AKNS系统的Marchenko积分方程，并基于反射系数和束缚态信息的矩阵三元组表示恢复了势函数。利用时间演化的散射数据，可得到Gerdjikov–Ivanov系统的解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对与可积系统DNLS III（Gerdjikov–Ivanov系统）相关联的一阶线性常微分方程组，系统地分析其正散射与逆散射问题，为求解该非线性可积系统提供基于散射反演的理论框架。

Method: 正散射问题中分析了Jost解和散射系数的性质，并使用矩阵三元组（matrix triplet pair）表示束缚态极点及相关归一化常数。逆散射问题中建立了一个线性积分方程组，其核函数和非齐次项由反射系数（reflection coefficients）的傅里叶变换及表示束缚态信息的矩阵三元组确定，该方程组对应于AKNS系统的Marchenko积分方程（Marchenko integral equations）。

Result: 建立了与DNLS III系统对应的Marchenko积分方程系统，并证明了从该积分方程的解中可以恢复出两个势函数。利用时间演化的反射系数和矩阵三元组，对应的势函数对给出了Gerdjikov–Ivanov系统的一个解。

Conclusion: 本文为Gerdjikov–Ivanov系统提供了完整的正散射与逆散射分析，建立了适用于任意数量及任意阶束缚态的Marchenko积分方程框架，从而为该系统提供了基于散射数据的求解方法。

Abstract: We consider a certain first-order linear system of ordinary differential equations, and we analyze the direct and inverse scattering problems for that linear system. The linear system involves two potentials in the Schwartz class, and those potentials linearly depend on the spectral parameter. This linear system is related to the integrable system of nonlinear partial differential equations known as the DNLS (derivative nonlinear Schrödinger) system III, which is also known as the Gerdjikov--Ivanov system. When analyzing the direct problem, we describe the pertinent properties of the Jost solutions and the scattering coefficients. The bound states poles and the associated normalization constants are represented via a matrix triplet pair, enabling us to deal with any number of bound states and any multiplicities. The inverse scattering problem comprises the determination of the two potentials when the reflection coefficients and the bound-state information are available. To solve the inverse problem, we establish a linear system of integral equations where the kernel and nonhomogeneous term are determined by the Fourier transforms of the reflection coefficients and the matrix triplet pair representing the bound-state information. This system of linear integral equations is the counterpart of the system of Marchenko integral equations available for the AKNS system associated with the integrable NLS (nonlinear Schrödinger) system. We recover the potentials from the solution of our established Marchenko integral system. When we use the time-evolved reflection coefficients and the time-evolved matrix triplets, the corresponding time-evolved potential pair yields a solution of the Gerdjikov--Ivanov system.

</details>


### [102] [Transitions with the same energy difference in the Bohr model of the hydrogen atom](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29134)
*Matthias W. Reinsch*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于玻尔氢原子模型，利用高斯整数（Gaussian integers）等范数与布拉马古普塔-斐波那契恒等式（Brahmagupta–Fibonacci identity），系统地找到了所有具有相同能量差的跃迁对，并利用费马定理（Fermat’s theorem）证明了超过三个能级的等频跃迁级联（cascade）不可能存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在玻尔氢原子模型中，存在特殊的跃迁对具有相同的能量差，已有文献（Do & Phan, arXiv:2010.08338）对此进行了系统处理。本文旨在发展一种更简洁的方法，以完整地找出所有这样的跃迁对，并进一步分析等频跃迁的级联结构。

Method: 采用高斯整数（Gaussian integers）的等范数（equal norms）条件，结合布拉马古普塔-斐波那契恒等式（Brahmagupta–Fibonacci identity），构建了一种简单的代数方法，用于枚举所有能量差相等的跃迁对。对于级联分析，则运用了费马定理（Fermat’s theorem）来限制级联的长度。

Result: 该方法能够系统地找出所有满足等能量差条件的跃迁对。对于等频跃迁级联（cascade of equal-frequency transitions），证明了超过三个能级的级联是不可能的。

Conclusion: 基于高斯整数和布拉马古普塔-斐波那契恒等式的方法为玻尔氢原子模型中的等能量差跃迁提供了完整的分类方案；费马定理则严格限制了等频级联的最大长度。

Abstract: In the Bohr model of the hydrogen atom, the energy levels are a negative constant divided by the square of the level number. It is well known that special pairs of transitions exist that have the same energy difference, and a systematic treatment of this is given in the paper by Do and Phan (arXiv:2010.08338). In this paper we describe a simple method (using equal norms of Gaussian integers, and the Brahmagupta--Fibonacci identity) for finding all such pairs of transitions. We also analyze cascades of equal-frequency transitions, and use a theorem due to Fermat to show that cascades with more than three levels are not possible.

</details>


### [103] [A Lorentzian construction of timelike Liouville field theory on the cylinder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29203)
*Sourav Chatterjee*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在柱面时空上构造了时间型Liouville场论（timelike Liouville field theory）的Lorentzian关联函数，建立了从重整化有限体积环面正则化到无穷体积Euclidean关联函数的构造，证明了解析延拓与Lorentzian边界值的显式围道积分公式，并验证了时空分离的顶点算符的交换性（locality）。在整数电荷扇区内，该构造给出了一个有序$*$-代数上的真空泛函，支持一种不具有正定性的AQFT型量子化，获得了局部代数、带不定Hermite形式的拓扑空间以及连续循环表示等结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间型Liouville场论是正曲率二维量子引力（positive curvature two-dimensional quantum gravity）的候选模型，但其在数学上可控的Lorentzian表述长期以来未能建立。本文旨在填补这一空白，在柱面$\mathbb{R}\times \mathbb{S}^1$上构造该理论的严格数学框架。

Method: 从重整化的有限体积环面正则化出发，构造无穷体积Euclidean关联函数；随后证明时间变量上的解析延拓（analytic continuation），并通过显式围道积分公式（contour formulas）确定Lorentzian边界值。在整数电荷扇区（integer screening sector）内，对重整化指数型可观测量（renormalized exponential observables）的自然代数进行操作。

Result: 获得了整数电荷场$e^{2nbφ}$生成的可观测量在Lorentzian理论中的精确关联函数，证明了时空分离的顶点算符（vertex operators）的交换性。这些Lorentzian期望值定义了有序$*$-代数上的真空泛函，并支撑一个不具有正定性（positivity）的AQFT型量子化，具体包括：等调局部代数（isotone local algebras）、带有非退化Hermite形式的完备局部凸空间$\mathcal H$及其稠密代数子空间$\mathcal H_0$、连续循环表示、算子拓扑下闭的表示局部代数、柱面平移的连续线性同胚作用，以及表示局部网的交换性。

Conclusion: 该构造未产生通常意义下的Hilbert空间或Haag-Kastler局部von Neumann代数网（Haag-Kastler net of local von Neumann algebras），但表明Euclidean-to-Lorentzian和代数重构机制在这一柱面时间型Liouville理论的不正定设定下仍可实质性保留。

Abstract: Timelike Liouville field theory is a candidate model for positive curvature two-dimensional quantum gravity, but a mathematically controlled Lorentzian formulation has remained elusive. In this paper we construct the theory on the cylinder $\mathbb{R}\times \mathbb{S}^1$ in the integer screening sector for a natural algebra of renormalized exponential observables. Starting from a renormalized finite-volume torus regularization, we construct infinite-volume Euclidean correlation functions, prove analytic continuation in the time variables, and identify the resulting Lorentzian boundary values by explicit contour formulas. This yields exact Lorentzian correlators for a natural class of exponential observables. We then prove locality: spacelike separated vertex operators commute in the Lorentzian theory. For smeared observables generated by the integer-charge fields $e^{2nbφ}$, these Lorentzian expectation values define a vacuum functional on an ordered $*$-algebra and support an AQFT-type quantization without positivity. More precisely, we obtain isotone local algebras, a complete locally convex space $\mathcal H$ with dense algebraic subspace $\mathcal H_0$ carrying a nondegenerate Hermitian form (shown to be indefinite for $b<8^{-1/2}$), a continuous cyclic representation, operator-topologically closed represented local algebras, an action of cylinder translations by continuous linear homeomorphisms, and locality for the represented local net. The construction does not produce a Hilbert space or a Haag-Kastler net of local von Neumann algebras in the usual sense, but it shows that a substantial part of the Euclidean-to-Lorentzian and algebraic reconstruction mechanism survives in this nonpositive setting for timelike Liouville theory on the cylinder.

### [104] [Connection Factorization in Constrained Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29241)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在利用联络分解方法澄清曲线与曲面上约束量子运动的基本数学结构，特别是拉普拉斯算子的一阶部分与正交标架的达布旋转联络（Darboux rotational connection）之间的内在联系。

Method: 采用联络分解方法（connection factorization methods），通过正交活动标架（orthonormal moving frames）推导平面曲线、空间曲线及嵌入曲面的有效几何贡献；利用结构方程对狄拉克约化（Dirac reductions）进行分析。

Result: 发现拉普拉斯算子的一阶部分与达布旋转联络等价，消除该旋转联络后自然产生类似于超对称里卡提势（supersymmetric Riccati potentials）的二次几何不变量；在费米型约化（Fermi-type reductions）中，标量Jensen–Koppe–da Costa贡献在约化狄拉克部分被抵消，留下残余的一阶旋量导数结构，并暗示存在由几何联络结构自然生成的隐藏幂零协变微分复形（nilpotent covariant differential complexes）。

Conclusion: 该框架揭示了约束量子运动中几何联络结构的深层代数性质，为理解曲线与曲面上的量子动力学提供了统一的联络理论视角。

Abstract: We investigate constrained quantum motion on curves and surfaces using connection factorization methods. We show that Laplace operators admit an exact half-connection factorization generated by connection one-forms. The first-order part of the Laplacian is identified with the Darboux rotational connection of the orthogonal frame. Elimination of this rotational connection naturally produces quadratic geometric invariants analogous to supersymmetric Riccati potentials. Using orthonormal moving frames, we derive effective geometric contributions for planar curves, spatial curves, and embedded surfaces. We further analyze Dirac reductions using structure equations and show that for Fermi-type reductions the scalar Jensen--Koppe--da Costa contribution is cancelled in the reduced Dirac sector, leaving a residual first-order spinorial derivative structure. The resulting framework suggests the existence of hidden nilpotent covariant differential complexes naturally generated by geometric connection structures.

### [105] [Robustness of Valley-Hall Interface Modes Against Sharp Bending](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29485)
*Habib Ammari,Jiayu Qiu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对周期介质中弯曲界面上谷霍尔界面模（valley-Hall interface modes）的鲁棒性（robustness）问题，首次给出了严格的数学证明：当界面以2π/3角度弯曲时，除有限个例外频率外，所有非零群速度的体带隙（bulk spectral gap）频率下的界面模均保持不变；角局域模（corner-localized modes）仅可能出现在这些例外频率处且具有有限多重性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 周期介质中直界面上的能带反转（band inversion）会产生沿界面传播的局域模，这是谷霍尔效应（valley-Hall effect）的关键机制。但弯曲界面下这些界面模是否仍然鲁棒，是一个长期未解决的问题。本文旨在为弯曲界面的免疫性提供严格的数学理论。

Method: 采用严格的数学分析方法，证明当界面以2π/3角度弯曲时，对于体谱带隙（bulk spectral gap）中群速度（group velocity）非零的每一个频率，界面模均持续存在，例外仅为一个有限集合。此外，对角局域模的存在性与频率的关系进行数学刻画。

Result: 1）弯曲角度为2π/3时，除有限个例外频率外，所有非零群速度的体带隙频率下的界面模都保持存在；2）角局域模如果出现，只能出现在这些例外频率处，且具有有限多重性（finite multiplicity）。

Conclusion: 本文首次建立了谷霍尔界面模弯曲免疫性（bending immunity）的严格数学理论，为理解弯曲界面下界面模式的鲁棒性提供了基础性数学框架。

Abstract: It is well known that band inversion across a straight interface in a periodic medium gives rise to interface modes that are localized near the interface and propagate along it inside the bulk spectral gap. This phenomenon constitutes the key mechanism underlying the valley-Hall effect. In this paper, we address the long-standing problem of the robustness of such interface modes. We prove that, when the interface is bent through an angle of $\frac{2π}{3}$, the interface modes persist for every frequency in the bulk spectral gap where the group velocity is non-vanishing, except for a finite exceptional set. We also show that corner-localized modes, if they occur, can appear only at these exceptional frequencies and have finite multiplicity. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first rigorous mathematical theory of the bending immunity of valley-Hall interface modes.

### [106] [Free energy expansion of determinantal Coulomb gases in the quadratic fields with a point charge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29594)
*Sung-Soo Byun,Meng Yang,Eui Yoo*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对复平面上的行列式库仑气（determinantal Coulomb gas）模型，在外势含各向异性参数τ和奇点位置a的情况下，推导了自由能展开至常数项的所有系数，并将常数项与液滴的刘维尔作用量（Liouville action）相联系。该结果可解释为椭圆Ginibre系综（elliptic Ginibre ensemble）特征多项式矩的渐近展开，证明基于包含奇点位置和各向异性参数的形变框架与平面正交多项式（planar orthogonal polynomials）的精细渐近分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将此前各向同性情形（τ=0）的自由能展开结果推广到各向异性（τ∈[0,1)）及含奇点外势的情形，并建立自由能展开、平面正交多项式精细渐近与共形不变几何泛函之间的统一理论框架。

Method: 采用形变框架（deformation framework），同时变化奇点位置a和各向异性参数τ，将自由能的变分与平面正交多项式的精细渐近联系起来；渐近分析使用Hedenmalm-Wennman的叶状流方法（foliation flow method），作为各向同性情形中Riemann-Hilbert方法的替代方案。

Result: 在液滴为单连通或双连通区域的情形下，推导了自由能展开至常数项的所有显式系数，并将常数项识别为液滴的刘维尔作用量。结果可用于椭圆Ginibre系综特征多项式矩的渐近展开。

Conclusion: 本文工作提出了一个连接自由能展开、平面正交多项式精细渐近与共形不变几何泛函的通用框架，其中若干中间结果已对一般代数Hele-Shaw势（algebraic Hele-Shaw potentials）进行了公式化表述。

Abstract: We study a determinantal Coulomb gas in the complex plane associated with the external potential $$ Q(z)=\frac{1}{1-τ^2}\big(|z|^2-τ\text{Re } z^2\big)-2c\log|z-a|, $$ where $τ\in[0,1)$, $c\ge0$, and $a\ge0$. In the regimes where the associated droplet is simply or doubly connected, we derive the free energy expansion up to and including the constant term, with all coefficients computed explicitly, thereby extending recent results in the isotropic case $τ=0$. In particular, we identify the constant term with the Liouville action associated with the droplet. Our result admits a natural interpretation in terms of asymptotic expansions of moments of characteristic polynomials for the elliptic Ginibre ensemble. The proof is based on a deformation framework involving both the singularity location $a$ and the anisotropy parameter $τ$, relating variations of the free energy to refined asymptotics of planar orthogonal polynomials. The asymptotic analysis relies on the foliation flow method of Hedenmalm and Wennman, providing an alternative to the Riemann--Hilbert approach used in the isotropic setting. The present work suggests a general framework connecting free energy expansions, refined asymptotics of planar orthogonal polynomials, and conformally invariant geometric functionals, with several intermediate results already formulated for general algebraic Hele-Shaw potentials.

</details>


### [107] [Corner Quantization of 4D $BF$ Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30006)
*Giovanni Canepa,Alberto S. Cattaneo,Filippo Fila-Robattino,Timon Leupp*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究四维BF理论的量子化角结构（quantized corner structure），分类了自由角代数（free corner algebra）与物理角代数（physical corner algebra），并构造了其表示。阿贝尔情形下，角代数被识别为带有阿贝尔直和项的无穷维谐振子型李代数（oscillator-type Lie algebra）；非阿贝尔情形下，角代数为双环代数（double-loop algebra）的中心扩张商结构，但构造的模块在物理商化中平凡下降，显示了表示构造的障碍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子场论中角结构（corner structure）的代数化描述是研究边界对称性和量子化的重要方向，四维BF理论作为拓扑场论（topological field theory）的典型模型，其角代数的分类与表示构造尚待系统建立。

Method: 采用生成元与关系（generators and relations）的方式显式给出阿贝尔情形的角代数表示；利用玻色型Fock空间（bosonic Fock space）构造无穷族简单模（simple module）。非阿贝尔情形中，将角代数描述为双环代数中心扩张（central extension）的商结构，并通过诱导模（induced module）程序构造自由角代数的Fock型模。

Result: 阿贝尔情形下，对任意闭定向曲面且无论是否存在宇宙学项（cosmological term），角代数均为带有阿贝尔直和项的无穷维谐振子型李代数。非阿贝尔情形下（环面），角代数为非半单李代数上双环代数中心扩张的商，构造的Fock型模在物理商化中仅平凡下降，表明当前构造存在障碍（obstruction）。

Conclusion: 四维BF理论的角结构在不同情形下呈现显著差异：阿贝尔情形表示构造完整，而非阿贝尔情形存在表示下降的障碍。该结果揭示了非阿贝尔角代数表示理论的复杂性，为后续研究更一般的角代数分类与表示提供了基础。

Abstract: This note studies the quantized corner structure of four-dimensional $BF$ theory, classifies the associated free and physical corner algebras and constructs possible representations. In the abelian case, for arbitrary closed oriented surfaces and in the presence or absence of a cosmological term, explicit presentations of the corner algebras are obtained in terms of generators and relations, identifying them as infinite-dimensional oscillator-type Lie algebras with an abelian summand. A construction of infinite families of simple modules via bosonic Fock space representations is provided. In the non-abelian case on the torus, the corner algebras are described as quotients constructed from the central extensions of double-loop algebras over certain non-semisimple Lie algebras. A construction of infinite families of simple Fock-type modules of the free corner algebra via an induced module procedure is also provided. The resulting modules descend only trivially to the physical quotient, revealing an obstruction in the present construction in the non-abelian setting.

</details>

Abstract: We study the Dirac equation in the Reissner-Nordström geometry in horizon-penetrating coordinates up to the Cauchy horizon.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用代数量子场论框架，将费米子投影子定义为准自由Hadamard态的单粒子密度算符；引入与图无关的$i\varepsilon$正则化方案实现紫外正则化；在全局双曲时空中执行连续极限分析（continuum limit analysis）。

Conclusion: 该工作为因果费米子体系在全局双曲时空中的严格构造提供了代数量子场论基础，并揭示了因果作用量原理与Einstein-Dirac方程之间的等价性。

Abstract: We construct the causal fermion system for globally hyperbolic spacetimes starting in the framework of algebraic quantum field theory. The fermionic projector is identified with the one-particle density operator of a quasi-free Hadamard state. The ultraviolet regularization is built into the fermionic projector via a chart-independent $i\varepsilon$-regularization scheme. The continuum limit analysis is developed in globally hyperbolic spacetimes. It is shown that the Euler-Lagrange equations of the causal action principle are satisfied in this setup if and only if the coupled Einstein-Dirac equations hold.

### [110] [Kernel Renormalization in Bayesian Deep Neural Networks: the Equivalent Wishart Ansatz in the Proportional Regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29684)
*Paolo Baglioni,Christian Keup,Vincenzo Zimbardo,Rosalba Pacelli,Alessandro Vezzani,Raffaella Burioni,Pietro Rotondo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种有效近似方法，通过Wishart Ansatz和大偏差分析，在比例极限（proportional limit）下预测深度贝叶斯多层感知器（MLP）和卷积神经网络（CNN）的泛化性能。该方法将层次化经验核的随机波动重正化为一个重正化NNGP核，并用最多L个标量序参数描述表示学习。在多个基准数据集上，对L~O(10)和P~O(10^3)的深度网络进行测试，结果与贝叶斯后验采样实验总体吻合良好，并识别出两类系统性偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管比例宽度机制（proportional-width regime）在浅层单隐层网络中已有深入研究，但将其非微扰结果推广到深度非线性网络极为困难。本文旨在填补这一空白，为深度贝叶斯MLP和CNN在比例极限下的泛化性能提供有效的理论预测方法。

Method: 提出等效Wishart Ansatz以捕捉深度MLP层次化经验核（hierarchical empirical kernels）的主导随机波动；在此基础上对配分函数（partition function）进行大偏差分析（large deviation analysis），将其表达为重正化NNGP核（renormalized NNGP kernel）的形式。该描述中，比例极限下的强表示学习（representation learning）由最多L个通过自洽条件确定的标量序参数（scalar order parameters）编码。对于卷积架构（CNN），进一步识别出一种层次化局部核重正化机制（hierarchical local kernel renormalization mechanism），以量化有限宽度效应导致的CNN大宽度核的数据依赖变换。

Result: 在经典基准数据集上，对深度L~O(10)、训练集规模P~O(10^3)的有限深度贝叶斯神经网络进行了后验采样实验。理论预测与实验结果总体吻合良好，同时识别出两种不同类型的系统性偏差。

Conclusion: 所提出的有效理论方法能够较为准确地预测深度贝叶斯神经网络在比例极限下的泛化性能，为理解深度网络中的有限宽度效应（finite-width effects）和表示学习提供了理论工具。研究中发现的系统性偏差为后续理论改进指明了方向。

Abstract: The scaling limit where both the size of the training set $P$ and the width $N$ of a deep neural network grow at the same rate, the so-called proportional-width regime, has been intensely studied for shallow, single-hidden-layer networks. However, extending these non-perturbative results from shallow architectures to deep non-linear networks has proven very challenging. Here we present an effective approximate approach to predict the generalization performance of Bayesian multi-layer perceptrons (MLPs) of fixed depth $L$ on arbitrary high-dimensional data. We propose an equivalent Wishart Ansatz to capture the dominant stochastic fluctuations of the hierarchical empirical kernels of MLPs. This allows us to perform a large deviation analysis for the partition function of MLPs in the proportional limit, expressed in terms of a renormalized NNGP kernel. In this description, even strong representation learning in the proportional limit is encoded in at most $L$ scalar order parameters, determined self-consistently. Extending the approach to convolutional architectures (CNNs), we identify a hierarchical local kernel renormalization mechanism, which allows to quantify more complex data-dependent transformations of the large-width kernel in CNNs due to finite-width effects. We test our effective theory against sampling experiments from the Bayesian posterior of finite deep neural networks with depths $L \sim O(10)$ and $P\sim O(10^3)$ on classic benchmark datasets, finding overall very good agreement together with two distinct types of systematic deviations.

</details>


### [111] [Ridge Regression from Poisson Resetting: A Renewal Perspective on Spectral Regularization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30059)
*Petar Jolakoski*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文建立了非平衡统计物理中的随机重置（stochastic resetting）与统计学习中的岭回归（ridge regularization）之间的精确联系。对于线性梯度流，以速率 $r$ 重置到原点产生的稳态均值恰好是惩罚参数 $\lambda=r$ 的岭估计量。指数重置时间分布是唯一能在每个特征方向上都产生精确标量岭滤波的更新律（renewal law），而非指数更新律则生成替代性谱滤波器（spectral filters）。在加性奥恩斯坦-乌伦贝克（Ornstein-Uhlenbeck）扩展下，均值层面的等式成立，但随机重置过程存在非零稳态协方差，与确定性岭估计不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将非平衡统计物理中的随机重置机制与统计学习中的岭正则化进行理论联系，探索两个领域之间的深层数学结构。

Method: 利用岭回归与梯度流指数时间平均之间的拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transform）关系，将指数时间重新解释为泊松重置（Poisson resetting）对应的稳态年龄（stationary age）。对于一般更新重置律，分析了不同重置时间分布下稳态均值的谱滤波特性；对于涨落层面，引入加性奥恩斯坦-乌伦贝克扩展作为随机梯度下降（SGD）的简化近似。

Result: 指数重置时间分布是唯一能产生精确标量岭滤波的更新律；非指数更新律生成替代性谱滤波器。在加性噪声扩展下，均值层面等式成立，但重置过程具有非零稳态协方差，而确定性岭估计是固定中心的无波动估计量。

Conclusion: 随机重置与岭正则化之间存在精确的理论对应关系，为理解正则化方法提供了统计物理视角；非指数重置律可生成不同于岭回归的预测性滤波器，在连续时间梯度流和二次目标函数上建立了稳态均值与谱滤波器的理论结果。

Abstract: We connect stochastic resetting from non-equilibrium statistical physics with ridge regularization in statistical learning. For linear gradient flow, resetting to the origin at rate $r$ produces stationary mean $(X^\top X+rI)^{-1}X^\top y$, exactly the ridge estimator with penalty $λ=r$. This uses the known Laplace-transform relationship between ridge regression and exponential-time averaging of gradient flow, with the exponential time now interpreted as the stationary age associated with Poisson resetting. We then extend this identity to general renewal reset laws: the exponential reset time distribution is the unique renewal law whose stationary mean reproduces scalar ridge in every eigendirection as an exact filter identity for every positive curvature, while non-exponential renewal laws generate alternative spectral filters. At the fluctuation level, we study a separate additive Ornstein-Uhlenbeck extension with constant diffusion, interpreted as a stylized SGD approximation. In this setting, the equality holds only at the level of the mean, since the reset process has a nonzero stationary covariance from accumulated OU noise and reset-timing variance, whereas deterministic ridge is a fixed estimator with the same center. Stylized experiments compare the deterministic renewal-induced filters directly and illustrate when filters induced by non-exponential reset-time laws can differ predictively from ridge. The results for the stationary mean and the induced spectral filters are established for continuous-time gradient flow with isotropic resetting on quadratic objectives; the covariance and risk formulas additionally assume additive noise with state-independent covariance.

</details>

### [112] [Polar Fidelities, Holevo Bases, and Unitary Factors of Generalized Fidelity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28885)
*Trung Dung Vuong*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究Afham-Ferrie广义保真度（generalized fidelity）理论中的极保真度（polar fidelities）、Holevo基（Holevo bases）及幺正因子（unitary factors）。证明了一侧极保真度及其对称化在(-∞,1]上非减、在[1,∞)上非增，极路径在[-1,1]上实现了所有z≥1/2的z-保真度值及Log-Euclidean保真度；同时指出对d≥2且0<z<1/2时该实现一般不成立。进一步求解了固定对的Holevo基方程，分类了所有Holevo基及其对应的幺正因子，并否定了全局反向包含关系SU(d)（d≥2）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受到Afham-Ferrie广义保真度理论中若干未解决问题的驱动，旨在系统研究极保真度、Holevo基以及幺正因子在正定矩阵锥（cone of complex positive definite matrices）上的数学结构与性质。

Method: 采用数学分析与矩阵理论方法，定义并研究单侧极保真度（one-sided polar fidelities）及其对称化，分析其在实参数轴上的单调性；通过建立极路径与z-保真度、Log-Euclidean保真度的映射关系，求解固定对Holevo基方程并分类Holevo基与幺正因子。

Result: 证明了固定对P,Q下，单侧极保真度及其对称化在(-∞,1]上非减、在[1,∞)上非增；极路径精确实现了[FM(P,Q), FU(P,Q)]区间，进而实现了所有z≥1/2的z-保真度值及Log-Euclidean保真度。对于d≥2且0<z<1/2，该实现一般不成立。求解了Holevo基方程，分类了所有Holevo基，并精确刻画了由某一基R可导出的广义保真度的幺正因子，即P^{-1/2}Q^{1/2}W相似于某正定矩阵的W。该结果恢复了特殊幺正约束（special-unitary constraint），并否定了d≥2时全局反向包含关系SU(d)。

Conclusion: 本文澄清了广义保真度理论中极路径与z-保真度之间的精确关系，划定了可实现的z值范围；通过对Holevo基和幺正因子的完全分类，揭示了广义保真度的代数结构，并否定了之前可能假设的全局反向包含关系。

Abstract: Motivated by several open problems in the Afham-Ferrie theory of generalized fidelity, we study polar fidelities, Holevo bases, and unitary factors on \(\Pd\), the cone of \(d\times d\) complex positive definite matrices. We prove that, for every fixed pair \(P,Q\in\Pd\), the one-sided polar fidelities \(x\mapsto F_{P^x}(P,Q)\) and \(x\mapsto F_{Q^x}(P,Q)\), as well as their symmetrization, are nondecreasing on \((-\infty,1]\) and nonincreasing on \([1,\infty)\). Hence the polar paths realize exactly the interval \([\FM(P,Q),\FU(P,Q)]\) on \([-1,1]\), yielding pointwise, generally pair-dependent realizations of all \(z\)-fidelity values with \(z\ge1/2\) and of the Log-Euclidean fidelity as generalized fidelities. We also show that for \(d\ge2\) and \(0<z<1/2\), such realization fails in general, even for interior fidelities. We further solve the fixed-pair Holevo-base equation \(F_R(P,Q)=\FH(P,Q)\), classify all Holevo bases, and classify exactly which unitary factors of generalized fidelity can arise from a base \(R\). These are precisely the unitaries \(W\) for which \(P^{-1/2}Q^{1/2}W\) is similar to a positive definite matrix. This recovers the special-unitary constraint and disproves the global reverse inclusion \(SU(d)\) for \(d\ge2\).

### [113] [A local description of strong symmetries and strong-to-weak symmetry breaking in quantum many-body systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28925)

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种局域化（local）的理解和诊断方案，用于分析量子混合态中的强对称性（strong symmetry）及其自发破缺为弱对称性（weak symmetry）的现象。通过在无穷大体积极限下严格定义强对称性，并引入“局域荷相干性（local charge coherence）”等等价表述，作者进一步提出了介于强、弱对称性之间的“冯·诺伊曼对称性（von Neumann symmetry）”，并在量子自旋链中推导了针对这类对称性的Lieb-Schultz-Mattis型反常约束（anomaly constraint）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过往研究表明，量子多体系统的混合态中，强对称性可“自发破缺”为弱对称性；然而，这种强到弱的对称性破缺（strong-to-weak symmetry breaking）在原有表述下表现为一种非局域（non-local）效应，缺乏清晰的局域理解与诊断工具。

Method: 核心方法是在无穷大体积（infinite volume）极限下对强对称性给出一个严格定义，该定义推广了传统的有限体积（finite-volume）定义，并提供了若干等价表述，其中包括基于“局域荷相干性”的方案。此外，引入“冯·诺伊曼系统”（von Neumann systems）来刻画介于强与弱对称性之间的无穷大体积对称性。

Result: 在无穷大体积下给出了强对称性的严格定义及其多种等价形式；提出了冯·诺伊曼对称性作为中间类型的对称性；在量子自旋链中推导出针对冯·诺伊曼对称性（从而也适用于强对称性）的Lieb-Schultz-Mattis型反常约束。

Conclusion: 该工作为强对称性及强到弱对称性破缺提供了一种显式局域化的理解方式，并通过引入冯·诺伊曼对称性及相应的反常约束，丰富了无穷大体积下量子混合态对称性的理论框架。

Abstract: In mixed states of quantum systems, symmetries come in two types: strong and weak. Furthermore, it has been argued that in quantum many-body systems, strong symmetries can be "spontaneously broken" down to weak symmetries. An issue is that as previously formulated, such "strong-to-weak symmetry breaking" appears to be a fairly non-local effect. In this paper, we show how to understand and diagnose strong symmetries and strong-to-weak symmetry breaking in an explicitly local way. Our main technical tool is a rigorous definition of strong symmetry in the limit of infinite volume, which generalizes the conventional finite-volume definitions, and for which we give several equivalent formulations, including one involving the concept of "local charge coherence". Finally, we introduce von Neumann systems, which in infinite-volume symmetries are intermediate between strong and weak symmetries. We derive a Lieb-Schultz-Mattis type anomaly constraint for von Neumann symmetries (and therefore, in particular, strong symmetries) in quantum spin chains.

### [114] [Analytic Properties of the Jost Functions via the Poincaré-Picard Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28859)
*Yannick Mvondo-She*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文从参数依赖的常微分方程（ordinary differential equations）视角出发，研究量子散射理论中Jost函数（Jost functions）的解析性质。通过因子化动量依赖的分支项，将散射问题转化为系数为复能量单值解析函数的微分系统，证明了变换后的Jost函数在有限径向距离上是能量的单值解析函数，并讨论了该因子化过程的黎曼曲面（Riemann surface）拓扑解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Jost函数的解析性质是量子散射理论（quantum scattering theory）和散射矩阵（scattering matrix）向复能量平面解析延拓的基础，本研究旨在从参数依赖的常微分方程角度系统阐明其解析性来源。

Method: 从短程中心势（short-range central potential）的径向薛定谔方程（radial Schrödinger equation）出发，推导出与Riccati-Bessel解和Riccati-Neumann解相关的系数函数的一阶微分系统；通过显式因子化动量依赖的分支项（branching terms），将散射问题转化为系数为复能量单值解析函数的微分系统，并利用常微分方程解对参数的解析依赖性经典理论进行分析。

Result: 证明了能量变量与动量之间的平方根关系（square-root relation）是Jost函数多值依赖性的来源；通过因子化动量依赖的分支项，变换后的Jost函数在有限径向距离（finite radial distance）上是复能量变量的单值解析函数（single-valued analytic functions）。

Conclusion: 本文从常微分方程的参数依赖理论出发，为Jost函数的解析性提供了严格的数学基础，并通过对因子化过程的黎曼曲面拓扑讨论，揭示了该方法的几何意义。

Abstract: The analytic properties of the Jost functions are fundamental in quantum scattering theory and in the analytic continuation of the scattering matrix into the complex energy plane. In this work, the analyticity of the Jost functions is investigated from the perspective of parameter-dependent ordinary differential equations. Starting from the radial Schrödinger equation for a short-range central potential, a first-order differential system is derived for the coefficient functions associated with the Ricatti--Bessel and Ricatti--Neumann solutions. The multivalued dependence on the energy variable is shown to originate from the square-root relation between energy and momentum. By explicitly factorizing the momentum-dependent branching terms, the scattering problem is transformed into a differential system whose coefficients are single-valued analytic functions of the complex energy. Using the classical theory of analytic dependence of solutions of ordinary differential equations on parameters, it is shown that the transformed Jost functions are single-valued analytic functions of the energy variable for finite radial distance. The geometric interpretation of the factorization procedure is also discussed in terms of the topology of the associated Riemann surface.
