### [115] [A tutorial on Dirac quantisation by analysing the problem of a ball on an inclined plane as a Hamiltonian system with constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28878)
*M. F. Araujo de Resende,Thales Machado F*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以实心球无滑滚动为例，采用狄拉克-伯格曼算法处理经典约束系统，通过将狄拉克括号（Dirac brackets）替换为对易子（commutators）实现从经典力学到量子力学的过渡，并将约束系统的哈密顿算符（Hamiltonian operator）限制至物理希尔伯特子空间（physical Hilbert subspace）。

Result: 证明了将约束系统的哈密顿算符限制到物理希尔伯特子空间后，所得结果与内禀方法导出的薛定谔方程完全一致。

Conclusion: 该一致性验证了狄拉克量子化方法在处理具有约束的哈密顿系统时的自洽性与有效性。

Abstract: In this paper, we present a detailed review/analysis of the Dirac quantisation of Hamiltonian systems with constraints. To this end, we use, as a guide, the physical example provided by the dynamics of a solid ball rolling, without slipping, down an inclined plane under the action of gravity. After all, however simple this physical system may be, it provides a rich framework for this analysis since, in addition to allowing us to discuss scenarios involving holonomic and non-holonomic constraints, it is also a gauge system. Indeed, due to this latter fact, we have carefully detailed how the transition, from classical to quantum mechanics, must be guided by the Dirac-Bergmann algorithm and by the consequent replacement of Dirac brackets with commutators. As a central result, we demonstrate that the restriction of the Hamiltonian operator of this system with constraints to the physical Hilbert subspace (which is identified with the quantisation of these constraints) reproduces the same Schrödinger equation that can be originally obtained in intrinsic terms, a fact that only reinforces the consistency of the Dirac quantisation method.

### [116] [Non-Perturbative Closed Form for the Typical Bipartite Mutual Information of Haar-Random States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29725)
*Zhi-Wei Wang,Pei-Wen Li,Samuel L. Braunstein*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文推导了Haar随机纯态中平均二分量子互信息（average bipartite quantum mutual information）的精确非微扰闭式，该表达式通过一个Bose-Einstein核上的收敛积分给出，并揭示了其与狄利克雷（Dirichlet）贡献和Schur主化（Schur-majorisation）特征值修正的严格分解关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平均二分量子互信息 $\langle I(A{:}B)\rangle$ 在Haar随机纯态中通常通过Page公式以双伽玛函数（digamma functions）的精确形式表达，但缺乏单一的非微扰闭式。本文旨在填补这一空白，并揭示该量更深层的数学结构与物理意义。

Method: 通过将Page熵精确分解为对角（狄利克雷，Dirichlet）贡献与Schur主化（Schur-majorisation）特征值修正，再将这些贡献组装为互信息，从而得到 $\langle I(A{:}B)\rangle$ 的非微扰闭式：$(d_A^2-1)(d_B^2-1)\,\mathcal{G}(d_A,d_B,d_E)$，其中 $\mathcal{G}$ 由含Bose-Einstein核的收敛积分显式给出。

Result: 互信息表达式中整体因子 $(d_A^2-1)(d_B^2-1)=\dim[\mathfrak{su}(d_A)]\cdot\dim[\mathfrak{su}(d_B)]$ 是精确的，而非渐近近似。$\mathcal{G}$ 的 $1/N$ 渐近展开产生了一个伯努利因子化（Bernoulli-factorised）级数，其系数涉及 $\zeta(1{-}2k)$，该级数发散，而积分形式是其精确的Borel和（Borel sum）。此外，通过核的尺度反演对称性，可显式证明 $\langle I\rangle < (d_A^2{-}1)(d_B^2{-}1)/(2N)$。

Conclusion: 该积分表示不仅提供了平均互信息的精确闭式，还将量子关联与经典关联在结构上清晰分离——互信息的构成自然地拆解为对角贡献（Dirichlet部分）与Schur主化修正，从而揭示了随机纯态中量子互信息（quantum mutual information）的深层结构来源。

Abstract: The average bipartite quantum mutual information $\langle I(A{:}B)\rangle$ of Haar-random pure states can be expressed exactly through Page's formula in terms of digamma functions. We show that this quantity admits a single non-perturbative closed form: $\langle I(A{:}B)\rangle = (d_A^2-1)(d_B^2-1)\,\mathcal{G}(d_A,d_B,d_E)$, where $\mathcal{G}$ is given by an explicit convergent integral over a Bose--Einstein kernel. The overall factor $(d_A^2-1)(d_B^2-1)=\dim[\mathfrak{su}(d_A)]\cdot\dim[\mathfrak{su}(d_B)]$ is exact, not merely asymptotic. The asymptotic expansion of $\mathcal{G}$ in $1/N$ yields a Bernoulli-factorised series whose coefficients involve $ζ(1{-}2k)$; this series diverges, and our integral is its exact Borel sum. The integral representation also makes $\langle I\rangle < (d_A^2{-}1)(d_B^2{-}1)/(2N)$ manifest via a scale-inversion symmetry of the kernel. Our derivation traces the mutual information's structure to an exact decomposition of Page's entropy into a diagonal (Dirichlet) contribution and a Schur-majorisation eigenvalue correction, whose assembly into the mutual information cleanly separates classical from quantum correlations.

</details>


### [117] [Exact Geometric Typicality and Bipartite Entanglement from the Projected Central Limit Theorem on Hyperspheres](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29732)
*Zhi-Wei Wang,Pei-Wen Li,Samuel L. Braunstein*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文从超球面上的精确投影中心极限定理出发，重新导出子系统占据概率的Beta分布和Lubkin纯度公式，并给出Haar随机纯态下二分量子互信息（bipartite quantum mutual information）的完整渐近展开与非微扰封闭形式，揭示了其伯努利因子化结构以及有限尺寸修正中的量子相干与经典概率分离机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有本征态热化（eigenstate-thermalization）和典型性（typicality）处理方法采用高斯近似，但该近似在有限尺寸下存在尾部“低峰态（platykurtic）”抑制偏差。本文旨在精确刻画Haar随机纯态下二分量子互信息的有限尺寸行为，并澄清其量子相干成分与经典概率成分的分离根源。

Method: 利用超球面上的精确投影中心极限定理（Projected Central Limit Theorem）和初等超球面矩（hyperspherical moments），重新推导Beta分布和Lubkin纯度公式；通过对Page公式进行精确代数重组，并借助Schur优超定理（Schur's majorisation theorem）和广义Bloch分解（generalised Bloch decomposition）的Cartan结构，分离出量子相干贡献与经典概率贡献。

Result: Haar随机纯态下二分量子互信息的完整$1/N$渐近展开呈伯努利因子化形式：每个$k \ge 1$阶项携带对称因子$(d_A^{2k}-1)(d_B^{2k}-1)$，所有高阶奇数阶修正严格为零。有限尺寸主导修正分为两部分：$\mathfrak{su}(d_A) \otimes \mathfrak{su}(d_B)$双部量子相干贡献$(d_A^2 - 1)(d_B^2 - 1)/(2N)$，以及减去后的经典概率（Cartan $\otimes$ Cartan）贡献$(d_A - 1)(d_B - 1)/(2N)$。该结果可整合为单一非微扰封闭形式$\langle I(A{:}B)\rangle = (d_A^2-1)(d_B^2-1)\,\mathcal{G}(d_A,d_B,d_E)$，其中$\mathcal{G}$由显式Bose–Einstein积分给出。

Conclusion: 本文首次给出了Haar随机纯态二分量子互信息的完整渐近展开与非微扰封闭形式，阐明了有限尺寸修正中量子相干与经典概率的自然分离机制，并从Cartan代数结构角度赋予了维度计数$(d-1)$和$(d^2-1)$以几何意义。

Abstract: Starting from the exact Projected Central Limit Theorem on hyperspheres, we rederive the Beta distribution for subsystem occupation probabilities and Lubkin's purity formula from elementary hyperspherical moments, quantifying the finite-size ``platykurtic'' suppression of tails relative to the Gaussian approximation used in standard eigenstate-thermalization and typicality treatments. Our main new result concerns the bipartite quantum mutual information $\langle I(A{:}B)\rangle$ for Haar-random pure states. We show that its full asymptotic expansion in $1/N$ admits a Bernoulli-factorized form in which every order $k \ge 1$ carries the symmetric factor $(d_A^{2k}-1)(d_B^{2k}-1)$ and all higher odd-order corrections vanish identically. Through an exact algebraic reorganization of Page's formula (conjectured in Ref.~\cite{Page1993} and subsequently proven~\cite{Foong1994, SanchezRuiz1995, Sen1996}), we establish that the leading finite-size correction separates into a dominant $\mathfrak{su}(d_A) \otimes \mathfrak{su}(d_B)$ bipartite quantum coherence contribution $(d_A^2 - 1)(d_B^2 - 1)/(2N)$ and a subtracted classical-probability (Cartan $\otimes$ Cartan) contribution $(d_A - 1)(d_B - 1)/(2N)$, and we trace this separation to the difference between diagonal and eigenvalue entropies via Schur's majorisation theorem, with the dimensional counts $(d-1)$ and $(d^2-1)$ acquiring meaning through the Cartan structure of the generalised Bloch decomposition. These results admit a single non-perturbative closed form: the exact typical mutual information factors as $\langle I(A{:}B)\rangle = (d_A^2-1)(d_B^2-1)\,\mathcal{G}(d_A,d_B,d_E)$, with $\mathcal{G}$ given by an explicit Bose--Einstein integral whose asymptotic expansion in $1/N$ reproduces the Bernoulli series.

</details>


### [118] [Gate Parameter Lee-Yang Zeros and Dynamical Phases in Quantum Circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29838)
*Chang Liu,Yu Wu,Yunfeng Jiang,Yang Zhang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出将门参数化的Lee-Yang零点（gate-parameter Lee-Yang zeros）作为探测量子电路中动力学相的有限尺寸探针。通过对砖墙模型的分析，发现零点在复化门参数平面上的凝聚曲线包含由等模Floquet本征值（equimodular Floquet eigenvalues）决定的普适分量和由初态投影决定的状态依赖分量，零点集的重组可作为动力学相变（dynamical phase transition）的有限比特诊断信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究通常基于热力学极限下的Loschmidt回波（Loschmidt echo）零点来定义动力学量子相变（dynamical quantum phase transition），但在有限尺寸量子电路中缺乏直接且可计算的诊断工具。本文旨在发展一种无需热力学极限、仅依赖有限量子比特即可识别动力学相变的方法。

Method: 本文采用砖墙模型（brickwork model），其中时间演化由Floquet算符（Floquet operator）的重复作用生成。Loschmidt振幅被表达为门参数的有理函数；通过复数化其中一个门参数并固定另一参数，研究零点在有限系统尺寸和大电路深度下的凝聚行为。分析框架基于Beraha-Kahane-Weiss定理（Beraha-Kahane-Weiss theorem）以及Floquet本征谱与本征态重叠的联合作用。

Result: 零点在复门参数平面上凝聚为极限曲线，该曲线包含两个部分：由等模Floquet本征值决定的普适分量，以及由Floquet算符本征态与初始态重叠控制的状态依赖分量。随着门参数的变化，零点集的拓扑结构发生突然重组，这一重组现象在有限比特系统中即可观测。该机制不依赖可积性（integrability），仅源于谱竞争（spectral competition）和局域幺正性（local unitarity）。

Conclusion: 门参数化的Lee-Yang零点提供了一种有限尺寸量子电路中诊断动力学相变的普适方法，不依赖于可积性或热力学极限，仅通过谱竞争和局域幺正性即可实现。这一发现拓展了凝聚态物理中Lee-Yang零点（Lee-Yang zeros）概念在非平衡量子动力学中的应用范围。

Abstract: We propose gate-parameter Lee-Yang zeros of Loschmidt amplitudes as probes of dynamical phases in finite quantum circuits. We illustrate this approach using a brickwork model, where the time evolution is generated by repeated application of a Floquet operator. The Loschmidt amplitude can be expressed as a rational function of the gate parameters. At fixed system size and large circuit depth, its zeros in one complexified gate parameter, with the other parameter held fixed, condense onto limiting curves. We show that these curves comprise a universal component governed by equimodular Floquet eigenvalues, as described by the Beraha-Kahane-Weiss theorem, together with state-dependent contributions controlled by the overlap of eigenstate of the Floquet operator with the initial state. As one of the parameters is varied, the set of zeros reorganizes abruptly, providing a finite-qubit diagnostic of a dynamical phase transition. This mechanism does not rely on integrability: while integrability enables an exact calculation of the Loschmidt amplitude, the condensation of zeros follows from spectral competition and local unitarity alone.

Method: 首先构建一套量子理论的公理系统（axioms for quantum theory）；随后研究一个经典振子（classical oscillator）置于热浴（thermostat）中的模型，该模型可被解释为量子振子，以此探讨微观与经典描述之间的对应关系。

Abstract: This book examines a number of problems of quantum mechanics, most of which are not usually discussed. What is the origin of probabilities in the mechanics of the microworld? What is the nature of Planck's constant h? What is the nature of probability amplitudes? What is the wave function? A system of axioms for quantum theory is formulated. A model is studied according to which a classical oscillator in a thermostat can be interpreted as a quantum one. The measurement problem is discussed in detail.
  For advanced undergraduate students, graduate students, and specialists interested in the foundations of quantum theory.

### [120] [Learning quantum ground states in the space of measurement outcomes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28931)
*Kartiek Agarwal*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种利用自回归神经网络（autoregressive neural network）在测量空间中直接变分学习量子多体基态的方法，将量子态表示为SIC-POVM测量结果的概率分布，通过梯度下降最小化哈密顿量期望值，并施加正定性约束以确保物理可实现性。在横向场伊辛模型和海森堡模型等一维系统中验证了该方法对多达128个格点系统的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索利用自回归神经网络直接从测量概率分布（measurement probability distribution）变分学习量子多体基态（quantum many-body ground states）的可能性，避免直接处理高维量子态波函数的复杂性。

Method: 将量子态表示为对称信息完备正算子值测度（SIC-POVM）结果上的概率分布；用基于门控循环单元（gated recurrent units, GRUs）的自回归神经网络参数化该概率分布；通过梯度下降更新概率分布以最小化给定哈密顿量下的能量；同时施加正定性约束（positivity constraints）以确保测量分布对应物理量子态。

Result: 在一维横向场伊辛模型（transverse-field Ising model）和海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）及加隙场（gapping fields）的基准测试中，对于多达L=128的格点系统，该方法表现出良好的有效性。

Conclusion: 约束施加的层次（正定性条件层级）、神经网络架构的多样性（多层、膨胀卷积、输入数据修改）对方法的成功起到关键作用；该方案在多种模型中均展现出广泛适用性。

Abstract: We investigate variational learning of quantum many-body ground states directly in measurement space using autoregressive neural networks. In particular, we represent quantum states via probability distributions of outcomes over a symmetric informationally complete positive operator-valued measure (SIC-POVM). The probability distribution is encoded in the parameters of an autoregressive neural-network-based on gated recurrent units (GRUs). Ground states are obtained by gradient descent that updates the probability distribution to minimize the energy with respect to a given Hamiltonian, while enforcing positivity constraints that ensure that the distribution of measurement outcomes correspond to a physical quantum state. We analyze the role of constraint enforcement (hierarchy of positivity conditions), variety of neural network architectures (multiple layers, dilation, and modifications of input data) in determining the success of this approach. We benchmark our approach on one-dimensional transverse-field Ising model and the Heisenberg model, along with gapping fields, for system sizes up to L=128, illustrating its efficacy across a wide variety of models.

### [121] [Local Strong-to-Weak Spontaneous Symmetry Breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28967)
*Francisco Divi,Leonardo A. Lessa,Chong Wang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种强到弱自发对称性破缺（strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking, SW-SSB）的局域定义，基于单点保真度关联函数（one-point fidelity correlator），相比原有的两点保真度关联函数定义，在可探测性和热力学极限下的良定义性方面具有优势，并展示了该局域框架下SW-SSB的关键特性（如有限深度对称信道下的稳定性、长程条件互信息）以及临界系统中的普适标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原有的SW-SSB定义依赖于两点保真度关联函数，在大规模系统中探测困难，且在热力学极限下密度矩阵本身不再良定义，限制了其适用范围。本文旨在提出一种局域化的SW-SSB定义，克服上述局限。

Method: 通过单点保真度关联函数（local one-point fidelity correlator）给出SW-SSB的局域定义；利用该局域序参量在热力学极限下保持良定义的性质，并在概念上类比于满足本征态热化假说（eigenstate thermalization hypothesis, ETH）的纯态局域热化过程。

Result: 局域SW-SSB在大小为$N$、资源量为${\rm poly}(N)$的系统中可探测到体积标度达$O(\log(N))$的局域保真度序；有限深度对称信道下的稳定性和长程条件互信息（conditional mutual information）等SW-SSB核心特征在该局域框架中依然成立；在临界系统（包括共形场论基态及弹道扩散自由费米子金属）中导出了局域保真度关联函数的普适标度行为。

Conclusion: 局域化定义使得SW-SSB在热力学极限下依然具有良定义，并提高了大规模系统中的可探测性；该框架为临界系统中的缺陷问题提供了一类新的视角，通过多个具体例子验证了其适用性。

Abstract: We propose a local notion of strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking (SW-SSB), through a local one-point fidelity correlator. Compared with the previous definition in terms of a two-point fidelity correlator, our local formulation offers two key advantages: (1) it is easier to detect in large systems: for a system of size $N$ and with ${\rm poly}(N)$ amount of resources, one can detect the local fidelity order up to volume scale $O(\log(N))$; and (2) the local SW-SSB order remains well defined in the thermodynamic limit, where the density matrix itself is not well defined. We show that key features of SW-SSB, including stability under finite-depth symmetric channels and long-range conditional mutual information, persist within this local framework. Our definition is conceptually analogous to local thermalization, as exemplified by pure states obeying the eigenstate thermalization hypothesis (ETH). For critical states, the local one-point fidelity correlator defines an interesting class of defect problems. We demonstrate the applicability of the local formulation through several concrete examples, and derive the universal scaling behavior of the local fidelity correlator in a range of critical systems, including ground states of conformal field theories as well as ballistic and diffusive free-fermion metals.

### [122] [Local diagnostics for strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking and non-equilibrium phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29113)
*Carolyn Zhang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文构造了强Z₂对称的局域马尔可夫/林德布拉德动力学，展示了从强顺磁行为到强-弱自发对称性破缺（SWSSB）的相变。在1+1维，吸收态构造给出与宇称守恒分支-湮灭随机游走（parity-conserving branching-annihilating random-walk）普适类一致的标度行为；在2+1维，图姆规则的pair-flip变体为稳定的强顺磁/弱对称破缺区以及活跃SWSSB区的相变提供了证据。此外，引入半径R的边缘保真度关联函数（marginal fidelity correlator），作为通常SWSSB保真度序参量的局域代理，仅需在O(R^d)大小区域上进行断层扫描，并证明对满足局域不可区分性假设的对称投影吉布斯态等广泛状态类，边缘与全局保真度关联函数之间的误差随R指数衰减。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者构造了强Z₂对称的局域马尔可夫/林德布拉德动力学，在1+1维采用吸收态（absorbing-state）构造，在2+1维采用图姆规则（Toom's rule）的pair-flip变体。同时引入了一种新的半径R边缘保真度关联函数（marginal fidelity correlator），作为全局保真度序参量的局域代理，仅需对O(R^d)大小的区域进行断层扫描。对满足局域不可区分性（local indistinguishability）假设的对称投影吉布斯态等广泛状态类，给出了边缘与全局关联函数之间的误差界。

Result: 在1+1维，吸收态构造给出的相变标度行为与宇称守恒分支-湮灭随机游走（parity-conserving branching-annihilating random-walk）普适类一致。在2+1维，发现了稳定的强顺磁/弱对称破缺（strong-paramagnetic/weakly symmetry-broken）区和向活跃SWSSB区的相变。边缘保真度关联函数与全局保真度关联函数之间的误差随半径R指数衰减，使其成为吸收态相变中与微观缺陷或活性概念无关的模型无关（model-independent）SWSSB诊断工具。

Conclusion: 研究表明，强Z₂对称的局域动力学能够呈现从强顺磁到强-弱自发对称性破缺（SWSSB）的相变，其临界行为因维度而异。新提出的边缘保真度关联函数作为局域可观测的SWSSB诊断工具，在广泛的量子态类中具有指数级收敛的精度，为研究吸收态相变中的SWSSB提供了不依赖微观细节的通用方法。

Abstract: We construct strongly $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric local Markov/Lindblad dynamics exhibiting transitions between strong-paramagnetic behavior and strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking. In 1+1d, an absorbing-state construction gives a transition with scaling consistent with the parity-conserving branching-annihilating random-walk universality class. In 2+1d, a pair-flip variant of Toom's rule provides evidence for a stable strong-paramagnetic/weakly symmetry-broken regime and a transition into an active SWSSB regime. We also introduce a marginal fidelity correlator of radius $R$, a local proxy for the usual SWSSB fidelity order parameter requiring tomography only on $\mathcal{O}(R^d)$-size regions. For broad classes of states, including symmetry-projected Gibbs-like states satisfying suitable local indistinguishability assumptions, we bound the error between the marginal and global fidelity correlators by terms decaying exponentially in $R$. These marginal fidelities provide a model-independent diagnostic of SWSSB in absorbing-state transitions, where microscopic notions of defects or activity are not universal.

*Taichi Kosugi,Hirofumi Nishi,Keito Kasebayashi,Hiroki Takahashi,Yu-ichiro Matsushita*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出QAVG（量子平均变网格法），一种结合低分辨率量子相位估计（QPE）与多次原点平移及物理驱动的连续参数化来精确重构光谱的游标式方法，并在Quantinuum H2-2硬件上通过CO分子吸附于χ-Fe₅C₂表面的从头计算模型系统进行了实验验证，证明该方法在噪声环境下仍能实现远低于名义QPE分辨率的光谱重构精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子相位估计（QPE）是从多电子系统中提取激发光谱的关键底层技术，但当前硬件上的低网格分辨率和环境噪声严重阻碍了其实用化。

Method: 提出QAVG（量子平均变网格法），一种游标式（vernier-type）方法，将低分辨率QPE与多次原点平移（origin shifts）及物理驱动的连续参数化（physically motivated continuous parametrization）相结合，以精确重构光谱。将该方法纳入针对CO分子吸附于χ-Fe₅C₂表面的从头计算（ab initio）模型系统的端到端工作流中，并在Quantinuum H2-2硬件上使用物理QPE电路以及由Steane码（Steane code）编码且带有离线比特翻转纠正（offline bit-flip correction）的逻辑QPE电路进行实验。

Result: QAVG即使在使用带噪声的直方图时，也能以远低于名义QPE分辨率的偏差精确重构光谱。在平移网格上平均化的代价景观（cost landscape）有效抑制了由频谱泄漏（spectral leakage）引起的局部极小值，从而稳定了试验参数（trial parameters）的优化。

Conclusion: QAVG为早期容错量子计算机（early-fault-tolerant quantum computers）时代的相关谱（correlated spectra）量子模拟提供了一条稳健的路径。

Abstract: Quantum phase estimation (QPE) is an underlying technology for extracting the excitation spectra of many-electron systems, yet its practical use on current hardware is hindered by low grid resolution and environmental noises. Here we propose QPE averaged over variable grids (QAVG), a vernier-type approach that combines low-resolution QPE with multiple origin shifts and physically motivated continuous parametrization to reconstruct the spectra accurately. We introduce this approach into an end-to-end workflow for the {\it ab initio}-based model system for a CO molecule adsorbed onto the $χ$-Fe$_5$C$_2$ surface. We perform experiments on Quantinuum H2-2 using both physical QPE circuits and logical QPE circuits encoded in the Steane code with offline bit-flip correction. We demonstrate that QAVG accurately reconstructs the spectra with deviations much smaller than the nominal QPE resolution, even when the noisy histograms are used. The cost landscapes averaged over the shifted grids substantially suppress the local minima arising from the spectral leakage, thereby stabilizing the optimization of trial parameters. These results indicate that QAVG provides a robust route to quantum simulations of correlated spectra toward the era of early-fault-tolerant quantum computers.

</details>


### [125] [Channel-agnostic finite-temperature phase estimation averaged over variable grids: reconstruction of Green's function for dynamical mean-field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29681)
*Taichi Kosugi,Hirofumi Nishi,Keito Kasebayashi,Hiroki Takahashi,Yu-ichiro Matsushita*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 提出一种用于量子计算机处理关联电子系统的量子-经典混合动力学平均场论（DMFT）方案，其中量子部分采用改进的量子相位估计（QPE）电路提取有限温度下的单粒子格林函数，经典部分通过QPE平均变分网格（QAVG）方法重构格林函数，并在SrVO₃体系中通过数值模拟验证了方案的有效性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出QAVG-DMFT混合方案：量子部分使用改进的量子相位估计（modified quantum phase estimation, QPE）电路，在有限温度下提取单粒子GF的谱振幅和激发能量；经典部分采用QPE平均变分网格（QPE averaged over variable grids, QAVG）方法，通过优化试验参数和建模概率分布来合理重构GF。

Result: 将该QAVG-DMFT方案应用于钙钛矿型氧化物SrVO₃，通过数值模拟验证了方案的有效性。

Conclusion: 所提出的量子-经典混合DMFT方案能够在不预先知道激发通道的情况下从QPE采样中可靠重构单粒子格林函数，为在量子计算机上处理关联电子系统提供了可行途径。

Abstract: For treating correlated electronic systems on quantum computers, we propose a quantum-classical hybrid scheme for dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT). In the quantum part of the scheme, we use modified quantum phase estimation (QPE) circuits suitable for the one-particle Green's function (GF) at a finite temperature so that we can extract spectral amplitudes and the excitation energies without knowing the excitation channel invoked at each measurement. In the classical part of the scheme, we adopt an approach that estimates reasonably the GF based on the data collected from the QPE sampling. We dub the approach the QPE averaged over variable grids (QAVG), that may help one to reconstruct the GF via optimization of trial parameters and modeling the probability distributions for various settings of the QPE circuits. We apply the QAVG-DMFT scheme to SrVO$_3$ to demonstrate its validity via numerical simulations.

### [126] [Heralded ultrafast generation of macroscopic quantum states in matter with bright squeezed vacuum light](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30224)
*Shohei Imai*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，明亮压缩真空光（bright squeezed vacuum light）结合单次正交测量，能够在弱耦合条件下通过正交基的标识（heralding）机制，在物质系统中超快制备宏观量子态，包括Dicke态和猫态（cat-like state）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索利用多光子量子光（multiphoton quantum light）在弱耦合体系中高效制备物质的宏观量子态，克服传统方法在速度和可扩展性上的限制。

Method: 采用明亮压缩真空光与物质相互作用后的单次正交测量（single-shot quadrature measurement）作为标识方案；基于高斯加权叠加原理对电偶极耦合二能级系统（two-level systems）进行量子态工程。

Result: 在弱耦合条件下，标识动力学起到关于电极化（electric polarization）的高斯滤波器作用；更亮（brighter）的压缩真空光可加速零本征值Dicke态（zero-eigenvalue Dicke state）的制备；反旋转项（counter-rotating terms）进一步驱动从Dicke态到猫态的超快跃迁。

Abstract: We show that bright squeezed vacuum light, combined with a single-shot quadrature measurement of the post-interaction light, enables the ultrafast generation of macroscopic quantum states in matter. Although in the weak-coupling regime multiphoton quantum light leaves the unconditional matter state as a classical mixture due to light--matter entanglement, quadrature-based heralding prepares the matter in a Gaussian-weighted quantum superposition. For an ensemble of resonantly electric-dipole-coupled two-level systems, this heralding dynamics acts as a Gaussian filter with respect to the electric polarization, with brighter squeezed-vacuum light accelerating the preparation of the zero-eigenvalue Dicke state. Counter-rotating terms further drive a stroboscopic transition from this Dicke state to a cat-like state. Our results open a route to ultrafast engineering of macroscopic quantum matter with strong-field quantum light.

### [127] [Quantum Synchronization of Fock States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30271)
*Fabian Hassler,David Scheer,Samah Saquaque,Steven Kim*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文展示了玻色模的量子同步化（quantum synchronization），其极限环（limit cycle）呈现非经典的非负维格纳函数（negative Wigner function）的福克态（Fock state-like）特征；通过外部驱动实现相位锁定，并在阿诺德舌头（Arnold tongue）区域内发生同步化；同步化本质上是动力学特性，与相位滑移（phase slips）的抑制密切相关，后者概率呈指数衰减；提出了一种从林德布拉德时间演化（Lindblad time evolution）中提取相位滑移率的新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典系统中的同步化现象已得到广泛研究，但量子域中同步化的非经典特性（如非经典极限环态）尚未被充分理解，特别是与负维格纳函数等非经典特征的联系仍有待探索。

Method: 通过外部驱动对呈现福克态极限环的玻色模进行相位锁定，观察其阿诺德舌头内的同步化行为；利用林德布拉德主方程的时间演化，提取相位滑移率以定量描述同步化动力学。

Result: 实现了具有负维格纳函数的稳态的量子同步化，同步化发生在阿诺德舌头区域内；相位滑移被抑制，其概率呈指数衰减，表明同步化与相位滑移抑制存在根本性关联。

Conclusion: 量子同步化是一种动力学特性，其本质由相位滑移的指数抑制决定；所提出的相位滑移率提取方法为理解和操控非经典同步化动力学提供了新途径。

Abstract: Synchronization, a ubiquitous phenomenon in classical systems, has recently been extended to the quantum domain. Here, we show quantum synchronization of a bosonic mode exhibiting a Fock state-like limit cycle, manifesting as a steady state with a negative Wigner function. We demonstrate that this non-classical state can be phase-locked to an external drive, achieving synchronization within an Arnold tongue regime. We argue that synchronization is a dynamical property and fundamentally tied to the suppression of phase slips, which we show to occur with exponentially decreasing probability. We introduce a novel method to extract the phase slip rate from the Lindblad time evolution of the system. This work opens new avenues for understanding and manipulating non-classical synchronization dynamics.

</details>


### [128] [Quantum Desynchronization of Limit Cycles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30302)
*Hans Christiansen,Jens Paaske*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文利用Keldysh路径积分（Keldysh path integral）描述极限环（limit cycles）的相位动力学，证明量子相位滑移（quantum phase slips）会破坏连续变量量子系统的相位锁定，类似于经典同步中噪声导致的相位滑移。研究还分析了非马尔可夫效应（non-Markovian effects）对同步的影响，并以超导谐振器通过电压偏置双量子点耦合为例进行了阐明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典弱耦合自激振荡器（self-sustained oscillators）可自发实现相位锁定（phase locking），但噪声会导致同步失效。论文旨在探究连续变量量子系统中同步失效的机制，即量子相位滑移如何破坏相位锁定。

Method: 采用Keldysh路径积分（Keldysh path integral）形式构建极限环（limit cycles）的相位动力学，分析量子相位滑移（quantum phase slips）对相位锁定的影响，并扩展处理非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）效应。

Result: 量子相位滑移（quantum phase slips）的增殖会破坏连续变量量子系统的实际相位锁定，尽管系统存在强相位关联（phase correlations）。

Conclusion: 连续变量量子系统的同步失效机制与经典同步类似，但源于量子相位滑移而非经典噪声。该框架还可用于研究非马尔可夫效应对极限环同步的影响，并通过超导谐振器与双量子点耦合体系给出具体示例。

Abstract: It is well known from classical physics that weakly coupled self-sustained oscillators may spontaneously lock their phases. Just like classical synchronization is known to break down due to noise induced phase slips, we show here how the synchronization of continuous variable quantum systems breaks down by proliferation of quantum phase slips. Within a Keldysh path integral formulation of limit cycles, we analyze the phase dynamics and show how, in spite of strong phase correlations, quantum phase slips degrade the actual phase locking. This approach also allows us to address non-Markovian effects on the synchronization of limit cycles, which we illustrate explicitly for superconducting resonators coupled via a voltage biased double quantum dot.

</details>

### [129] [Comment on "Spin-1/2 Kagome Heisenberg Antiferromagnet: Machine Learning Discovery of the Spinon Pair-Density-Wave Ground State"](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28861)
*Helia Kamal,Dominik Kufel,DinhDuy Vu,Chris R. Laumann,Norman Y. Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文指出，近期一篇声称利用群等变卷积神经网络（group-equivariant convolutional neural network）在kagome海森堡反铁磁体研究中取得突破的论文，其低变分能量源于Metropolis-Hastings采样中单自旋翻转更新规则导致的遍历性破缺（broken ergodicity）；在强制实现遍历采样后，神经网络收敛能量显著高于已有密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）结果，原论文结论存疑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证一篇2025年发表于Physical Review X的论文中所报告的、基于群等变卷积神经网络（group-equivariant convolutional neural network）的kagome海森堡反铁磁体变分能量是否可靠，以及其声称的自旋子对密度波（spinon pair-density-wave）基态是否真实。

Method: 通过分析原论文使用的Metropolis-Hastings采样中单自旋翻转更新规则的动力学行为，检验其是否导致马尔可夫链（Markov chain）冻结；随后引入自旋交换更新（spin-exchange update）以强制实现遍历采样（ergodic sampling），重新训练神经网络并比较所得能量与密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）结果。

Result: 原论文中报告的低变分能量是Metropolis-Hastings采样下单自旋翻转更新规则导致遍历性破缺（broken ergodicity）的伪影；改用自旋交换更新实现遍历采样后，神经网络收敛到的能量显著高于现有密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）计算结果。

Conclusion: 原论文的声称因方法学缺陷（遍历性破缺）不可靠，其结论应受到质疑。

Abstract: A recent article [Phys. Rev. X 15, 011047 (2025)] utilizes group-equivariant convolutional neural networks to study the ground state of the kagome Heisenberg antiferromagnet. On the largest finite-size cluster studied to date ($N=108$), the authors report variational energies significantly lower than other numerical methods, including state-of-the-art density matrix renormalization group (DMRG) calculations. In contrast to previous results suggesting a possible spin-liquid ground state, the authors observe a spinon pair-density-wave ground state. We find that: (i) the reported low energies are artifacts of broken ergodicity in the Metropolis--Hastings sampling, since the single-spin-flip update rule utilized by the authors effectively freezes the Markov chains; and (ii) when ergodic sampling is enforced via spin-exchange updates, the neural network converges to energies significantly higher than existing DMRG results, calling the paper's claims into question.

</details>


### [130] [Improving CFT Operators Using Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28929)
*Lior Oppenheim,Snir Gazit,Zohar Ringel*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种数据驱动的格点算符（lattice operator）改进方法，通过增强与连续共形场论（conformal field theory）中原始算符（primary operator）的重叠（overlap），有效减小有限尺寸效应（finite-size effects）对共形数据（conformal data）提取精度的影响。在伊辛模型（Ising model）、q=3 Potts模型及稀q=3 Potts模型三个二维临界系统（critical system）中，该方法得到的领先自旋算符（spin operator）和能量算符（energy operator）均表现出更小的标度修正（corrections to scaling），并给出更精确的标度维度（scaling dimension）估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在临界系统的格点模拟（lattice simulation）中，有限尺寸效应限制了从模拟数据中提取共形数据的精度。现有的作用量改进（action improvement）虽能抑制部分标度修正（corrections to scaling），但无法解决由格点对连续共形场（continuum conformal field）的不完美表示所导致的算符依赖效应（operator-dependent effects）。因此，需要一种能够直接改进格点算符本身的方法。

Method: 提出一种数据驱动（data-driven）方法，通过构造与连续共形场论（conformal field theory）中原始算符（primary operator）具有更强重叠（overlap）的格点算符估计量（estimator），直接改进格点算符的表示。该方法不需要对作用量进行修改，而是从模拟数据中优化算符的构建。

Result: 在伊辛模型（Ising model）、q=3 Potts模型以及稀q=3 Potts模型三个二维临界系统（critical system）中，该方法得到的领先自旋算符（spin operator）和能量算符（energy operator）均表现出更小的标度修正（corrections to scaling），并给出了比传统格点算符（conventional lattice operator）选择更准确的标度维度（scaling dimension）估计。

Conclusion: 数据驱动的格点算符改进方法能够有效提高临界系统格点模拟中共形数据（conformal data）的提取精度。该方法具有通用性，且所有代码与分析工作流已开源在GitHub仓库中，便于他人复现和应用。

Abstract: Finite-size effects limit the accuracy with which conformal data can be extracted from lattice simulations of critical systems. While action improvement suppresses some corrections to scaling, it does not address operator-dependent effects arising from imperfect lattice representations of continuum conformal fields. In this work, we propose a data-driven method for improving lattice operators themselves, constructing estimators with enhanced overlap with the corresponding primary operators of the continuum conformal field theory. We identify improved lattice representations of leading spin and energy operators in three two-dimensional critical systems: the Ising model, the q = 3 Potts model, and the dilute q = 3 Potts model. In all cases, the resulting operators exhibit reduced corrections to scaling and yield more accurate estimates of scaling dimensions compared to conventional lattice choices. The code and analysis workflows used to produce these results are made available in an accompanying GitHub repository.

</details>


### [131] [Controlled Loop Expansion for Strained Twisted Bilayer Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28937)
*Eyal Keshet,Yaar Vituri,Erez Berg*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文为周期安德森模型（periodic Anderson model）建立了一种受控的图解框架（diagrammatic framework），并将其应用于异质应变魔角扭曲双层石墨烯（MATBG）。通过小参数 $s^2$（莫尔布里渊区中具有非平庸量子几何的分数）进行戴森重求和（Dyson resummation），发现在应变条件下该展开在低温下可控。平坦手征极限下，涌现的近似 $\rm{U}(1)$ 对称性抑制了主导散射通道，使莫特带（Mott band）在 $s^2$ 阶保持尖锐；偏离手征极限时，线宽非零但比无应变情况小一个数量级以上。应变还引入类电子-声子扭结和新平带“三子”（trion）带。该框架还被用于预测量子扭结显微镜谱，并与实验对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为周期安德森模型建立一种受控的图解框架，解决现有方法在低能强关联区域（如魔角扭曲双层石墨烯）难以系统展开的问题。

Method: 基于 arXiv:2604.14278，构建自能插入（self-energy insertions）并进行戴森重求和（Dyson resummation），将展开控制在 $s^2$（莫尔布里渊区中具有非平庸量子几何的分数）的各阶。在异质应变魔角扭曲双层石墨烯体系中，利用拓扑重费米子表述（topological heavy-fermion formulation）进行分析。

Result: 应变条件下，该展开在应变能标不过小时可低至任意温度皆可控。平坦手征极限下，涌现的近似 $\rm{U}(1)$ 对称性抑制了主导散射通道，使莫特带在 $s^2$ 阶依然尖锐（对比无应变情况线宽为 $N_f s^2 U$ 量级）。偏离手征极限时，$s^2$ 阶线宽非零，但比无应变情况小一个数量级以上。应变能标在谱中以类电子-声子扭结（electron-phonon-like kink）和额外平坦“三子”带（trion band）的形式显现。计算得到单圈阶（one-loop order）的量子扭结显微镜谱（Quantum Twisting Microscope spectrum），并与近期实验对比。

Conclusion: 所建立的图解框架可有效处理应变魔角扭曲双层石墨烯中的强关联问题，揭示了应变对莫特带线宽的显著抑制效应以及应变诱导的新谱特征（扭结与三子带），为解释相关实验提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We develop a controlled diagrammatic framework for periodic Anderson models,and apply it to heterostrained magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene (MATBG) at charge neutrality using the topological heavy-fermion formulation. Building on arXiv:2604.14278, we organize self-energy insertions and perform a Dyson resummation to any order in the small parameter $s^2$ -- the fraction of the moiré Brillouin zone with nontrivial quantum geometry. For strained MATBG, the expansion remains controlled down to arbitrarily low temperatures as long as the strain induced energy scale is not too small. In the flat-chiral limit, an emergent approximate $\rm{U}(1)$ symmetry forbids the leading scattering channel and leaves the Mott bands sharp at order $s^2$. This is in stark contrast to the unstrained case, where the linewidth is of order $N_f s^2 U$ with $U$ the on-site $f$-$f$ Hubbard interaction and $N_f$ the number of $f$ states per site. Away from the chiral limit, the linewidth is non-zero at order $s^2$ but more than an order of magnitude smaller than in the unstrained case. The strain-induced energy scale also imprints itself directly on the spectrum: as an electron-phonon-like kink in the dispersion, and as an additional flat ``trion'' band -- a single-particle excitation bound to a local $f$ particle-hole pair. We use the framework to predict the Quantum Twisting Microscope spectrum at one-loop order for both strained and unstrained MATBG, and compare with recent experiments.

</details>


### [132] [Topological superconductivity from Abelian fractional Chern insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29034)
*Taige Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文基于U(3)红外部分子理论（infrared parton theory），系统地分析了ν=1/3分数量子陈绝缘体（fractional Chern insulator, FCI）中的超导配对机制，揭示了三种不同的超导相及其与Laughlin anyon流体、电荷密度波（charge density wave, CDW）之间的统一理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Laughlin anyon流体是否能转变为拓扑超导体（topological superconductor），并统一描述ν=1/3 FCI及其邻近的CDW态与超导态之间的内在关联。

Method: 采用U(3)红外部分子理论，将电子视为三个电荷为e/3的组成粒子（constituent），通过这三个组成粒子的配对形成规范不变的电荷2e库珀对（Cooper pair），从而分析不同超导态的性质。

Result: 该框架预测了三类超导态：保留母体Laughlin U(1)₃序的SC*相、手征拓扑超导体（chiral topological superconductor）c_-=3/2相、以及强配对anyon超导体（strong-pairing anyon superconductor）c_-=3相。此外，还得到了一个σ_xy=0的CDW态。在公度填充下，正常态及c_-=3和c_-=3/2的超导后裔与周期三密度序背景自然关联，而SC*分支可保持微观平移对称性。非公度填充下，chargon金属可配入c_-=3/2拓扑超导体。

Conclusion: FCI态、再入CDW态和手征超导态在U(3)部分子理论中得到统一描述，表明anyo流体可以通过部分子配对机制自然地转变为多种类型的拓扑超导体。

Abstract: Can a Laughlin anyon fluid become a topological superconductor? We answer this question for a $ν=1/3$ fractional Chern insulator (FCI) using a $U(3)$ infrared parton theory. Three charge-$e/3$ constituents form the electron, while three constituent pairs form a gauge-invariant charge-$2e$ Cooper pair. The resulting superconductors share an ordinary charge-$2e$ sector but differ in their neutral color response, giving an SC$^\ast$ with the parent Laughlin $U(1)_3$ order, a chiral topological superconductor with $c_-=3/2$, and a strong-pairing anyon superconductor with $c_-=3$. The same framework organizes a nearby $σ_{xy}=0$ charge density wave (CDW) state. At commensurate filling, the normal state and the $c_-=3$ and $c_-=3/2$ superconducting descendants are naturally tied to a period-three density order background, while the SC$^\ast$ branch can preserve microscopic translations. Away from commensuration, a chargon metal can pair into the same $c_-=3/2$ topological superconductor. The FCI, reentrant CDW, and chiral superconductivity are unified in the $U(3)$ parton theory.

</details>


### [133] [Strongly-coupled hybrid lattice-plasmons in layered cuprates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29100)
*Ke-Jun Xu,Nathan Giles-Donovan,Stefano Agrestini,Jaewon Choi,Mirian Garcia-Fernandez,Kejin Zhou,Junfeng He,Costel R. Rotundu,Young S. Lee,Thomas P. Devereaux,Zhi-Xun Shen,Dung-Hai Lee,Robert J. Birgeneau,Wei-Sheng Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究利用共振非弹性X射线散射（RIXS）追踪电子掺杂铜氧化物Nd2-xCexCuO4中从金属态到Mott绝缘态的集体电荷激发演化，揭示了从声学等离激元（acoustic plasmon）到能隙杂化模，再到与氧呼吸声子耦合的139 meV激发的连续转变，建立了电子掺杂铜氧化物相图中集体电荷激发的统一图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在离域价电子的金属体系和电子被束缚于离子的传统绝缘体之间，集体电荷激发的中间态行为尚不清楚，这对理解强关联体系（如层状铜氧化物）中位于Mott局域化与巡游性边界上的电荷动力学至关重要。

Method: 采用共振非弹性X射线散射（resonant inelastic X-ray scattering, RIXS）技术，对原型电子掺杂铜氧化物Nd2-xCexCuO4中低能电荷响应随掺杂浓度的演化进行实验追踪。

Result: 发现了低能电荷响应的连续转变：金属态中的声学等离激元（acoustic plasmon）→中间掺杂的能隙杂化模→半填充（half filling）时近无色散的139 meV激发。该139 meV激发能量约为角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）中色散扭结（kink）对应的氧呼吸声子能量的两倍，与拉曼光谱中观测到的双声子激发（2-phonon excitation）一致。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了电子掺杂铜氧化物相图中集体电荷激发的统一图像，表明此类模式通过强耦合到晶格自由度（lattice degrees of freedom）而跨越Mott转变持续存在，揭示了载流子掺杂Mott绝缘体中电荷动力学的一个缺失环节。

Abstract: Metallic systems with delocalized valence electrons host collective charge density oscillations known as plasmons. On the other hand, conventional insulators do not have free electrons and the low energy charge degrees of freedom are pinned to the ions. The fate of the collective charge excitations in the intermediate regime is an outstanding question. This problem is especially important for strongly correlated systems such as the layered cuprates, where unconventional superconductivity and other emergent phenomena arise from valence electrons on the border between Mott localization and itinerancy. Using resonant inelastic X-ray scattering, we track this evolution in the prototypical electron-doped cuprate Nd2-xCexCuO4. We find a continuous transformation of the low-energy charge response: from an acoustic plasmon in the metallic regime, to a gapped hybrid mode at intermediate doping, and finally to a nearly dispersionless 139 meV excitation at half filling. Remarkably, the 139 meV excitation has approximately twice the energy of the oxygen breathing phonon responsible for the dispersion kink observed in angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, and is consistent with a putative 2-phonon excitation observed in Raman spectroscopy. These results establish a unified picture of collective charge excitations across the phase diagram of electron-doped cuprates, showing that such modes persist across the Mott transition via strong coupling to lattice degrees of freedom and revealing a missing link in the charge dynamics of carrier doped Mott insulators.

</details>


### [134] [Tetrahedrally ferromagnetic correlations and a glassy-freezing anomaly in the breathing pyrochlore magnet $\mathrm{AgInCr_4S_8}$ with partial $A$-site disorder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29349)
*Yuya Haraguchi,Masahiro Kitamura,Masaki Gen,Yusuke Nambu,Akira Matsuo,Koichi Kindo,Masaki Kondo,Masashi Tokunaga,Hiroko Aruga Katori*

TL;DR: 本文通过同步辐射X射线与中子粉末衍射、直流磁化率和热容测量，系统研究了铬基呼吸烧绿石（breathing pyrochlore）硫化物AgInCr₄S₈。实验确认了其F¯43m呼吸结构、大的呼吸比及约16%的A位Ag/In互占，未发现长程磁有序，但在约9 K处观测到类似玻璃态冻结（glassy-freezing）的磁异常，表明短程铁磁关联与淬灭A位无序（quenched A-site disorder）的竞争主导了其低温磁性行为。

Method: 采用同步辐射X射线衍射（synchrotron x-ray diffraction）、中子粉末衍射（neutron powder diffraction）、直流磁化率（dc magnetization）和热容（heat capacity）等多种实验手段对AgInCr₄S₈进行表征。

Conclusion: AgInCr₄S₈中强呼吸畸变和A位淬灭无序共同抑制了长程磁有序，产生了以有效S = 6簇磁矩（cluster moment）为特征的短程铁磁关联与低温玻璃态冻结行为，为理解呼吸烧绿石中的磁无序竞争提供了重要范例。

Abstract: We investigate the chromium breathing pyrochlore sulfide $\mathrm{AgInCr_4S_8}$, a chromium-based thiospinel, by synchrotron x-ray and neutron powder diffraction, dc magnetization, and heat capacity. Diffraction confirms the $F\bar{4}3m$ breathing structure with alternating large and small $\mathrm{Cr_4}$ tetrahedra, a large breathing ratio ($d^\prime/d = 1.106$ at 300 K), and substantial Ag/In intermixing on the $A$ sublattice ($\sim 16\%$). No structural transition or magnetic Bragg peaks are detected down to 1.5 K. An enlarged low-angle difference plot between the 1.5 and 20 K neutron diffraction patterns shows a weak broad diffuse-like enhancement, consistent with short-range or frozen correlated moments within the sensitivity of the present data. Susceptibility yields a positive Weiss temperature $θ_{\mathrm{W}} = +92$ K and a moment enhancement in 30--60 K, while the magnetic entropy released by $\sim 30$ K approaches a scale of order $R\ln 13$, together consistent with the development of short-range tetrahedral ferromagnetic correlations and an effective $S = 6$ cluster-moment picture. A broad susceptibility cusp with ZFC--FC bifurcation and a low-temperature specific heat anomaly near 9 K indicate a phenomenological glassy-freezing anomaly without long-range order. $\mathrm{AgInCr_4S_8}$ provides a benchmark for the interplay of strong breathing distortion and quenched $A$-site disorder in chromium breathing pyrochlores.

### [135] [Shear Viscosity at the van Hove singularity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29501)
*Yi-Hui Xing,Wu-Ming Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过图解久保形式（diagrammatic Kubo formalism）计算了范霍夫奇点处的临界输运系数，发现电导率与玻尔兹曼结果一致，但直流剪切粘滞度表现出定性不同的行为，揭示了强关联系统中半经典玻尔兹曼输运理论的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强关联系统中，准粒子激发定义不明确，半经典玻尔兹曼输运理论（semiclassical Boltzmann transport theory）的适用性受到根本挑战。特别地，当费米子谱展宽远大于玻色子展宽时，输运的玻尔兹曼方法在临界区域的脏极限下未必有效，因此需要更可靠的量子输运理论框架。

Method: 采用图解久保形式计算多个临界输运系数；同时在费米子尖峰近似（fermion sharp peak approximation）下证明领头阶费曼图可约化为玻尔兹曼方程，并指出该近似在脏临界极限下严格失效。

Result: 在范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularity）处，电导率意外地与玻尔兹曼结果一致，但直流剪切粘滞度（dc shear viscosity）表现出定性不同的行为。该临界模型给出了光学和直流剪切粘滞度的实验可检验预言：Re[η(Ω)]∼(|Ω|^{3/2}+T^{3/2})/Ω² 以及 Re[η(Ω=0)]∼T。

Conclusion: 图解久保形式的结果比玻尔兹曼方法更可靠；该模型还能解释奇异金属（strange metal）行为，为评估理论框架的有效性提供了实验检验机会。

Abstract: The applicability of the semiclassical Boltzmann transport theory is fundamentally challenged in strongly correlated systems where quasiparticle excitations are ill-defined. When the fermion spectral broadening becomes much larger than the boson broadening, the Boltzmann approach to transport is not always valid, particularly in the dirty limit of the critical regime. Using a diagrammatic Kubo formalism, we compute several critical transport coefficients at a van Hove singularity and show that, while the conductivity happens to agree with the Boltzmann result, the dc shear viscosity exhibits qualitatively different behavior. The diagrammatic Kubo results are more reliable because, under the fermion sharp peak approximation--an assumption that strictly breaks down in the dirty critical limit--we demonstrate that the leading order Feynman diagrams reduce to the Boltzmann equation. The same critical model, which can also account for strange metal, makes experimentally testable predictions for the optical and dc shear viscosities, ${\rm Re}[η(Ω)]\sim (|Ω|^{3/2}+T^{3/2})/Ω^2$ and ${\rm Re}[η(Ω=0)]\sim T$, providing further opportunities to assess the validity of our theoretical framework.

TL;DR: 本文通过slave-rotor方法研究Lieb晶格上交变磁Hubbard模型在位点排斥相互作用U驱动下的金属-绝缘体相变，发现系统经历从正常金属到交变磁金属、交变磁绝缘体、再到交变磁Mott绝缘体的级联相变过程，且自旋劈裂在Mott绝缘相中被显著抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究交变磁（altermagnetic）Hubbard模型中由在位相互作用U驱动的金属-绝缘体相变（metal-insulator transition）及其微观机制，特别是自旋劈裂（spin splitting）在不同关联强度下的行为。

Method: 采用slave-rotor方法（slave-rotor approach）在Lieb晶格（Lieb lattice）上对半填充（half filling）的交变磁Hubbard模型进行分析，并结合电子谱函数（electronic spectral function）计算进行验证。

Result: 随着U增加，系统呈现级联相变：正常金属 → 交变磁金属 → 交变磁绝缘体 → 交变磁Mott绝缘体（quasiparticle weight完全消失）。电子谱函数在金属和绝缘态均显示自旋劈裂能带，但Mott绝缘相中自旋劈裂被显著抑制。

Abstract: We investigate the metal-insulator transition driven by the onsite repulsive interaction $U$ in an altermagnetic Hubbard model defined on a Lieb lattice. Using the slave-rotor approach at half filling, we find that the system exhibits a cascade of interaction-driven phase transitions. As $U$ increases, the system evolves from a normal metal to an altermagnetic metal, then to an altermagnetic insulator, and eventually to an altermagnetic Mott insulator characterized by the complete suppression of the quasiparticle weight. These phases are supported by the calculation of the electronic spectral function, which features spin-split bands in both the metallic and insulating regimes. However, the spin splitting becomes substantially suppressed in the Mott insulating phase. Our results suggest that the observation of spin splitting in the spectral function of $d$-wave altermagnets with a Lieb-lattice-like structure may be limited to the weak-to-moderate correlation regime.

### [137] [Electronic Origin of Ferromagnetic Excitations in the Candidate Spin-Triplet Superconductor CeSb2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30074)
*Xiaoxiao Wang,Xiaoyang Chen,Suppanut Sangphet,Yifei Fang,Yilin Wang,Chihao Li,Minyinan Lei,Nan Guo,Yuanhe Song,Rui Peng,Haichao Xu,Donglai Feng*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）实验揭示了准二维晶格材料CeSb₂中准一维铁磁（FM）激发的电子起源——能带选择性近藤耦合（band-selective Kondo coupling）机制，该机制产生强各向异性磁交换相互作用，可自然解释准一维铁磁激发和竞争磁有序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 候选自旋三重态超导体CeSb₂中准一维铁磁激发的起源此前尚不明确，需要阐明其微观物理机制。

Method: 采用高分辨角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）和共振ARPES技术，观测费米口袋上的能隙、Ce 4f谱权重增强及各向异性特征。

Result: 高分辨ARPES未在色散费米口袋上探测到自旋密度波（spin-density-wave）能隙，排除了嵌套驱动（nesting-driven）机制；共振ARPES发现Ce 4f谱权重在沿Ce梯子（Ce ladder）排列的C₂分布费米口袋上出现显著选择性增强。

Conclusion: 实验结果表明，能带选择性近藤耦合是关联f电子体系中低维磁性涌现的微观机制，可同时解释准一维铁磁激发与竞争磁有序的共存。

Abstract: The origin of quasi-one-dimensional (q1D) ferromagnetic (FM) excitations in the candidate spin-triplet superconductor CeSb$_2$ has remained unclear. Here we report an electronic mechanism for emergent q1D magnetism in the quasi-two-dimensional lattice of CeSb$_2$, revealed by angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES). High-resolution ARPES resolves no spin-density-wave gap on the dispersive Fermi pockets, disfavoring a nesting-driven mechanism for the q1D FM excitations. Instead, resonant ARPES reveals a pronounced selective enhancement of Ce 4$f$ spectral weight on the $C_2$-distributed Fermi pockets aligned with the Ce ladder. This observation signifies band-selective Kondo coupling that generates strongly anisotropic magnetic exchange interactions, which can naturally account for both the q1D ferromagnetic excitations and the competing magnetic orders. Our results identify a band-selective Kondo coupling mechanism for emergent low-dimensional magnetism in correlated $f$-electron systems.

### [138] [Neural Scaling Laws for Jet Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28940)
*Oz Amram,Darius A. Faroughy,Tjarko Gerdes,Anna Hallin,Gregor Kasieczka,Michael Krämer,Humberto Reyes-Gonzalez,David Shih*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次探索了粒子喷注生成（particle jet generation）任务中的缩放定律（scaling laws），发现模型规模缩放呈现对数缩放行为，但数据集规模和计算量缩放明显弱于语言模型，并引入“可学习窗口”（learnable window）概念解释这一现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期经验缩放定律描述了基础模型在数据集规模、计算量和模型参数三方面变化时的性能规律，但传统调参方式对大规模复杂模型不可行。本文首次探究粒子喷注生成任务中是否也存在类似的缩放定律，该任务既可作为基础模型的预训练目标，也可作为原位模拟（in-situ simulation）工具。

Method: 研究对自回归生成模型（autoregressive generative model）进行缩放定律分析，同时考察下一个词元预测验证损失（next token prediction validation loss）和五种物理量的切片Wasserstein距离（sliced Wasserstein distance）。引入“可学习窗口”概念分析弱缩放行为。

Result: 模型规模缩放呈现对数缩放行为；切片Wasserstein距离与下一个词元预测验证损失呈单调关系，表明该损失可作为物理性能的良好代理指标。数据集规模和计算量缩放则表现出明显弱化的缩放行为，自回归下一个词元预测在喷注成分上相比语言模型研究更快达到饱和。

Conclusion: 模型规模缩放符合对数缩放定律，但数据集和计算量缩放显著弱于语言模型。可能的成因包括量子色动力学辐射（QCD radiation）的随机性以及生成式与监督式学习任务在对撞机物理中的差异。

Abstract: Recently observed empirical scaling laws describe the performance of foundation-type models as three independent key quantities -- dataset size, compute, and model parameters -- are modified. Extracting these scaling laws informs the training of large complex models for which the tuning of hyperparameters in traditional ways is not feasible. This work for the first time explores if scaling laws can also be observed for the task of particle jet generation -- both relevant as a pre-training objective for foundation models and as in-situ simulation by itself. We indeed replicate the key logarithmic scaling law behavior for model-size scaling. Beyond studying the next token prediction validation loss of the generative model, we also study the sliced Wasserstein distance of five physical quantities that are not immediately available to the model during training. Our study shows that this quantity is monotonically related to the next token prediction validation loss, meaning that this loss is indeed a good proxy for the physics performance. For the scaling with dataset size and compute, we observe substantially weaker scaling behavior of both the loss and the sliced Wasserstein distance. We analyze this behavior by introducing the concept of a learnable window, and argue that autoregressive next token prediction on jet constituents exhibits comparatively rapid saturation relative to language-model studies. We discuss possible origins of this behavior, including the stochastic nature of QCD radiation and differences between generative and supervised learning tasks in collider physics.

</details>


### [139] [Twilight of the WIMP: Comprehensive Phenomenology of Electroweak Triplet Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29031)
*Gaurav,Niharika Shrivastava,Rahul Srivastava,Sushant Yadav*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了电弱三重态标量或费米子作为暗物质候选者的现象学，发现仅有Y=0的费米子三重态暗物质参数空间仍存活，且位于未来间接探测实验的灵敏度范围内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型（Standard Model）无法解释暗物质（dark matter）的存在，因此有必要研究超越标准模型的新物理中提出并检验暗物质候选者。

Method: 在标准模型扩展中引入超荷（hypercharge）Y=0或Y=2的电弱三重态（electroweak triplet）标量或费米子，通过Z₂离散对称性稳定暗物质；随后对参数空间进行细致分析，施加包括 relic abundance、直接探测（direct detection）和间接探测（indirect detection）约束在内的宇宙学与实验限制。

Result: Y=0标量三重态被 relic density、直接探测与间接探测联合排除；Y=2的标量和费米子三重态因大自旋无关散射截面（spin-independent scattering cross-section）被直接探测实验排除；Y=0费米子三重态存在存活参数空间，位于近期未来实验的预期灵敏度内。

Conclusion: 在四种电弱三重态暗物质候选者中，仅Y=0的费米子三重态仍未排除，其间接探测信号有望被下一代实验检验，附录还讨论了对撞机（collider）上的探测前景。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive study of dark matter phenomenology in standard model extensions featuring an electroweak triplet scalar or fermion with hypercharge $Y = 0$ or $Y = 2$. These minimal triplet extensions provide well-motivated dark matter candidates stabilised by the $Z_2$ discrete symmetry. We perform a detailed analysis of the parameter space consistent with current cosmological and experimental constraints, including the relic abundance, direct detection limits, and indirect detection bounds. We find that the scalar triplet with $Y=0$ is ruled out by a combination of relic density, direct detection and indirect detection constraints. On the other hand, the scalar and fermionic triplets with $Y=2$ are both excluded by current direct detection experiments due to their large spin-independent scattering cross-sections. The viable parameter space of the remaining $Y=0$ fermion triplet dark matter lies within the projected sensitivity of near-future experiments, particularly those targeting indirect detection signatures. Collider prospects for these triplet extensions are also discussed in the Appendix.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用tau轻子（tau lepton）μ子衰变产生的起始径迹事件中可见非弹性度系统性大于μ子中微子相互作用事件这一特征，实现两种味（flavor）的统计分离。采用真实IceCube曝光量和探测器性能参数进行分析。

Conclusion: 起始径迹非弹性度（starting-track inelasticity）是一种强大且即时可用的天体物理中微子味测量探针，也可用于探索超出标准中微子混合（beyond standard neutrino mixing）的新物理。

Abstract: Astrophysical neutrinos provide a unique probe of neutrino flavor changes over cosmological baselines. While the tau component of the neutrino flux is expected to arise almost entirely from mixing, current measurements rely primarily on rare double-cascade signatures. We investigate a complementary method to measure the tau fraction using the visible inelasticity of starting track events in neutrino telescopes. Muonic decays of tau leptons produce tracks with systematically larger visible inelasticity than those from muon neutrino interactions, potentially enabling statistical separation of the two flavors. Using realistic IceCube exposures and detector performance, we show that this observable already yields competitive sensitivity to the tau-to-muon flux ratio, $R_{τμ}$, achievable with existing data. This approach may further enable flavor measurements of individual sources and the selection of tau-enhanced source catalogs. Starting-track inelasticity thus provides a powerful and immediately accessible probe of astrophysical neutrino flavor and of potential physics beyond standard neutrino mixing.

Method: 通过引入更高维相互作用（higher-dimensional interactions）并利用对准极限（alignment limit）下希格斯-标量混合被抑制的条件，重新组织新标量粒子的衰变模式；构建了两个代表性实现：单标量扩展模型（single-scalar extension）和双单态模型（two-singlet scenario）。

Abstract: Contrary to conventional expectations, we identify a class of extended scalar-sector scenarios in which final states with two, three, or four Higgs bosons constitute the leading discovery channels for new physics at the LHC. In these scenarios, higher-dimensional interactions, together with suppressed Higgs-scalar mixing near the alignment limit, reorganize the decay patterns of new scalar states, suppressing conventional modes while enhancing multi-Higgs final states. We illustrate the emergence of dominant triple- and quadruple-Higgs signatures in two representative realizations: a single-scalar extension of the Standard Model, where higher-dimensional operators suppress conventional two-body decays while preserving couplings to higher-multiplicity Higgs final states; and a two-singlet scenario, where similar signatures arise through cascade decays with a simpler operator structure. In both cases, the new scalar states can be produced via gluon fusion, yielding potentially observable rates for multi-Higgs production at the LHC. Although both realizations lead to identical final states, they exhibit distinct kinematic features reflecting their underlying topologies, providing a direct handle on the dynamics.

### [142] [FunKit: A computer algebra toolkit for functional approaches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28935)
*Franz R. Sattler*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: FunKit 是一个 Mathematica 软件包，用于从任意主方程推导和追踪泛函方程；它提供了表达式词汇与规则集，支持多种场论方程（如 Dyson–Schwinger 方程、泛函重整化群方程等），并能将推导结果导出为 C++、Julia 或 Fortran 代码进行数值评估。

Method: FunKit 构建了一套表达式词汇（expression vocabulary）与规则集（set of rules），使用户能够从任意主方程出发进行泛函推导。该软件包可与 \FORM 语言接口对接，高效追踪大张量表达式；同时提供代码生成功能，将任意 Mathematica 表达式（包括推导结果）导出为 C++、Julia 或 Fortran 代码。追踪和代码生成两个模块也可独立使用，并与其他软件包组合。

Result: FunKit 能够处理多种场论方程系统，包括 Dyson–Schwinger 方程、泛函重整化群（functional RG）方程、流动重参数化（flowing reparametrisations）、nPI 方程、(修正的) Slavnov–Taylor 恒等式与 Ward–Takahashi 恒等式、泛函 Polchinski 流和 Wegner 流、带源的泛函主方程等。此外，FunKit 实现了将符号推导结果直接转换为 C++、Julia 或 Fortran 代码的能力，支持后续数值评估。

Conclusion: FunKit 提供了一种通用、可扩展的泛函方程推导与追踪框架，适用于广泛的场论系统，并有效连接了符号推导与高性能数值计算。其独立模块设计也便于与其他现有工具协同使用。

Abstract: We introduce FunKit, a Mathematica package for the derivation and tracing of functional equations from arbitrary master equations. FunKit provides an expression vocabulary and a set of rules that allow for derivations in any given field theory and master equation. It also allows users to add extensions for more specific equation systems. Therefore, it can be used in a wide range of situations, for example Dyson--Schwinger or functional RG equations, flowing reparametrisations, nPI equations, (modified) STIs and WTIs, functional Polchinski and Wegner flows, functional master equations with sources, and many others. Besides interfacing with the \FORM language to trace large tensor expressions efficiently, FunKit also provides facilities to export arbitrary Mathematica expressions to C++, Julia or Fortran code, including the results of derivations, which can then be evaluated numerically. Both the tracing and code generation can also be used independently and in combination with other packages.

Abstract: We propose a new framework for solving the strong CP problem via a heavy axion, using mirror symmetry and grand unification. The mirror GUT sector remains unbroken and dynamically generates a calculable heavy mass scale via confinement without fine tuning. Models in this class feature a heavy axion, whose potential is less sensitive to Planck scale corrections, as well as a rich hidden sector from the confined mirror GUT. The solution to the strong CP problem remains unspoiled by the presence of additional phases in the GUT Yukawas, yet allowing the possibility of electric dipole moments within the reach of future experiments. Our proposal offers new directions in GUT model building, axion phenomenology, dark matter and cosmology.

### [144] [High-Quality Axion Dark Matter without Isocurvature Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29370)
*Masahiro Kawasaki,Jie Sheng,Tsutomu T. Yanagida*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文指出，在高尺度暴胀（high-scale inflation）场景中，由离散规范对称性（discrete gauge symmetry）保护的高质量轴子（high-quality axion）可自然避免等曲率扰动（isocurvature constraint）约束。通过引入一个破坏 Peccei-Quinn 对称性但保持规范不变性的算符，可在暴胀期间诱导出大的有效轴子质量，从而抑制轴子量子涨落，同时解决轴子质量问题与等曲率问题，并对未来实验可验证的轴子参数空间给出预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入一个既破坏 Peccei-Quinn 对称性又保持规范不变性的算符（Peccei-Quinn-violating but gauge-invariant operator），在暴胀期间诱导出大的有效轴子质量（effective axion mass），从而抑制轴子场的量子涨落。

Result: 该机制可同时解决轴子质量问题（axion quality problem）与等曲率问题（isocurvature problem），并对轴子参数空间（axion parameter space）给出可被未来实验检验的预言。

Conclusion: 离散规范对称性保护的高质量轴子能够自然规避等曲率约束，为高尺度暴胀中的轴子暗物质提供了一条自洽的理论路径，并通过参数空间预测与未来实验建立可检验的联系。

Abstract: Axion dark matter in high-scale inflation is subject to the isocurvature constraint, since quantum fluctuations of the axion field during inflation may exceed the current CMB bound. One conventional way to suppress these fluctuations is to assume that the Peccei-Quinn field has a large expectation value during inflation. However, this mechanism becomes ineffective when the axion domain wall number is large. In this work, we point out that a high-quality axion protected by a discrete gauge symmetry can naturally evade this problem. A Peccei-Quinn-violating but gauge-invariant operator induces a large effective axion mass during inflation, thereby suppressing the axion fluctuation. The same setup can address both the axion quality problem and the isocurvature problem, while leading to a prediction for the axion parameter space to be verified in future experiments.

### [146] [Thermodynamics in symmetry-improved Cornwall-Jackiw-Tomboulis formalism: application to the low-energy effective theory of QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29701)
*Yuepeng Guan,Mamiya Kawaguchi,Shinya Matsuzaki,Akio Tomiya*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 不同压力定义方案下的全局热力学结构保持稳定；定量差异集中于交叉过渡和一级相变区域附近。

Conclusion: 该研究为在对称性改进的2PI方法中构建热力学一致的观测值建立了实用的理论框架。

Abstract: We study the thermodynamics of the symmetry-improved Cornwall-Jackiw-Tomboulis (SICJT) formalism and apply it to a low-energy effective theory of QCD. In the symmetry-improved formulation, Ward-Takahashi identities are restored by auxiliary sources whose values are fixed self-consistently by the equilibrium state. While this construction improves the symmetry properties of the loop-wise truncated two-particle-irreducible (2PI) theory, it also makes the thermodynamic interpretation of the pressure nontrivial. We formulate several pressure prescriptions, including the conventional vacuum-subtracted pressure, a source-matched subtraction, and a pulled-back pressure in which the explicit source-induced energy shift is removed. Using the three-flavor linear sigma model with quarks, we analyze the equation of state, isentropic trajectories, adiabatic sound velocity, and trace anomaly across the chiral transition. We find that the global thermodynamic structure is stable under the different prescriptions, while quantitative differences are concentrated near the crossover and first-order transition region. These results establish a practical framework for constructing thermodynamically consistent observables in symmetry-improved 2PI approaches.

### [147] [HyperPrecision: A Mathematica package for High-Precision Numerical Evaluation of Multivariate Hypergeometric Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30216)
*Sumit Banik,Souvik Bera*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文介绍了HyperPrecision，一个用于高精度数值计算一般Horn型多元超几何函数（multivariate hypergeometric functions）及其在小参数ε下Laurent展开的Mathematica软件包。该软件包通过自动构建Pfaffian偏微分方程组并将其约化为一维常微分方程，再使用Frobenius方法求解，从而克服了超几何函数级数定义域受限与解析延拓困难的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多元超几何函数广泛出现在量子场论、弦论、数论和统计学等物理与数学领域，但其高精度数值计算面临严峻挑战，因其定义级数仅在有限区域内收敛，而超出该区域的解析延拓（analytic continuation）通常非平凡。

Method: HyperPrecision自动为给定超几何函数构建Pfaffian偏微分方程组（Pfaffian system of partial differential equations），将其限制在变量空间中连接起始点与目标点的一维轮廓（one-dimensional contour）上，从而得到常微分方程；随后采用Frobenius方法求解该常微分方程，边界条件由定义级数解析确定。

Result: 通过评估常见的多元超几何函数（包括Appell F₁、F₂、F₃、F₄函数，Horn G-和H-级数，以及Lauricella F_A、F_B、F_C、F_D函数）展示了该软件包的功能，并进一步应用于角度积分（angular integrals）、费曼积分（Feynman integrals）以及宇宙学和全息关联函数（cosmological and holographic correlators）的计算。

Conclusion: HyperPrecision提供了一种自动化的高精度数值计算方案，有效解决了多元超几何函数在受限收敛域之外的计算困难，并在多个前沿物理问题中展现了实用价值。

Abstract: In this paper, we present HyperPrecision, a Mathematica package for high-precision numerical evaluation of general Horn-type multivariate hypergeometric functions and their Laurent expansions in a small parameter $ε$. Such functions appear widely in physics and mathematics, with applications ranging from quantum field theory and string theory to number theory and statistics. Their high-precision numerical evaluation, however, remains challenging, since their defining series converge only in restricted domains and analytic continuation beyond these domains is, in general, non-trivial. HyperPrecision addresses this problem by automatically constructing the Pfaffian system of partial differential equations for a given hypergeometric function and restricting it to a one-dimensional contour in the space of variables connecting the starting to the target point. The resulting ordinary differential equation is then solved by the Frobenius method, with boundary conditions fixed analytically by the defining series. We illustrate the use of the package by evaluating commonly occurring multivariate hypergeometric functions, including the Appell $F_1$, $F_2$, $F_3$, and $F_4$ functions, the Horn $G$- and $H$-series, and the Lauricella $F_A$, $F_B$, $F_C$, and $F_D$ functions, as well as by considering applications to angular integrals, Feynman integrals, and cosmological and holographic correlators.

</details>

### [148] [Symmetry and integrability in the anyon-Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28956)
*Martin Bonkhoff,Grennon Gurney,Friethjof Theel,Peter Schmelcher,Nathan L. Harshman,Thore Posske*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文分析了有限长度任意子-哈伯德模型（anyon-Hubbard model）的对称性、可积性及简并性，揭示了对称性类在 AI、BDI 和 CI 之间的切换依赖于系统尺寸、粒子数和边界条件，并发现了隐藏在连续谱中的精确可解双粒子束缚态（doublon state）以及两个非相互作用任意子的零空间精确解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期冷原子实验已实现一维任意子（one-dimensional anyons）并能在玻色子与费米子之间调节一维统计量，但该模型在有限长度下的对称性、可积性及相关简并性尚未被系统理解。

Method: 对有限长度的任意子-哈伯德模型进行对称性分析、可积性判定以及模型极限（尤其是相互作用玻色子和赝费米子）的全面分析，并通过解析手段揭示隐藏态和零空间解。

Result: 结果表明，对称性类在 AI、BDI 和 CI 之间切换，受系统尺寸、粒子数和边界条件调控；周期性边界条件下两个任意子可积，而开边界条件下不可积；发现了一个隐藏在散射态连续谱中的精确可解 doublon 态，以及两个非相互作用任意子零空间的精确解。

Conclusion: 所揭示的对称性塑造了一维任意子的基本性质，且预测的态可在当前最先进的实验中得到观测。

Abstract: Recent cold atom experiments have realized one-dimensional anyons and enabled the tuning of 1D~statistics between bosons and fermions. Here, we analyze the symmetries, integrability, and resulting degeneracies of the underlying anyon-Hubbard model of finite length. Our results reveal a switching between symmetry classes AI, BDI, and CI in dependence on system size, particle number, and boundary conditions, and show that two anyons with periodic boundaries are integrable, while two anyons with open boundary conditions are not. We include a comprehensive analysis of all model limits, especially of interacting bosons and pseudofermions and resolve spectral signatures. We additionally reveal an exactly solvable doublon state that hides in the continuum of scattering states and the exact solution of the nullspace of two noninteracting anyons. The uncovered symmetries shape the fundamental properties of the one-dimensional anyons at hand, and the predicted states are accessible in state-of-the-art experiments.

</details>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [149] [Phast: Simultaneous reconstruction of photoelectron count and time profiles from PMT waveforms via machine learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29391)
*Yiming Xu,Youwen Fan,Siyu Chen,Hongyue Duyang,Teng Li,Yaoguang Wang*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于机器学习的PMT波形重建方法\phast{}，利用共享的wave-transformer编码器结合计数分支与时间分支，同时重构光电子（PE）计数与时间分布。在多个toy Monte Carlo数据集上，该方法在不同波形条件下均表现出稳定且准确的性能，验证了卷积特征提取与基于查询的transformer解码器结合的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PMT波形重建（PMT waveform reconstruction）是粒子与核物理实验中的基础任务，需要从波形中精确提取光电子（photoelectron, PE）的多重度与时间信息。然而，真实探测器环境中的堆积（pileup）、电荷涨落（charge fluctuations）、噪声（noise）等电子学效应使得精确恢复物理可观测量极具挑战性。

Method: 方法名为\phast{}，由一个共享的wave-transformer编码器（wave-transformer encoder）和两个专用分支组成：计数分支（counting branch）用于预测总PE数，时间分支（time branch）采用计数条件查询解码器（count-conditioned query decoder）并引入动态查询激活（dynamic query activation）机制。

Result: 在包含均匀（uniform）和混合快-慢双时间分量（mixed fast-slow double-temporal-components）配置的多个toy Monte Carlo PMT波形数据集上，\phast{}在PE计数和时间重建方面均表现出高度一致性（high consistency），实现了稳定且准确的性能。

Conclusion: 卷积特征提取（convolutional feature extraction）与基于查询的transformer解码器（query-based transformer decoder）相结合的架构，为复杂PMT波形重建任务提供了一种有效方案。

Abstract: Photomultiplier tubes (PMTs) are widely used in particle and nuclear physics experiments. The reconstruction of PMT waveforms is a fundamental task in these experiments, where accurate extraction of photoelectron (PE) multiplicities and time from the waveform is required for downstream event reconstruction and analysis. In realistic detector environments, PMT waveform reconstruction is complicated by electronic effects such as pileup, charge fluctuations, noise etc., which make precise recovery of physical observables challenging. To address these challenges, we present \phast{}, a machine-learning-based method that reconstructs PE count and time profile simultaneously. The model consists of a shared wave-transformer encoder followed by two dedicated branches: a counting branch for the total PE number prediction, and a time branch employing a count-conditioned query decoder with dynamic query activation. To study the reconstruction performance under controlled conditions, we construct several toy Monte Carlo PMT waveform datasets, including both uniform and mixed fast-slow double-temporal-components configurations. The proposed method demonstrates stable and accurate reconstruction performance across various waveform conditions, achieving high consistency in both PE counting and time reconstruction. These results indicate that architectures combining convolutional feature extraction with query-based transformer decoders provide an effective approach for complex PMT waveform reconstruction tasks.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文利用 Belle 探测器采集的 102×10⁶ Υ(1S) 和 158×10⁶ Υ(2S) 衰变事件，搜索 Ξ⁰p、Ω⁻p 和 Ω⁻n 双重子态（dibaryon states），未发现显著信号，并首次在 90% 置信水平上给出了这些衰变分支比的上限（量级为 10⁻⁷–10⁻⁶）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多奇异重子-重子相互作用（multistrange baryon-baryon interactions）与中子星物质（neutron-star matter）的性质密切相关，但实验约束严重不足；同时，已有实验和理论研究暗示 ΞN 和 ΩN 相互作用可能存在吸引力，这为弱束缚双重子态的存在提供了可能性。

Method: 使用 Belle 探测器在 KEKB 非对称能量正负电子对撞机（asymmetric-energy e⁺e⁻ collider）上收集的 Υ(1S)（102×10⁶ 事例）和 Υ(2S)（158×10⁶ 事例）衰变样本，在相应重子对阈值附近的质量区间内搜索 Ξ⁰p、Ω⁻p 和 Ω⁻n 双重子态信号。

Result: 在所有搜索通道中均未观测到显著信号。首次在 90% 置信水平（confidence level）上设定了 Υ(1S) 和 Υ(2S) 衰变至 Ξ⁰p、Ω⁻p 和 Ω⁻n 双重子态的分支比（branching fraction）上限，其量级因通道及所假设的与相应重子对阈值的质量差（mass difference）不同而处于 10⁻⁷ 至 10⁻⁶ 之间。

Conclusion: 在 Belle 数据中未发现 Ξ⁰p、Ω⁻p 和 Ω⁻n 双重子态的明确证据；所设定的分支比上限为未来对多奇异重子-重子相互作用及其在核天体物理中作用的理论与实验研究提供了新的约束。

Abstract: We search for $Ξ^0p$, $Ω^-p$, and $Ω^-n$ dibaryon states in $Υ(1S)$ and $Υ(2S)$ decays, probing mass regions near the corresponding baryon-pair thresholds. Multistrange baryon-baryon interactions are relevant to neutron-star matter but remain largely unconstrained. Experimental and theoretical studies supporting attractive $ΞN$ and $ΩN$ interactions, where $N$ denotes a nucleon, motivate searches for weakly bound states. We use samples of $102$ million $Υ(1S)$ and $158$ million $Υ(2S)$ decays collected with the Belle detector at the KEKB asymmetric-energy $e^+e^-$ collider. No significant signals are observed, and the first $90$% confidence-level upper limits are set on the branching fractions of $Υ(1S)$ and $Υ(2S)$ decays to $Ξ^0p$, $Ω^-p$, and $Ω^-n$ dibaryon states, at the level of $O(10^{-7})$-$O(10^{-6})$, depending on the channel and the assumed mass difference from the corresponding baryon-pair threshold.

### [151] [Invariantised Euler-Lagrange equations and conserved quantities for nonconservative Herglotz variational problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29065)
*Tânia M. N. Gonçalves,Delfim F. M. Torres,Gastão S. F. Frederico*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文针对 n 阶一维 Herglotz 变分问题，推导了广义 Euler-Lagrange 方程及其相关守恒量的结构，并利用移动标架（moving frames）与不变变分法（invariant calculus of variations）加以证明。研究表明，这些结构不仅能提供几何洞见，还可为极值曲线的确定提供更高效的路径，并以受限洛伦兹群 $SO^+(1,2)$ 下的 Herglotz 问题为例加以说明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前人尚未系统地基于移动标架与不变变分法来推导高阶一维 Herglotz 变分问题的广义 Euler-Lagrange 方程及其守恒量结构。

Method: 采用移动标架（moving frames）与不变变分法（invariant calculus of variations）作为理论框架，对 n 阶一维 Herglotz 变分问题中的广义 Euler-Lagrange 方程和相关守恒量进行结构推导。

Result: 成功导出 n 阶一维 Herglotz 变分问题的广义 Euler-Lagrange 方程及其关联守恒量的结构，并以受限洛伦兹群 $SO^+(1,2)$ 不变 Herglotz 问题为例验证了该结构对极值曲线确定的效率提升。

Conclusion: 所导出的结构不仅提供了几何层面的新理解，也为极值曲线的求解开辟了一条更高效的路径。

Abstract: In this paper the structures of the generalised Euler-Lagrange equations and their associated conserved quantities are derived for one-dimensional Herglotz variational problems of order $n$. Their derivations use the framework of moving frames and invariant calculus of variations. The knowledge of these structures not only offers a geometric insight, it may provide a more efficient path for the determination of extremals. This is exemplified with a Herglotz problem invariant under the restricted Lorentz group $SO^+(1,2)$.

</details>

# cond-mat.supr-con [[Back]](#toc)

### [152] [Graph-based emulation of $d$-dimensional curved spaces with superconducting arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28942)
*Mehmet Dede,Guilherme Delfino,André L. G. Mudry,Junseok Oh,Andrew P. Higginbotham,Christopher Mudry,Claudio Chamon*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出一种利用超导导线阵列构建任意维度弯曲空间模拟框架，通过将空间离散化为图、用约瑟夫森结耦合超导导线，实现标量场理论。以双曲（反德西特）空间为例，验证了全息对偶在无序存在下的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子模拟平台难以在实验可控条件下实现任意维度的弯曲空间和复杂拓扑结构，尤其是高维双曲空间（hyperbolic space）的模拟，从而限制了全息对偶（holographic duality）等理论的实验检验。

Method: 采用上下两层堆叠的超导导线阵列（每层内导线平行，层间垂直），将空间离散化为图（graph）：每个顶点（vertex）对应一根具有刚性相位（rigid phase）的超导导线，图边（edge）通过约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）耦合相邻导线。超导相位实现所模拟几何上的标量场理论（scalar field theory）。

Result: 建立了实验可实现的架构条件，并构建了可观测电路量与模拟场论量之间的字典（dictionary）。实现了恒定负曲率的双曲空间（Anti-de Sitter空间），并用于探索任意维度的全息对偶。分析表明，约瑟夫森耦合中的无序（disorder）会转化为体-边界对应（bulk-boundary correspondence）中的度规变化，但全息对偶在强无序下依然保持鲁棒。

Conclusion: 该框架不仅为全息对偶提供了实验可访问的平台，还拓展至非平凡图上的物理探索以及动力学时空（dynamical spacetimes）的玩具模型，展示了广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: We introduce a framework for emulating graphs and, through them, curved spaces of arbitrary dimension, using arrays of superconducting wires. The array consists of two stacked layers of wires, horizontal and vertical, such that wires are parallel within each layer and perpendicular between layers. By discretizing a space into a graph, assigning a superconducting wire with a rigid phase to each vertex, and coupling pairs of wires through Josephson junctions along the graph edges, arbitrary geometries and topologies can be engineered in a controlled setting. The superconducting phases then realize scalar field theories on the emergent geometry. We establish experimentally realistic conditions for implementing these architectures and develop a dictionary relating measurable circuit observables to quantities in the emulated field theory. As an application, we develop the implementation of hyperbolic (Anti-de Sitter) spaces of constant negative curvature and use them as an experimentally accessible platform to explore holographic duality in arbitrary dimensions. We investigate the effects of disorder in the Josephson couplings, which translate into metric variations in the bulk-boundary correspondence, and analyze their impact on boundary scaling exponents both analytically and numerically, finding that holographic duality remains robust even in the presence of strong disorder. Beyond holography, the framework opens a broad range of architectural possibilities, including the exploration of physics on highly nontrivial graphs and toy models of dynamical spacetimes.

</details>


### [153] [Effective Theory of Fermion Quartet Condensation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29338)
*Qiao-Ru Xu,Congjun Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文基于费米子四重态（fermion quartet）凝聚发展了一套超导/超流理论，构建了类似于BCS（Bardeen–Cooper–Schrieffer）变分波函数，定义了能隙参数并导出了能隙方程，计算了超流份数，发现其与常规超导体相同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在稀薄自旋-1/2费米子体系中，现有超导理论主要基于库珀对（Cooper pair）凝聚；本文旨在建立一种基于费米子四重态（fermion quartet）凝聚的超导/超流理论，以描述四体关联效应占主导的体系。

Method: 采用Bardeen–Cooper–Schrieffer（BCS）变分法的精神，构建一个变分波函数（variational wavefunction）；在“稀薄四重态近似（dilute quartet approximation）”下，该波函数成为有效四次哈密顿量（effective quartic Hamiltonian）的基态。针对有利于四重态凝聚的两体相互作用，定义能隙参数（gap parameter）并导出能隙方程（gap equation）。对于激发态，基于一个十六维“占据空间（occupation space）”给出直观的物理图像，并获得相应的本征能量。

Result: 通过该理论计算了超流份数（superfluid fraction），发现其与常规超导体中的超流份数相同，尽管四重态问题存在相互作用。

Conclusion: 本文表明，基于费米子四重态凝聚（fermion quartet condensation）的超导/超流理论在稀薄自旋-1/2费米子体系的零温极限下是自洽的；超流份数的计算结果揭示出四重态体系与常规BCS超导体在宏观超流响应上具有一致性。

Abstract: We develop a theory of superconductivity (or superfluidity) based on condensed fermion quartets focusing on the dilute spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ systems at zero temperature. In the spirit of the Bardeen--Cooper--Schrieffer ansatz, a variational wavefunction is constructed such that, within the so-called ``dilute quartet approximation", it is the ground state of an effective quartic Hamiltonian. For a given two-body interaction in favor of quartetting, the gap parameter is suitably defined and the gap equation is also derived. As to the excited states, an intuitive physical picture based on a sixteen-dimensional ``occupation space" is depicted and the associated eigen-energies are obtained. This theory is applied to compute the superfluid fraction, which is found to be the same as in conventional superconductors, despite the interacting nature of the quartet problem.

</details>


### [154] [Hole-doped superconductivity above 100 K in infinite-layer cuprate thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29352)
*Biemeng Jin,Saurav Prakash,Zhaoyang Luo,Shengwei Zeng,Jing-Yang Chung,Xing Gao,Zhi Shiuh Lim,Jiangbo Luo,King Yip,Wei Zhang,Nurul Fitriyah,Shuhan Lu,Taiyu An,Ping Yang,Qian He,Silvija Gradečak,Huajun Liu,A. Ariando*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文报告了在空穴掺杂的无限层铜氧化物（infinite-layer cuprate）薄膜中首次实现超导电性。通过在Sr1-xRbxCuO2单晶薄膜中测量电阻率和磁场响应，观察到起始温度高达100 K的超导转变。空穴掺杂通过铷替代与顶氧（apical oxygen）掺入的协同效应实现。该发现为研究铜氧化物超导体中的奇异金属（strange metal）和电子-空穴对称性（electron-hole symmetry）等关键难题提供了独特平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无限层铜氧化物自约40年前提出以来，通过化学替代实现空穴掺杂超导电性一直未能成功，成为该领域的一个基本未解问题。本文旨在解决这一长期存在的开放性问题。

Method: 通过铷（rubidium）替代和顶氧（apical oxygen）掺入的协同效应实现空穴掺杂，在Sr1-xRbxCuO2单晶薄膜中进行电阻率和磁场响应测量，并结合结构分析与输运测量加以验证。

Result: 在空穴掺杂的无限层铜氧化物薄膜中观测到超导电性，超导转变起始温度高达100 K。

Conclusion: 空穴掺杂的无限层铜氧化物作为铜氧化物家族的最简母体结构，为重新审视铜氧化物超导体中的奇异金属行为、电子-空穴对称性以及铜氧化物-镍酸盐对称性（cuprate-nickelate symmetry）等关键问题提供了独特的研究平台。

Abstract: Since the discovery of superconductivity in (La,Ba)2CuO2 (Ref.~\cite{bednorz1986possible}), a broad family of structurally distinct cuprate superconductors has been proposed or engineered to elucidate the physics of high-temperature superconductivity~\cite{chu2015hole,plakida2010high}. Among them, the infinite-layer cuprate has the simplest structure, consisting only of the essential ingredients for superconductivity: CuO$_2$ square planes separated by spacer ions~\cite{siegrist1988parent}. Despite being proposed nearly 40 years ago, the hole-doped superconductivity via chemical substitution in this compound has not yet been achieved, a fundamental open question in the field. Here, we report the observation of superconductivity in the hole-doped infinite-layer cuprate thin film. Measurements of resistivity and magnetic-field response in Sr1-xRbxCuO2 single-crystal thin films show superconducting transitions with a high onset temperature of 100 K. Hole doping is achieved via the synergistic effect of rubidium substitution and apical oxygen incorporation, as evidenced by structural analysis and transport measurements. As the parent structure of the cuprate family~\cite{chu2015hole}, hole-doped infinite-layer cuprate provides a unique platform for revisiting key puzzles in cuprate superconductors~\cite{keimer2015quantum,tsuei2000pairing,armitage2010progress,dagotto1994correlated}, including strange metal~\cite{proust2019remarkable,taillefer2010scattering} and electron-hole symmetry~\cite{tohyama2004asymmetry,segawa2010zero,lee2014asymmetry}, while bridging to cuprate-nickelate symmetry~\cite{li2019superconductivity,zeng2022superconductivity,chow2025bulk,lechermann2020late}.

</details>


### [155] [Thickness-driven crossover from conventional to chiral nonreciprocal superconductivity in kagome metal CsV3Sb5](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29665)
*Wei Zhang,Jiangbo Luo,Nikolai Peshcherenko,Zheyu Wang,Chun Wai Tsang,Kwing To Lai,King Yau Yip,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Junxiong Hu,Yang Zhang,Swee K. Goh,A. Ariando*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过厚度依赖的输运测量，在Kagome金属CsV3Sb5的薄片中观测到零场超导二极管效应和非互易二次谐波磁输运信号，揭示从三维向二维超导的维度交叉，表明厚度诱导的手性超导相同时打破了反演对称性和时间反演对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kagome金属CsV3Sb5在体材料中通常表现为常规s波配对，但超薄薄片却表现出非互易输运和零场超导二极管效应，这表明存在对称性破缺。然而，这种厚度依赖的配对对称性转变及其物理机制尚不明确，亟需澄清。

Method: 采用厚度依赖的输运测量方法，包括非互易二次谐波磁输运信号测量、零场超导二极管效应观测，以及上临界场（upper critical field）测量以判定超导维度。

Result: 观测到非互易二次谐波磁输运信号和零场超导二极管效应的出现，伴随面外相干长度（out-of-plane coherence length）随厚度减小而显著降低；上临界场测量揭示了从三维超导到二维超导的维度交叉（dimensional crossover）。

Conclusion: 这些发现表明在二维极限下存在厚度诱导的手性超导相（chiral superconducting phase），同时打破了反演对称性和时间反演对称性。该工作澄清了CsV3Sb5配对对称性的长期争议，并建立薄片Kagome超导体作为工程化非互易量子器件和探索新兴拓扑相的多功能平台。

Abstract: Superconductivity and its potential applications are governed by the symmetry of the superconducting order parameter. In the kagome metal CsV3Sb5, most bulk studies indicate conventional s-wave pairing. However, ultrathin flakes exhibit nonreciprocal transport, in particular a zero-field superconducting diode effect, which requires broken inversion and time-reversal symmetries. Here, using thickness dependent transport measurements, we observe the emergence of non-reciprocal second-harmonic magnetotransport signals and a zero-field superconducting diode effect, accompanied by a pronounced reduction of the out-of-plane coherence length with decreasing thickness. Upper critical field measurements further reveal a dimensional crossover from three-dimensional superconductivity in bulk to two-dimensional superconductivity in thin flakes. These findings indicate a thickness-induced chiral superconducting phase that breaks both inversion and time-reversal symmetries in the two-dimensional limit. Our work not only clarifies long-standing controversies regarding the pairing symmetry in CsV3Sb5, but also establishes thin-flake kagome superconductors as a versatile platform for engineering nonreciprocal quantum devices and exploring emergent topological phases.
