### [156] [Stability Analysis of Superconductivity in $\textit{P6/mmm}$-LaSc$_2$H$_{24}$ and its Experimental Reproducibility from La-Sc Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29985)
*Dmitrii V. Semenok,Ivan A. Troyan,Di Zhou,Emil A. Yuzbashyan,Boris L. Altshuler,Viktor V. Struzhkin*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文分析镧-钪氢化物 LaSc₂H₂₄ 在室温超导方面的可行性。电子-声子耦合计算中，双δ函数的σ展宽方法导致超导临界温度T_c(σ)对任意σ强烈依赖，而四面体法无此缺陷，且在300 GPa下预测T_c > 300 K。实验合成在250-280 GPa下未成功，产物中未观测到超导电性，同时沉积La和Sc金属的前驱体制备方法可能是成功合成的关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证镧-钪氢化物 LaSc₂H₂₄ 在高压下实现室温超导（room-temperature superconductivity）的可行性，解决其电子-声子耦合计算中方法依赖性问题，并检验其合成路径的有效性。

Method: 采用两种电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）计算方法——双δ函数的σ展宽（σ-broadening）和四面体法（tetrahedral method）——对比计算超导临界温度T_c；通过分析金属态稳定性参数ξ评估化合物稳定性；在250-280 GPa条件下从(La,Sc₂)合金前驱体尝试高压合成。

Result: σ展宽法使T_c(σ)对展宽参数σ产生强烈依赖，而四面体法消除此缺陷，预测在300 GPa下T_c > 300 K。LaSc₂H₂₄在250-300 GPa下处于稳定性边缘（ξ = 0.54），与fcc LaH₁₀在140-150 GPa时类似。实验合成产物中未检测到超导电性痕迹。

Conclusion: 四面体法比σ展宽法更适合LaSc₂H₂₄的电子-声子耦合计算，理论支持其室温超导潜力；但实验合成因前驱体制备方法不当而失败，同时沉积La和Sc金属可能为实现成功合成的关键路径。

Abstract: In this work, we analyze the feasibility of room-temperature superconductivity in the lanthanum-scandium hydride $\textit{P6/mmm}$-LaSc$_2$H$_{24}$. We demonstrate that the electron-phonon coupling calculations performed using the $σ$-broadening of the double $δ$-function at the Fermi surface lead to a very strong dependence of $\textit{T$_c$}(σ)$ on the arbitrary $σ$, whereas the tetrahedral method for the electron-phonon interaction is free from this drawback and leads to $\textit{T$_c$}$ > 300 K at 300 GPa in agreement with previous predictions. By analyzing the stability of the metallic state of LaSc$_2$H$_{24}$ at 250-300 GPa, we show that this compound is at the edge of the stability region ($ξ$ = 0.54), similar to $\textit{fcc}$ LaH$_{10}$ at 140-150 GPa. Experimental attempts to synthesize LaSc$_2$H$_{24}$ at 250-280 GPa starting from the (La,Sc$_2$) alloy are unsuccessful and indicate the absence of even traces of superconductivity at 245-300 K in all the resulting La-Sc-H hydrides. The method for preparing the precursor by simultaneous deposition of La and Sc metals may be a key factor for the successful synthesis of LaSc$_2$H$_{24}$.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于第一性原理的密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算，对通过四价元素替代实现电子掺杂的La₃Ni₂O₇薄膜进行系统研究；并利用约束随机相位近似（constrained random phase approximation, cRPA）评估相互作用参数。

Result: 铈（Ce）掺杂难以有效将电子载流子引入低能带；相比之下，锆（Zr）、铪（Hf）和钍（Th）可作为有效的电子掺杂剂，显著增大d_z²轨道之间的层间跃迁（interlayer hopping）t⊥，从而可能增强超交换耦合（superexchange coupling）J⊥并提升超导临界温度Tc。

Conclusion: 研究识别出可实现电子掺杂La₃Ni₂O₇的候选掺杂元素，为澄清该体系中关于配对机制（pairing mechanism）的持续争论提供了一条途径。

Abstract: The bilayer Ruddlesden-Popper nickelate $\mathrm{La_3Ni_2O_7}$ has emerged as a promising platform for exploring and understanding high-temperature superconductivities. While most prior doping studies
  have focused on hole doping via strontium (Sr) substitution or by tuning oxygen content, electron doping remains largely unexplored. In this work,we systematically investigate electron doping in $\mathrm{La_3Ni_2O_7}$ thin films through
  tetravalent element substitution, employing first-principles density functional theory calculations.
  Our results reveal that, unlike in cuprates, $\mathrm{cerium}$ (Ce) doping is difficult to effectively introduce electron carriers into the low-energy bands. In contrast, zirconium (Zr), hafnium (Hf), and thorium (Th) can act as efficient electron dopants. These element substitutions can significantly increase the interlayer hopping $t_{\perp}$ between $d_{z^2}$ orbitals, which may lead to enhanced superexchange coupling $J_{\perp}$ , and thereby potentially elevated superconducting $T_c$. We evaluate the interaction parameters using constrained random phase approximation. Our results identify candidate dopants for achieving electron-doped $\mathrm{La_3Ni_2O_7}$, offering a route to clarify the ongoing debate on pairing mechanisms in this system.

### [158] [Comparing Spatially Periodic Feedback and Space-Time Modulation for Unidirectional Wave Propagation in a 1D Mass-Spring-Damper System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29086)
*João H. S. Brandão,Danilo Braghini,José R. F. Arruda*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在周期性一维质量-弹簧-阻尼集总系统中实现定向波传播的两种策略：时空调制（space-time modulation）与空间周期反馈（spatially periodic feedback）。前者通过平面波展开（Plane Wave Expansion, PWE）与Bloch-Floquet理论分析，后者通过非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect, NHSE）实现定向放大或衰减，并分别评估了系统的稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单向波传播已成为非互易力学与声学超材料（non-reciprocal mechanical and acoustic metamaterials）动力学中的关键概念。本文旨在探索并对比两种本质上不同的策略，以在弹性波导（elastic waveguide）中实现定向波传播。

Method: 第一种方法采用时空调制，对刚度进行空间与时间上的周期性调制，基于Bloch-Floquet理论通过平面波展开获取色散关系（dispersion relation）。第二种方法通过空间周期反馈作用引入非互易性，基于经典力学原理建立有限单元集总系统的状态空间模型（state-space model）。

Result: 时空调制产生非对称色散图与定向带隙（directional band gaps），因时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）破缺导致弹性波优先沿单一方向传播。周期反馈通过非厄米趋肤效应产生定向放大或衰减，由拓扑不变量——绕数（winding number）表征的边界局域模态所识别。

Conclusion: 时空周期系统通过Lyapunov-Floquet理论评估稳定性，周期反馈情形则通过状态矩阵的特征值分析稳定性。这些结果为弹性波导中的定向波传播提供了设计指导准则。

Abstract: Unidirectional wave propagation has emerged as a key concept in the dynamics of non-reciprocal mechanical and acoustic metamaterials. This work investigates two fundamentally distinct strategies for achieving directional wave propagation in a periodic one-dimensional mass-spring-damper lumped system: space-time modulation and spatially periodic feedback. In the first approach, the stiffness is modulated periodically in both space and time. The resulting space-time periodic system is analyzed using a Plane Wave Expansion (PWE) formulation based on the Bloch-Floquet theory to obtain the dispersion relation. The traveling modulation produces asymmetric dispersion diagrams and directional band gaps, within which elastic waves propagate preferentially in a single direction due to broken time-reversal symmetry. In the second approach, non-reciprocity is introduced through a spatially periodic feedback action. The force can depend on the displacement and/or its derivatives, such as velocity or acceleration, and is applied to the masses along the system. The lumped system with a finite number of unit cells is modeled using classical mechanics principles, yielding a state-space model of the system. The active mechanism can generate directional amplification or attenuation via the non-Hermitian skin effect (NHSE), characterized by boundary-localized modes identified by a topological invariant, the winding number. The stability of the space-time periodic system is assessed through the Lyapunov-Floquet theory. In the periodic feedback case, stability is investigated using the eigenvalues of the state matrix. These results provide design guidelines for directional wave propagation in elastic waveguides.

</details>

### [159] [Multifidelity Proper Orthogonal Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29213)
*Nicole Aretz,Karen Willcox*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出一种多保真度（multifidelity）公式，通过利用低保真度模型的数据来降低高保真度模型本征正交分解（proper orthogonal decomposition, POD）的计算成本，在相同精度下将离线快照生成的计算成本降低了一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维参数空间中对高保真度模型进行采样以生成充足的训练快照集计算成本过高；快照不足则会导致POD基过拟合且泛化能力差。

Method: 提出多保真度POD（MFPOD）公式：将计算预算重新分配给成本更低、可广泛采样的低保真度模型；通过控制变量（control-variate）公式对高、低保真度快照数据进行加权，以保证对高保真度最小二乘投影误差的期望的无偏估计；MFPOD子空间通过最小化该投影误差的估计值来选定。

Result: 在预算趋于无穷时，MFPOD依概率收敛到与单保真度POD相同的子空间；在预算受限时，MFPOD代价函数的方差低于POD，使子空间对训练数据变化更鲁棒、不易过拟合；在松岛冰川流速数值算例中，MFPOD在相同精度下将离线快照生成计算成本降低了一个数量级。

Conclusion: MFPOD通过多保真度策略在保证无偏估计和收敛性的前提下，显著降低了POD训练数据的离线计算负担，提高了有限预算下的子空间鲁棒性。

Abstract: This paper introduces a multifidelity formulation that reduces the computational cost of the proper orthogonal decomposition (POD) of a high-fidelity model by leveraging data from cheaper, lower-fidelity models. POD is a prevalent technique for extracting a low-dimensional basis from training data to achieve subsequent dimension reduction or reduced-order modeling. In scientific and engineering applications, the training data are typically numerical snapshot solutions of a high-fidelity model, and computation of a sufficiently rich snapshot set can be prohibitively expensive, especially when sampling over a high-dimensional parameter space. Insufficient snapshot training data risks overfitting and poor generalizability of the POD basis to outside the training regime. Our multifidelity POD (MFPOD) formulation reallocates computational budget to cheaper, low-fidelity models that can be sampled more extensively. MFPOD then weights high- and low-fidelity snapshot data via a control-variate formulation to guarantee an unbiased estimate of the expected high-fidelity least-squares projection error. The MFPOD subspace is chosen to minimize the estimate of this projection error, and converges in probability to the same subspace as single-fidelity POD in the limit of an arbitrarily large budget. For restrictive computational budgets, the MFPOD cost function has (under some assumptions) lower variance than the POD cost function, which makes the MFPOD subspace more robust against variations in the training data and thus less prone to overfitting. For a numerical example modeling the velocity of the Pine Island glacier, MFPOD achieves the same accuracy as single-fidelity POD with an order of magnitude reduction in the offline computational cost of snapshot generation.

</details>

### [160] [An End-to-End PyTorch Interface for Differentiable PDE Solvers: A RANS Model-Correction Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28858)
*Luca Saverio,Michele Alessandro Bucci,Gianmarco Farro,Cédric Content,Denis Sipp*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种端到端策略，在完全可微分的机器学习框架内求解受偏微分方程（PDE）约束的反问题，将可微分PDE求解器与参数化可微分校正项相结合，并在压缩流的RANS方程上验证了该方法在湍流建模等数据驱动问题中的灵活性与适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上求解受偏微分方程（PDE）约束的反问题（如数据同化、封闭建模）缺乏统一且用户友好的方法论，且将PDE求解器集成到可微分机器学习工作流中存在困难。

Method: 将基线的可微分PDE求解器（预测状态w，满足非线性系统R(w)=0）与一个通用的加性参数化可微分校正项f_φ(w)（含可训练参数φ）相结合；通过将PDE重新表述为隐式层（implicit layer），在PyTorch自动微分图中实现端到端优化。

Result: 在2D NASA壁挂鼓包（Wall-Mounted Hump）测试案例中，优化了生产项参数以匹配时间平均LES数据；在VKI LS-59涡轮叶片案例中，通过优化可训练空间场重构了Spalart-Allmaras涡黏性场（eddy viscosity field）。

Conclusion: 该框架具有高度灵活性，其适用性可超越湍流建模，扩展到更广泛的物理信息PDE约束问题（physics-informed PDE-constrained problems）与数据驱动组件。

Abstract: This work presents an end-to-end strategy for solving inverse problems constrained by Partial Differential Equations within a fully differentiable Machine Learning framework. The proposed formulation provides a unified and user-friendly methodology applicable to a wide range of problems, from data assimilation to closure modeling. Our approach combines a baseline differentiable PDE solver, which predicts the state w from the nonlinear system $R(w) = 0$, with a generic additive, parametrized, and differentiable correction $f_φ(w)$, with trainable parameters $φ$. We show how to optimize phi within a fully differentiable Python workflow by reformulating the PDE as an implicit layer, enabling its integration into arbitrary objective functions, while leveraging PyTorch's automatic differentiation graph. The method is demonstrated on the Reynolds-Averaged Navier-Stokes equations for compressible flows, where the closure term, or a portion of it, is modeled using trainable parameters or a Neural Network. The first application considers the 2D NASA Wall-Mounted Hump test case, where a production-term parameter is optimized against time-averaged LES data. A second application is carried out on the VKI LS-59 turbine blade, where the Spalart-Allmaras eddy viscosity field is reconstructed through the optimization of a trainable spatial field. A dataset is generated starting from the VKI LS-59 turbine blade geometry using the differentiable BROADCAST solver with the Spalart-Allmaras turbulence model. The results highlight the flexibility of the framework, showing its applicability beyond turbulence modeling to a broader class of physics-informed PDE-constrained problems with data-driven components.

</details>

### [161] [That Damned Equation. Rigour, Credit Attribution, and the Wheeler-DeWitt Equation 1962-1967](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29696)
*Alexander S. Blum,Dean Rickles,Karim Thébault*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 本文论证理论物理学中的“严格性”是内生的规范，其核心目标并非追求绝对真理，而是消除具体计算和清晰概念化的障碍。通过对1962-67年间Wheeler-DeWitt方程的案例研究，提出关键贡献在于通过内积表达式实现方程的严格化（rigorisation），而非方程本身的提出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清物理学实践中“严格性”（rigour）的内在含义，挑战将数学严格性视为统一外部标准的传统观点，揭示理论物理学在严格性问题上独特的、情境化的规范。

Method: 基于对1962-1967年期间Wheeler-DeWitt方程（Wheeler-DeWitt equation）发展史和学术贡献归属的详细历史案例研究，结合档案材料与已发表文献进行论证。

Result: 发现在该案例中，真正的关键步骤并非方程形式本身的首次提出，而是通过内积（inner product）表达式的引入实现了对方程的严格化处理，后者才是Wheeler和DeWitt工作中的决定性贡献。

Conclusion: 理论物理学的严格性规范是内生的、隐含的、局域的且随时间变化；其核心功能是使最初半形式化的构造转变为形式上定义良好的模型，以便通过可观测量（quantities of interest）的计算与世界建立具体联系。追求严格性本身并非目的。

Abstract: The notion of rigour relevant to the practice of physics is an endogenous one. Theoretical physics has its own internal norms about mathematical practice and notions of legitimate derivations or formal objects. These norms are often implicit, local, and change in substantial ways over time. Moreover, norms of rigour in theoretical physics, at least in the mid-twentieth century, are primarily focused on the goal of removing barriers for concrete calculation and clear conceptualisation. Rather than pursuit of rigour for its own sake, or to achieve some `higher' standard of truth, theoretical physicists seek to `rigorise' initial, semi-formal constructions in order to render formally well-defined models with which they can make concrete contact with the world, through calculations of quantities of interest. In what follows we will support this thesis based upon a detailed historical case study of the development of and attribution of credit for the Wheeler-DeWitt equation in the period 1962-67. Drawing upon archival material and the published record we develop and defend the explanatory hypothesis that it was the rigorisation of the equation via the expression for the inner product that was the crucial step in the work of Wheeler and DeWitt rather than the statement of the equation itself.

</details>
